4.8.2	yajño 'si sarvataḥ śritaḥ sarvato māṃ bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyac chrayatāṃ śataṃ me santv āśiṣaḥ sahasraṃ me santu sūnṛtā irāvatīḥ paśumatīḥ prajāpatir asi sarvataḥ śritaḥ sarvato māṃ bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyac chrayatāṃ śataṃ me santv āśiṣaḥ sahasraṃ me santu sūnṛtā irāvatīḥ paśumatīr ity āgneyaṃ puroḍāśam āsannam abhimṛśati sarvāṇi vā havīṃṣi
4.8.3	idam indriyam amṛtaṃ vīryam anenendrāya paśavo cikitsan / tena devā avatopa mām iheṣam ūrjaṃ yaśaḥ saha ojaḥ saneyaṃ śṛtaṃ mayi śrayatām iti prātardoham / yat pṛthivīm acarat tat praviṣṭaṃ yenāsiñcad balam indre prajāpatiḥ / idaṃ tac chukraṃ madhu vājinīvad yenopariṣṭād adhinon mahendraṃ dadhi māṃ dhinotv iti dadhi
4.8.4	ayaṃ yajñaḥ samasadad dhaviṣmān ṛcā sāmnā yajuṣā devatābhiḥ / tena lokān sūryavato jayemendrasya sakhyam amṛtatvam aśyām iti sarvāṇi havīṃṣi
4.8.5	yo naḥ kanīya iha kāmayātā asmin yajñe yajamānāya mahyam / apa tam indrāgnī bhuvanān nudetām ahaṃ prajāṃ vīravatīṃ videyety aindrāgnam
4.8.6	mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv ity anuvākena sarvāṇi havīṃṣy āsannāny abhimṛśed aṣṭābhir vā
4.8.7	caturhotrā paurṇamāsyāṃ havīṃṣy āsannāny abhimṛśet prajākāmaḥ pañcahotrāmāvāsyāyāṃ svargakāmo nityavad eke samāmananti
4.9.1	daśahotāraṃ vadet purastāt sāmidhenīnām
4.9.2	aṅgiraso māsya yajñasya prātaranuvākair avantv iti sāmidhenīnāṃ pratipadi japati
4.9.3	anūcyamānāsu daśahotāraṃ vyākhyāyocchuṣmo agna iti samidhyamānam / samiddho agnir āhutaḥ svāhākṛtaḥ pipartu naḥ / svagā devebhya idaṃ nama iti samiddham
4.9.4	mano 'si prājāpatyam iti srauvam āghāryamāṇam
4.9.5	srucyam anvārabhya vāg asy aindrīty anumantrayate
4.9.6	devāḥ pitaraḥ pitaro devā yo 'ham asmi sa san yaje yasyāsmi na tam antaremi svaṃ ma iṣṭaṃ svaṃ dattaṃ svaṃ pūrtaṃ svaṃ śrāntaṃ svaṃ hutam / tasya me 'gnir upadraṣṭā vāyur upaśrotādityo 'nukhyātā dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā prajāpatir bandhur ya evāsmi sa sanyaja iti hotṛpravare 'dhvaryupravare ca pravriyamāṇe
4.9.7	caturhotāraṃ vyākhyāya vasantam ṛtūnāṃ prīṇāmīty etaiḥ pratimantraṃ prayājān hutaṃhutam
4.9.8	eko mamaikā tasya yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo dvau mama dve tasya trayo mama tisras tasya catvāro mama catasras tasya pañca mama na tasya kiṃcana yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma ity etaiś ca pratimantram
4.9.9	agnīṣomayor ahaṃ devayajyayā cakṣuṣmān bhūyāsam ity ājyabhāgau
4.9.10	vihṛtānumantraṇau vā
4.9.11	agninā yajñaś cakṣuṣmān agner ahaṃ devayajyayā cakṣuṣmān bhūyāsam / somena yajñaś cakṣuṣmāṁ somasyāhaṃ devayajyayā cakṣuṣmān bhūyāsam iti vihṛtau
4.9.12	pañcahotāraṃ vadet purastād dhaviravadānasya
4.9.13	agner ahaṃ devayajyayānnādo bhūyāsam ity āgneyaṃ hutam anumantrayate dabdhir asīty upāṃśuyājam agnīṣomayor ity agnīṣomīyam indrāgniyor ity aindrāgnam indrasyety aindraṃ sāmnāyyaṃ mahendrasyeti māhendram agneḥ sviṣṭakṛta iti sauviṣṭakṛtam
4.9.14	purastātsviṣṭakṛto 'nyadevatāny eke samāmananti
4.10.1	indrasya vaimṛdhasyāhaṃ devayajyayāsapatno vīryavān bhūyāsam indrasya trātur ahaṃ devayajyayā trāto bhūyāsaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyor ahaṃ devayajyayobhayor lokayor ṛdhyāsaṃ / bhūmānam pratiṣṭhāṃ gameyam ity eke / pūṣṇo 'haṃ devayajyayā prajaniṣīya prajayā paśubhiḥ sarasvatyā ahaṃ devayajyayā vācam annādyaṃ puṣeyaṃ viśveṣāṃ devānām ahaṃ devayajyayā prāṇaiḥ sāyujyaṃ gameyam aryamṇo 'haṃ devayajyayā svargaṃ lokaṃ gameyam adityā ahaṃ devayajyayā pra prajayā ca paśubhiś ca janiṣīyendrasyendriyāvato 'haṃ devayajyayendriyāvy annādo bhūyāsam iti yathāliṅgaṃ vaikṛtīḥ
4.10.2	agnir mā duriṣṭāt pātv iti prāśitram avadīyamānam
4.10.3	surūpavarṣavarṇa ehītīḍām
4.10.4	bhūyasyehi śreyasyeti vasīyasyehi citta ehi dadhiṣa ehīḍa ehi sūnṛta ehītīḍāyā upāṃśūpahave sapta devagavīr japati / cid asi manāsi dhīr asi rantī ramatiḥ sūnuḥ sūnarīty uccair upahave sapta manuṣyagavīḥ / devīr devair abhi mā nivartadhvaṃ syonāḥ syonena ghṛtena mā samukṣata nama idamudaṃbhiṣag ṛṣir brahmā yad dade samudrād udacann iva srucā vāg agre viprasya tiṣṭhati śṛṅgebhir daśabhir diśann iti ca
4.10.5	upahūyamānāyāṃ vāyav iḍā te māteti hotāram īkṣamāṇo vāyuṃ manasā dhyāyet
4.10.6	sā me satyāśīr ity āśiḥṣu / āśīr ma ūrjam iti ca
4.10.7	iḍāyā ahaṃ devayajyayā paśumān bhūyāsam ity upahūtām // iḍā dhenuḥ sahavatsā na āgād ūrjaṃ duhānā payasā prapīnā / sā no annena haviṣota gobhir iḍābhy asmāṁ āgād iti bhakṣāyāhriyamāṇām
4.10.8	ukta iḍābhakṣo mārjanī ca
4.10.9	bradhna pinvasva dadato me mā kṣāyi kurvato me mopadasad diśāṃ kḷptir asi diśo me kalpantāṃ kalpantāṃ me diśo daivīś ca mānuṣīś cāhorātre me kalpetām ardhamāsā me kalpantāṃ māsā me kalpantām ṛtavo me kalpantāṃ saṃvatsaro me kalpatāṃ kḷptir asi kalpatāṃ ma iti barhiṣi puroḍāśam āsannam abhimṛśati
4.11.1	athainaṃ pratidiśaṃ vyūhaty āśānāṃ tvāśāpālebhyaś caturbhyo amṛtebhyaḥ / idaṃ bhūtasyādhyakṣebhyo vidhema haviṣā vayam // brahmapā hi bhajatāṃ bhāgī bhāgaṃ mābhāgo bhakta nirabhāgaṃ bhajāmaḥ / apas pinvauṣadhīr jinva dvipāt pāhi catuṣpād ava divo vṛṣṭim eraya // brāhmaṇānām idaṃ haviḥ somyānāṃ somapīthinām / nirbhakto 'brāhmaṇo nehābrāhmaṇasyāstīti
4.11.2	upahūto dyauḥ pitopa māṃ dyauḥ pitā hvayatām agnir āgnīdhrād āyuṣe varcase jīvātvai puṇyāyopahūtā pṛthivī mātopa māṃ mātā pṛthivī hvayatām agnir āgnīdhrād āyuṣe varcase jīvātvai puṇyāyety āgnīdhrabhāgasya vaiśeṣikam
4.11.3	bradhna pinvasvety antarvedy anvāhāryam āsannam abhimṛśati // iyaṃ sthāly amṛtasya pūrṇā sahasradhāra utso akṣīyamāṇaḥ / sa dādhāra pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ divaṃ ca tenaudanenātitarāṇi mṛtyum iti ca
4.11.4	uktaḥ saṃpraiṣo 'nvāhāryasya ca dānam
4.11.5	eṣā te agne samid ity ānūyājikīṃ samidham ādhīyamānām // yaṃ te agna āvṛścāmy ahaṃ vā kṣipitaś caran / prajāṃ ca tasya mūlaṃ ca nīcair devā nivṛścata // agne yo no 'bhidāsati samāno yaś ca niṣṭyaḥ / idhmasyeva prakṣāyato mā tasyoccheṣi kiṃcana // yo māṃ dveṣṭi jātavedo yaṃ cāhaṃ dveṣmi yaś ca mām / sarvāṃs tān agne saṃdaha yāṃś cāhaṃ dveṣmi ye ca mām ity āhitāyām agnim
4.11.6	vedir barhiḥ śṛtaṃ havir idhmaḥ paridhayaḥ srucaḥ / ājyaṃ yajña ṛco yajur yājyāś ca vaṣaṭkārāḥ / saṃ me saṃnatayo namantām idhmasaṃnahane huta iti saṃmārgān hutān
4.11.7	saptahotāraṃ vadet purastād anūyājānām upariṣṭād vā
4.12.1	barhiṣo 'haṃ devayajyayā prajāvān bhūyāsam ity etaiḥ pratimantram anūyājān hutaṃhutam
4.12.2	ubau vājavatyau japataḥ
4.12.3	vasūn devān yajñenāpipreṃ rudrān devān yajñenāpiprem ādityān devān yajñenāpiprem iti pratimantraṃ paridhīn ajyamānān // samaṅktāṃ barhir haviṣā ghṛtena sam ādityair vasubhiḥ saṃ marudbhiḥ / sam indreṇa viśvebhir devebhir aṅktāṃ divyaṃ nabho gacchatu yat svāheti prastaram ajyamānam
4.12.4	agner aham ujjitim anūjjeṣam iti yathāliṅgaṃ sūktavākadevatāḥ
4.12.5	yadā cāsya hotā nāma gṛhṇīyād atha brūyād emā agmann āśiṣo dohakāmā iti
4.12.6	sā me satyāśīr devān gamyāj juṣṭāj juṣṭatarā paṇyāt paṇyatarāreḍatā manasā devān gamyād yajño devān gacchatv ado ma āgacchatv iti sūktavākasyāśiḥṣu yat kāmayate tasya nāma gṛhṇāti
4.12.7	rohitena tvāgnir devatāṃ gamayatv ity etaiḥ pratimantram agnīdhā prastaraṃ prahriyamāṇam
4.12.8	divaḥ khīlo 'vatataḥ pṛthivyā adhyutthitaḥ / tenā sahasrakāṇḍena dviṣantaṃ śocayāmasi / dviṣan me bahu śocatv oṣadhe mo ahaṃ śucam iti prastaratṛṇe prahriyamāṇe
4.12.9	vi te muñcāmīti paridhiṣu vimucyamāneṣu
4.12.10	viṣṇoḥ śaṃyor iti śaṃyuvāke / yajña namas te yajña namo namaś ca te yajña śivena me saṃtiṣṭhasva syonena me saṃtiṣṭhasva subhūtena me saṃtiṣṭhasva brahmavarcasena me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajñasyarddhim anu saṃtiṣṭhasvopa te yajña nama upa te nama upa te nama iti ca // iṣṭo yajño bhṛgubhir draviṇodā yatibhir āśīrdā vasubhir āśīrvān / atharvabhis tasya meṣṭasya vītasya draviṇehāgamer iti saṃsrāvaṃ hutam
4.13.1	somasyāhaṃ devayajyayā suretā reto dhiṣīyeti yathāliṅgaṃ patnīsaṃyājān hutaṃhutam
4.13.2	rākāyā ahaṃ devayajyayā prajāvān bhūyāsaṃ sinīvalyā ahaṃ devayajyayā paśumān bhūyāsaṃ kuhvā ahaṃ devayajyayā puṣṭimān paśumān bhūyāsam iti kāmyāḥ
4.13.3	rākāyā ahaṃ devayajyayā prajāvatī bhūyāsaṃ sinīvālyā ahaṃ devayajyayā paśumatī bhūyāsaṃ kuhvā ahaṃ devayajyayā puṣṭimatī paśumatī bhūyāsam iti patny anumantrayate
4.13.4	iḍāsmān anu vastāṃ ghṛtena yasyāḥ pade punate devayantaḥ / vaiśvānarī śakvarī vāvṛdhanopa yajñam asthita vaiśvadevīty ājyeḍām
4.13.5	antarvedi vedaṃ nidhāyābhimṛśati vedo 'sīti
4.13.6	purā videyeti yadyad bhrātṛvyasyābhidhyāyet tasya nāma gṛhṇīyāt / tad evāsya sarvaṃ vṛṅkta iti vijñāyate
4.13.7	yā sarasvatī viśobhagīnā tasyāṃ me rāsva tasyāste bhaktivāno bhūyāsmeti phalīkaraṇahome hute mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe
4.13.8	vasur yajño vasumān yajñas tasya mā yajñasya vasor vasumato vasv āgacchatv ado ma āgacchatv iti samiṣṭayajur hutam anumantrayate / yat kāmayate tasya nāma gṛhṇāti
4.13.9	saṃ yajñapatir āśiṣeti yajamānabhāgaṃ prāśnāti
4.14.1	dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam iti sāyaṃdoham / idaṃ havir iti prātardoham
4.14.2	nābrāhmaṇaḥ sāṃnāyyaṃ prāśnīyāt
4.14.3	antarvedi praṇītāsv adhvaryuḥ saṃtatām udakadhārāṃ srāvayati / sadasi san me bhūyā ity ānīyamānāyāṃ japati
4.14.4	prācyāṃ diśi devā ṛtvijo mārjayantām ity etair yathāliṅgaṃ vyutsicya samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomi svām yonim apigacchata / acchidraḥ prajayā bhūyāsaṃ mā parāseci matpaya ity antarvedi śeṣaṃ ninīya yad apsu te sarasvati goṣv aśveṣu yan madhu / tena me vājinīvati mukham aṅgdhi sarasvati / yā sarasvatī vaiśambalyā tasyāṃ me rāsva tasyās te bhakṣīya tasyās te bhūyiṣṭhabhājo bhūyāsmeti mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe
4.14.5	ubhau kapālavimocanaṃ japataḥ
4.14.6	viṣṇoḥ kramo 'sīti dakṣiṇe vedyante dakṣiṇena padā caturo viṣṇukramān prācaḥ krāmaty uttaramuttaraṃ jyāyāṃsam anatiharan savyam
4.14.7	nāhavanīyam atikrāmati
4.14.8	avasthāya caturthaṃ japati
4.14.9	viṣṇukramān viṣṇvatikramān atīmokṣān iti vyatiṣaktān eke samāmananti / vinirūḍhān eke
4.14.10	agninā devena pṛtanā jayāmīti viṣṇvatikramāḥ / ye devā yajñahana ity atīmokṣāḥ
4.14.11	aganma suvaḥ suvar aganmety ādityam upatiṣṭhate
4.15.1	udyann adya mitram ahaḥ sapatnān me anīnaśaḥ / divainān vidyutā jahi nimrocann adharān kṛdhi // udyann adya vi no bhaja pitā putrebhyo yathā / dīrghāyutvasya heśiṣe tasya no dehi sūrya // udyann adya mitram aha ārohann uttarāṃ divam / hṛdrogaṃ mama sūrya harimāṇaṃ ca nāśaya // śukeṣu me harimāṇaṃ ropaṇākāsu dadhmasi / atho hāridraveṣu me harimāṇaṃ nidadhmasi // udagād ayam ādityo viśvena sahasā saha / dviṣantaṃ mama randhayan mo ahaṃ dviṣato radham // yo naḥ śapād aśapato yaś ca naḥ śapataḥ śapāt / uṣāś ca tasmai nimruk ca sarvaṃ pāpaṃ samūhatām iti ca
4.15.2	aindrīm āvṛtam anvāvarta iti pradakṣiṇam āvartate
4.15.3	yady abhicared idam aham amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasya prāṇaṃ niveṣṭayāmīti dakṣiṇasya padaḥ pārṣṇyā nimṛdnīyāt
4.15.4	puṇyā bhavantu yā lakṣmīḥ parābhavantu yāḥ pāpīr ity uktvā sam ahaṃ prajayā saṃ mayā prajeti punar upāvartate
4.15.5	samiddho agne me dīdihi sameddhā te agne dīdyāsam ity āhavanīyam upasaminddhe / vasumān yajño vasīyān bhūyāsam ity upatiṣṭhate
4.16.1	yo naḥ sapatno yo 'raṇo marto 'bhidāsati devāḥ / idhmasyeva prakṣāyato mā tasyoccheṣi kiṃcaneti ca
4.16.2	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity āgnipāvamānībhyāṃ gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate / agne gṛhapata iti ca
4.16.3	putrasya nāma gṛhṇāti tām āśiṣam āśāse tantava ity ajātasya / amuṣmā iti jātasya
4.16.4	jyotiṣe tantave tvāsāv anu mā tanvacchinno daivyas tantur mā manuṣyaś chedi divyād dhāmno mā cchitsi mā mānuṣād iti priyasya putrasya nāma gṛhṇāti
4.16.5	agne vahne svaditaṃ nas tanaye pituṃ paca / śaṃ tokāya tanuve syona iti dakṣiṇāgnim
4.16.6	jyotiṣe tantave tvety antarvedy upaviśati / pūrvavan nāmagrahaṇam
4.16.7	jyotir asi tantava ity upaviśya japati
4.16.8	vedam upastha ādhāyāntarvedy āsīno 'tīmokṣāñ japati
4.16.9	atra vedastaraṇaṃ yajamānabhāgasya ca prāśanam eke samāmananti
4.16.10	kas tvā yunakti sa tvā vimuñcatv iti yajñaṃ vimuñcati
4.16.11	agne vratapate vratam acāriṣam iti vrataṃ visṛjate
4.16.12	yajño babhūveti yajñasya punarālambhaṃ japati
4.16.13	gomān iti prāṅ udetya gomatīṃ japati
4.16.14	atra vā yajamānabhāgaṃ prāśnīyāt
4.16.15	yajña śaṃ ca ma upa ca ma āyuś ca me balaṃ ca me yajña śivo me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajña sviṣṭo me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajñāriṣṭo me saṃtiṣṭhasveti darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ somena paśunā veṣṭvā japati
4.16.16	vṛṣṭir asi vṛśca me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upāgām itīṣṭvāpa upaspṛśati / tad idaṃ sarvayajñeṣūpasparśanaṃ bhavati
4.16.17	brāhmaṇāṃs tarpayitavā iti saṃpreṣyati
4.16.18	pravasan kāle vihāram abhimukho yājamānaṃ japati
4.16.19	prāco viṣṇukramān krāmati
4.16.20	prāṅ udetya gomatīṃ japati japati
5.1.1	agnyādheyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
5.1.2	yo aśvatthaḥ śamīgarbha āruroha tve sacā / taṃ te harāmi brahmaṇā yajñiyaiḥ ketubhiḥ saheti śamīgarbhasyāśvatthasyāraṇī āharati
5.1.3	apy aśamīgarbhasyeti vājasaneyakam
5.1.4	aśvatthād dhavyavāhād dhi jātām agnes tanūṃ yajñiyāṃ saṃbharāmi / śāntayoniṃ śamīgarbham agnaye prajanayitave / āyur mayi dhehy āyur yajamāna ity araṇī abhimantrya sapta pārthivān saṃbhārān āharati / evaṃ vānaspatyān / pañcapañca vā
5.1.5	bhūyaso vā pārthivān
5.1.6	na saṃbhārān saṃbhared iti vājasaneyakam
5.1.7	vaiśvānarasya rūpaṃ pṛthivyāṃ parisrasā / syonam āviśantu na iti sikatāḥ // yad idaṃ divo yad adaḥ pṛthivyāḥ saṃjajñāne rodasī saṃbabhūvatuḥ / ūṣān kṛṣṇam avatu kṛṣṇam ūṣā ihobhayor yajñiyam āgamiṣṭhā ity ūṣān // ūtīḥ kurvāṇo yat pṛthivīm acaro gūhākāram ākhurūpaṃ pratītya / tat te nyaktam iha saṃbharantaḥ śataṃ jīvema śaradaḥ suvīrā ity ākhukarīṣam // ūrjaṃ pṛthivyā rasam ābharantaḥ śataṃ jīvema śaradaḥ purūcīḥ / vamrībhir anuvittaṃ guhāsu śrotraṃ ta urvy abadhirā bhavāma iti valmīkavapām // prajāpatisṛṣṭānāṃ prajānāṃ kṣudho 'pahatyai suvitaṃ no astu / upaprabhinnam iṣam ūrjaṃ prajābhyaḥ sūdaṃ gṛhebhyo rasam ābharāmīti sūdam // yasya rūpaṃ bibhrad imām avindad guhā praviṣṭāṃ sarirasya madhye / tasyedaṃ vihatam ābhranto 'cchambaṭkāram asyām vidhemeti varāhavihatam
5.2.1	yābhir adṛṃhaj jagataḥ pratiṣṭhām urvīm imāṃ viśvajanasya bhartrīm / tā naḥ śivāḥ śarkarāḥ santu sarvā iti śarkarāḥ // agne retaś candraṃ hiraṇyam adbhyaḥ saṃbhūtam amṛtaṃ prajāsu / tat saṃbharann uttarato nidhāyātiprayacchan duritiṃ tareyam iti hiraṇyam
5.2.2	iti pārthivāḥ
5.2.3	yadi pañcaudumbarāṇi lohaśakalāni pañcamo bhavati
5.2.4	aśvo rūpaṃ kṛtvā yad aśvatthe 'tiṣṭhaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ devebhyo nilāya / tat te nyaktam iha saṃbharantaḥ śataṃ jīvema śaradaḥ suvīrā ity aśvattham // ūrjaḥ pṛthivyā adhyutthito 'si vanaspate śatavalśo viroha / tvayā vayam iṣam ūrjaṃ madanto rāyaspoṣeṇa samiṣā mademety udumbaram // gāyatriyā hriyamāṇasya yat te parṇam apatat tṛtīyasyai divo 'dhi / so 'yaṃ parṇaḥ somaparṇād dhi jātas tato harāmi somapīthasyāvaruddhyai // devānāṃ brahmavādaṃ vadatāṃ yad upāśṛṇoḥ suśravā vai śruto 'si / tato mām āviśatu brahmavarcasaṃ tat saṃbharaṃs tad avarundhīya sākṣād ity etābhyāṃ parṇam // yayā te sṛṣṭasyāgner hetim aśamayat prajāpatiḥ / tām imām apradāhāya śamīṃ śāntyai harāmy aham iti śamīm // yat te sṛṣṭasya yato vikaṅkataṃ bhā ārchaj jātavedaḥ / tayā bhāsā saṃmita uruṃ no lokam anuprabhāhīti vikaṅkatam / yat te tāntasya hṛdayam ācchindañ jātavedo maruto adbhis tamayitvā / etat te tad aśaneḥ saṃbharāmi sātmā agne sahṛdayo bhavehety aśanihatasya vṛkṣasya // yat paryapaśyat sarirasya madhya urvīm apaśyaj jagataḥ pratiṣṭhām / tat puṣkarasyāyatanād dhi jātaṃ parṇaṃ pṛthivyāḥ prathanaṃ harāmīti puṣkaraparṇam // iti vānaspatyāḥ
5.3.1	yaṃ tvā samabharaṃ jātavedo yathā śarīraṃ bhūteṣu nyaktam / sa saṃbhṛtaḥ sīda śivaḥ prajābhya uruṃ no lokam anuneṣi vidvān iti saṃbhṛtya nidadhāti
5.3.2	atha nakṣatrāṇi
5.3.3	kṛttikāsu brāhmaṇa ādadhīta mukhyo brahmavarcasī bhavati
5.3.4	gṛhāṃs tasyāgnir dāhuko bhavati
5.3.5	rohiṇyām ādhāya sarvān rohān rohati
5.3.6	mṛgaśīrṣe brahmavarcasakāmo yajñakāmo vā
5.3.7	yaḥ purā bhadraḥ san pāpīyān syāt punarvasvoḥ
5.3.8	pūrvayoḥ phalgunyor yaḥ kāmayeta dānakāmā me prajā syur iti
5.3.9	uttarayor yaḥ kāmayeta bhagy annādaḥ syām iti
5.3.10	etad evaike viparītam
5.3.11	athāparam / pūrvayor ādhāya pāpīyān bhavaty uttarayor vasīyān
5.3.12	haste yaḥ kāmayeta pra me dīyeteti
5.3.13	citrāyāṃ rājanyo bhrātṛvyavān vā
5.3.14	viśākhayoḥ prajākāmo 'nurādheṣv ṛddhikāmaḥ śravaṇe puṣṭikāma uttareṣu proṣṭhapadeṣu pratiṣṭhākāmaḥ
5.3.15	sarvāṇi nityavad eke samāmananti
5.3.16	phalgunīpūrṇamāsa ādadhītety uktvāha yat phalgunīpūrṇamāsa ādadhyāt saṃvatsarasyainam āsan dadhyād dvyahe puraikāhe vā
5.3.17	amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vādheyaḥ
5.3.18	vasanto brāhmaṇasya grīṣmo rājanyasya hemanto vā śarad vaiśyasya varṣā rathakārasya
5.3.19	ye trayāṇāṃ varṇānām etat karma kuryus teṣām eṣa kālaḥ
5.3.20	śiśiraḥ sārvavarṇikaḥ
5.3.21	somena yakṣyamāṇo nartuṃ sūrkṣen na nakṣatram
5.3.22	udavasāya śālīna ādadhītānudavasāya yāyāvaraḥ
5.3.23	ekāhaṃ vā prayāyāt
5.4.1	uddhanyamānam asyā amedhyam apa pāpmānaṃ yajamānasya hantu / śivā naḥ santu pradiśaś catasraḥ śaṃ no mātā pṛthivī tokasāteti prācīnapravaṇaṃ devayajanam uddhatya śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya āpo bhavantu pītaye / śaṃyor abhisravantu na ity adbhir avokṣya tasminn udīcīnavaṃśaṃ śaraṇaṃ karoti
5.4.2	tasyāgreṇa madhyamaṃ vaṃśaṃ gārhapatyāyatanaṃ bhavati
5.4.3	tasmāt prācīnam aṣṭāsu prakrameṣu brāhmaṇasyāhavanīyāyatanam / ekādaśasu rājanyasya / dvādaśasu vaiśyasya
5.4.4	caturviṃśatyām aparimite yāvatā vā cakṣuṣā manyate tasmān nātidūram ādheya iti sarveṣām aviśeṣeṇa śrūyate
5.4.5	dakṣiṇātaḥpurastādvitṛtīyadeśe gārhapatyasya nedīyasi dakṣiṇāgner āyatanam
5.4.6	anyad āhavanīyāgāram anyad gārhapatyasya
5.4.7	agreṇāhavanīyaṃ sabhāyāṃ sabhyaḥ
5.4.8	taṃ pūrveṇāvasatha āvasathyaḥ
5.4.9	keśaśmaśru vapate nakhāni nikṛntate snāti / evaṃ patnī keśavarjam
5.4.10	kṣaume vasānau jāyāpatī agnim ādadhīyātām
5.4.11	te dakṣiṇākāle 'dhvaryave dattaḥ
5.4.12	aparāhṇe 'dhivṛkṣasūrye vaupāsanād agnim āhṛtyāpareṇa gārhapatyāyatanaṃ brāhmaudanikam ādadhāti
5.4.13	aupāsanaṃ vā sarvam
5.4.14	nirmathyaṃ vā
5.4.15	yadi sarvam aupāsanam āhared apūpaṃ yavamayaṃ vrīhimayaṃ caudumbaraparṇābhyāṃ saṃgṛhyāyatana upāsyed yavamayaṃ paścād vrīhimayaṃ purastāt tasminn ādadhyāt
5.4.16	sarvam apy aupāsanam āharann āpūpāv upāsyed ity aparam
5.5.1	apareṇa brāhmaudanikaṃ lohite carmaṇy ānaḍuhe prācīnagrīva uttaralomni pājake vā niśāyāṃ brahmaudanaṃ catuḥśarāvaṃ nirvapati
5.5.2	devasya tvety anudrutya brahmaṇe prāṇāya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmīti prathamam apānāyeti dvitīyaṃ vyānāyeti tṛtīyaṃ brahmaṇe juṣṭam iti caturtham
5.5.3	tūṣṇīṃ vā sarvāṇi
5.5.4	caturṣūdapātreṣu pacati
5.5.5	na prakṣālayati na prasrāvayati
5.5.6	kṣīre bhavatīty eke
5.5.7	jīvataṇḍulam iva śrapayatīti vijñāyate
5.5.8	darvyā brahmaudanād uddhṛtya pra vedhase kavaye medhyāya vaco vandāru vṛṣabhāya vṛṣṇe / yato bhayam abhayaṃ tan no astv ava devān yaje heḍyān iti juhoty abhi vā mantrayate
5.5.9	caturdhā brahmaudanaṃ vyuddhṛtya prabhūtena sarpiṣopasicya karṣann anucchindaṃś caturbhya ārṣeyebhya ṛtvigbhya upohati
5.5.10	apāttāḥ prathame piṇḍā bhavanty apratihatāḥ pāṇayaḥ / atha brahmaudanaśeṣaṃ saṃkṛṣya tasminn ājyaśeṣam ānīya tasmiṃś citriyasyāśvatthasya tisraḥ samidha ārdrāḥ sapalāśāḥ prādeśamātryaḥ stibhigavatyo vivartayati
5.6.1	citriyād aśvatthāt saṃbhṛtā bṛhatyaḥ śarīram abhisaṃskṛtā stha / prajāpatinā yajñamukhena saṃmitās tisras trivṛdbhir mithunāḥ prajātyā iti
5.6.2	athādadhāti ghṛtavatībhir āgneyībhir gāyatrībhir brāhmaṇasya triṣṭugbhī rājanyasya jagatībhir vaiśyasya
5.6.3	samidhāgniṃ duvasyatety eṣā // upa tvāgne haviṣmatīr ghṛtācīr yantu haryata / juṣasva samidho mama // taṃ tvā samidbhir aṅgiro ghṛtena vardhayāmasi / bṛhac chocā yaviṣṭhyeti brāhmaṇasya // samidhyamānaḥ prathamo nu dharmaḥ samaktubhir ajyate viśvavāraḥ / śociṣkeśo ghṛtanirṇik pāvakaḥ suyajño agnir yajathāya devān // ghṛtapratīko ghṛtayonir agnighṛtaiḥ samiddho ghṛtam asyānnam / ghṛtapruṣas tvā sarito vahanti ghṛtaṃ piban suyajā yakṣi devān // āyurdā agna iti rājanyasya // tvām agne samidhānaṃ yaviṣṭha devā dūtaṃ cakrire havyavāham / urujrayasaṃ ghṛtayonim āhutaṃ tveṣaṃ cakṣur dadhire codayanvati // tvām agne pradiva āhutaṃ ghṛtena sumnāyavaḥ suṣamidhā samīdhire / sa vāvṛdhāna oṣadhībhir ukṣita uru jrayāṃsi pārthivā vitiṣṭhase // ghṛtapratīkaṃ va ṛtasya dhūrṣadam agniṃ mitraṃ na samidhāna ṛñjate / indhāno akro vidatheṣu dīdyac chukravarṇām ud u no yaṃsate dhiyam iti vaiśyasya
5.7.1	samitsu tisro vatsatarīr dadāti
5.7.2	prāśnanti brāhmaṇā odanam
5.7.3	prāśitavadbhyaḥ samānaṃ varaṃ dadāti
5.7.4	yasmin nakṣatre 'gnim ādhāsyan syāt tasmin saṃvatsare purastād etāḥ samidha ādadhyād dvādaśāhe dvyahe tryaha ekāhe vā
5.7.5	ādheyās tv evāgnim ādadhānena
5.7.6	atha vrataṃ carati na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti nāsyāgniṃ gṛhād dharanti nānyata āharanti
5.7.7	brāhmaudanikena saṃvatsaram āsīta
5.7.8	aupāsanaś ced āhita etasminn asyāgnikarmāṇi kriyante
5.7.9	na prayāyāt
5.7.10	nānugacchet
5.7.11	yadi prayāyād anu vā gacched brahmaudanaṃ paktvaitayaivāvṛtā samidha ādadhyāt
5.7.12	yady enaṃ saṃvatsare 'gnyādheyaṃ nopanamed brahmaudanaṃ paktvā samidha ādhāya yadainam upanamed athādadhīta
5.7.13	tasya yāthākāmī bharaṇakalpānām
5.7.14	dvādaśāhaṃ cared ekāhaṃ vā
5.7.15	śva ādhāsyamānaḥ punar brahmaudanaṃ pacati
5.7.16	yo 'syāgnim ādhāsyan syāt sa etāṃ rātriṃ vrataṃ carati na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti
5.7.17	prajā agne saṃvāsayāśāś ca paśubhiḥ saha / rāṣṭrāṇy asmā ādhehi yāny āsan savituḥ sava ity uttareṇa gārhapatyāyatanaṃ kalmāṣam ajaṃ badhnāti
5.8.1	atha yajamāno vratam upaiti vācaṃ ca yacchaty anṛtāt satyam upaimi mānuṣād daivyam upaimi daivīṃ vācaṃ yacchāmīti
5.8.2	vīṇātūṇavenainam etāṃ rātriṃ jāgarayanti
5.8.3	api vā na jāgarti na vācaṃ yacchati
5.8.4	śalkair etāṃ rātrim etam agnim indhāna āste śalkair agnim indhāna ubhau lokau sanem aham / ubhayor lokayor ṛddhvāti mṛtyuṃ tarāmy aham ity etayā
5.8.5	tasminn upavyuṣam araṇī niṣṭapati jātavedo bhuvanasya reta iha siñca tapaso yaj janiṣyate / agnim aśvatthād adhi havyavāhaṃ śamīgarbhāj janayan yo mayobhūḥ // ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya ity etābhyām
5.8.6	agnī rakṣāṃsi sedhati śukraśocir amartyaḥ / śuciḥ pāvaka īḍya ity araṇī abhimantrya mahī viśpatnī sadane ṛtasyārvācī etaṃ dharuṇe rayīṇām / antarvatnī janyaṃ jātavedasam adhvarāṇāṃ janayathaḥ purogām ity araṇī āhriyamāṇe yajamānaḥ pratīkṣate
5.8.7	dohyā ca te dugdhabhṛccorvarī te te bhāgadheyaṃ prayacchāmīti yajamānāya prayacchati
5.8.8	ārohataṃ daśataṃ śakvarīr mamartenāgna āyuṣā varcasā saha / jyog jīvanta uttarāmuttarāṃ samāṃ darśam ahaṃ pūrṇamāsaṃ yajñaṃ yathā yajā iti pratigṛhyartviyavatī stho agniretasau garbhaṃ dadhāthāṃ te vām ahaṃ dade / tat satyaṃ yad vīraṃ bibhṛtho vīraṃ janayiṣyathaḥ // te matprātaḥ prajaniṣyethe te mā prajāte prajanayiṣyathaḥ / prajayā paśubhir brahmavarcasena suvarge loka iti pratigṛhyābhimantrayate yajamānaḥ
5.9.1	mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agniṃ yo no agniḥ pitara ity ubhau japataḥ / apeta vīteti gārhapatyāyatanam uddhatya śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya ity adbhir avokṣati
5.9.2	evaṃ dakṣiṇāgner āhavanīyasya sabhyāvasathyayoś ca
5.9.3	evam anupūrvāṇy evaiṣv ata ūrdhvaṃ karmāṇi kriyante
5.9.4	sikatānām ardhaṃ dvaidhaṃ vibhajyārdhaṃ gārhapatyāyatane nivapaty ardhaṃ dakṣiṇāgneḥ / ardhaṃ traidhaṃ vibhajya pūrveṣu
5.9.5	etenaiva kalpena sarvān pārthivān nivapati
5.9.6	agner bhasmāsīti sikatā nivapati / saṃjñānam ity ūṣān
5.9.7	tān nivapan yad adaś candramasi kṛṣṇaṃ tad ihāstv iti manasā dhyāyati
5.9.8	udehy agne adhi mātuḥ pṛthivyā viśa āviśa mahataḥ sadhasthāt / ākhuṃ tvā ye dadhire devayanto havyavāhaṃ bhuvanasya gopām ity ākhukarīṣam // yat pṛthivyā anāmṛtaṃ saṃbabhūva tve sacā / tad agnir agnaye 'dadāt tasminn ādhīyatām ayam iti gārhapatyāyatane valmīkavapāṃ nivapati
5.9.9	yad antarikṣasyeti dakṣiṇāgneḥ / yad diva iti pūrveṣu
5.9.10	utsamudrān madhumāṁ ūrmir āgāt sāmrājyāya pratarāṃ dadhānaḥ / amī ca ye maghavāno vayaṃ ceṣam ūrjaṃ madhumat saṃbharemeti sūdam / iyaty agra āsīr iti varāhavihatam
5.9.11	ado devī prathamānā pṛthag yad devair nyuptā vyasarpo mahitvā / adṛṃhathāḥ śarkarābhis triviṣṭapy ajayo lokān pradiśaś catasra iti śarkarāḥ / dveṣyaṃ ca manasā dhyāyati
5.10.1	ṛtaṃ stṝṇāmi purīṣaṃ pṛthivyām ṛte 'dhy agnim ādadhe satye 'dhy agnim ādadha ity āyataneṣu saṃbhārān anuvyūhati
5.10.2	saṃ yā vaḥ priyās tanuva ity eṣā // saṃ vaḥ sṛjāmi hṛdayāni saṃsṛṣṭaṃ mano astu vaḥ / saṃsṛṣṭaḥ prāṇo astu va iti vānaspatyān saṃsṛjya sikatāvan nivapatītaḥ prathamaṃ jajñe agnir ity etayā
5.10.3	yās te śivās tanuvo jātavedo yā antarikṣe divi yāḥ pṛthivyām / tābhiḥ saṃbhūya sagaṇaḥ sajoṣā hiraṇyayonir vaha havyam agna iti gārhapatyāyatane sauvarṇaṃ hiraṇyaśakalam uttarataḥ saṃbhāreṣūpāsyati
5.10.4	candram agniṃ candrarathaṃ haritvacaṃ vaiśvānaram apsuṣadaṃ suvarvidam / vigāhaṃ tūrṇiṃ taviṣībhir āvṛtaṃ bhūrṇiṃ devāsa iha suśriyaṃ dadhur ity upāstam abhimantrayate / dveṣyāya rajataṃ prayacchati
5.10.5	yadi dveṣyaṃ nādhigacched yāṃ diśaṃ dveṣyaḥ syāt tena nirasyet
5.10.6	evaṃ sarveṣūpāsya karoti
5.10.7	brāhmaudanikād bhasmāpohya tasmiñ chamīgarbhād agniṃ manthati
5.10.8	udyatsu raśmiṣu daśahotrāraṇī samavadadhāti
5.10.9	sahāgne 'gninā jāyasva saha rayyā saha puṣṭyā saha prajayā saha paśubhiḥ saha brahmavarcasenety upatiṣṭhaty aśve 'gniṃ manthati
5.10.10	śveto 'śvo 'viklinnākṣo bhavati rohito vāsitajānur api vā ya eva kaścit sāṇḍaḥ
5.10.11	mathyamāne śakteḥ sāṃkṛteḥ sāma gāyati / dhūme jāte gāthinaḥ kauśikasya / araṇyor nihito jātavedā iti ca
5.10.12	upāvaroha jātaveda iti nirvartyamānam abhimantrayate
5.11.1	atra caturhotṝn yajamānaṃ vācayati
5.11.2	ajann agniḥ pūrvaḥ pūrvebhyaḥ pavamānaḥ śuciḥ pāvaka īḍya iti jātam abhimantrayate
5.11.3	jāte yajamāno varaṃ dadāti
5.11.4	gaur vai varo 'tivaro 'nyo dhenur varo 'tivaro 'nyo 'naḍvān varo 'tivaro 'nyaḥ paṣṭhauhī varo 'tivaro 'nyaḥ
5.11.5	jātaṃ yajamāno 'bhiprāṇiti prajāpates tvā prāṇenābhiprāṇimi pūṣṇaḥ poṣeṇa mahyaṃ dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya śataṃ śaradbhya āyuṣe varcase jīvātvai puṇyāyeti
5.11.6	ajījanann amṛtaṃ martyāso 'sremāṇaṃ taraṇiṃ vīḍujambham / daśa svasāro agruvaḥ samīcīḥ pumāṃsaṃ jātam abhisaṃrabhantām iti jātam añjalinābhigṛhya samrāḍ asi virāḍ asi sārasvatau tvotsau samindhātām annādaṃ tvānnapatyāyety upasamidhyāthainaṃ prāñcam uddhṛtyāsīnaḥ sarveṣāṃ mantrāṇām antena rathaṃtare gīyamāne yajñāyajñīye ca yatharṣyādhānena prathamayā vyāhṛtyā dvābhyāṃ vā prathamābhyāṃ ca sarparājñībhyāṃ prathamena ca gharmaśirasā
5.11.7	bhṛgūṇāṃ tvā devānāṃ vratapate vratenādadhāmīti bhārgavasyādadhyāt / aṅgirasāṃ tvā devānāṃ vratapate vratenādadhāmīti yo brāhmaṇa āṅgirasaḥ syāt / ādityānāṃ tvā devānāṃ vratapate vratenādadhāmīty anyāsāṃ brāhmaṇīnāṃ prajānām / varuṇasya tvā rājño vratapate vratenādadhāmīti rājñaḥ / indrasya tvendriyeṇa vratapate vratenādadhāmīti rājanyasya / manos tvā grāmaṇyo vratapate vratenādadhāmīti vaiśyasya / ṛbhūṇāṃ tvā devānāṃ vratapate vratenādadhāmīti rathakārasyeti yatharṣyādhānāni
5.12.1	bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar iti vyāhṛtyaḥ / bhūmir bhūmneti sarparājñiyaḥ / gharmaḥ śiras tad ayam agniḥ saṃpriyaḥ paśubhir bhuvat / chardis tokāya tanayāya yaccha // vātaḥ prāṇas tad ayam agniḥ saṃpriyaḥ paśubhir bhuvat / svaditaṃ tokāya tanayāya pituṃ paca // arkaś cakṣus tad asau sūryas tad ayam agniḥ saṃpriyaḥ paśubhir bhuvat / yat te śukra śaukraṃ varcaḥ śukrā tanūḥ śukraṃ jyotir ajasraṃ tena me dīdihi tena tvādadhe 'gnināgne brahmaṇeti gharmaśirāṃsi
5.12.2	yās te śivās tanuvo jātavedo yā antarikṣa uta pārthivīr yāḥ / tābhiḥ saṃbhūya sagaṇaḥ sajoṣā hiraṇyayonir vaha havyam agne // prāṇaṃ tvāmṛta ādadhāmy annādam annādyāya goptāraṃ guptyai / divas tvā vīryeṇa pṛthivyai mahimnāntarikṣasya poṣeṇa paśūnāṃ tejasā sarvapaśum ādadhe // agne gṛhapate 'he budhnyā pariṣadya divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣāl lokaṃ vinda yajamānāya / pṛthivyās tvā mūrdhan sādayāmi yajñiye loke / yo no agne niṣṭyo yo 'niṣṭyo 'bhidāsatīdam ahaṃ taṃ tvayābhinidadhāmīti saṃbhāreṣu nidadhāti
5.12.3	sugārhapatyo vidahann arātīr uṣasaḥ śreyasīḥśreyasīr dadhat / agne sapatnāṁ apabādhamāno rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dhehīty ādhīyamānam abhimantrayate yajamāno ghramaśirāṃsi cainam adhvaryur vācayati
5.13.1	ardhodite sūrya āhavanīyam ādadhāti
5.13.2	udite brahmavarcasakāmasya
5.13.3	gārhapatye praṇayanīyam āśvattham idhmam ādīpayati sikatāś copayamanīr upakalpayate
5.13.4	tam udyacchaty ojase balāya tvodyacche vṛṣaṇe śuṣmāyāyuṣe varcase / sapatnatūr asi vṛtratūḥ // yas te deveṣu mahimā suvargo yas ta ātmā paśuṣu praviṣṭaḥ / puṣṭir yā te manuṣyeṣu paprathe tayā no agne juṣamāṇa ehi // divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣād vātāt paśubhyo adhy oṣadhībhyaḥ / yatrayatra jātavedaḥ saṃbabhūtha tato no agne juṣamāṇa ehi // ud u tvā viśve devā ity etābhiś catasṛbhiḥ
5.13.5	uparīvāgnim udyacchati
5.13.6	udyatam upayataṃ dhārayati
5.13.7	athāśvasya dakṣiṇe karṇe yajamānam agnitanūr vācayati yā vājinn agneḥ paśuṣu pavamānā priyā tanūs tām āvaha yā vājinn agner apsu pāvakā priyā tanūs tām āvaha yā vājinn agneḥ sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūs tām āvaheti / dhārayaty evāgnim
5.13.8	athāgnīdhro laukikam agnim āhṛtya mathitvā vordhvajñur āsīno dakṣiṇām agnim ādadhāti yajñāyajñīye gīyamāne yatharṣyādhānena dvitīyayā vyāhṛtyā tisṛbhiḥ sarparājñībhir dvitīyena ca gharmaśirasā // yās te śivās tanuvo jātavedo yā antarikṣa uta pārthivīr yāḥ / tābhiḥ saṃbhūya sagaṇaḥ sajoṣā hiraṇyayonir vaha havyam agne // vyānaṃ tvāmṛta ādadhāmy annādam annādyāya goptāraṃ guptyai / divas tvā vīryeṇa pṛthivyai mahimnāntarikṣasya poṣeṇa paśūnāṃ tejasā sarvapaśum ādadhe // agne 'nnapā mayobhuva suśevadivaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣāl lokaṃ vinda yajamānāya / pṛthivyās tvā mūrdhan sādayāmi yajñiye loke / yo no agne niṣṭyo yo 'niṣṭyo 'bhidāsatīdam ahaṃ taṃ tvayābhinidadhāmīti saṃbhāreṣu nidadhāti
5.14.1	yo brāhmaṇo rājanyo vaiśyaḥ śūdro vāsura iva bahupuṣṭaḥ syāt tasya gṛhād āhṛtyādadhyāt puṣṭikāmasya
5.14.2	gṛhe tv asya tato nāśnīyāt
5.14.3	ambarīṣād annākāmasya vṛkṣāgrāj jvalato brahmavarcasakāmasya
5.14.4	vāmadevyam abhigāyata āhavanīya uddhriyamāṇe
5.14.5	prācīm anu pradiśam ity eṣā // vikramasva mahāṁ asi vediṣan mānuṣebhyaḥ / triṣu lokeṣu jāgṛhi prajayā ca dhanena ca // imā u mām upatiṣṭhantu rāya ābhiḥ prajābhir iha saṃvaseya / iho iḍā tiṣṭhatu viśvarūpī madhye vasor dīdihi jātaveda iti prāñco 'śvaprathamā abhipravrajanti
5.14.6	dakṣiṇato brahmā rathaṃ rathacakraṃ vā vartayati yāvaccakraṃ triḥ parivartate
5.14.7	ṣaṭkṛtvo dveṣyasya
5.14.8	jānudaghne dhārayamāṇas tṛtīyam adhvano 'gniṃ harati nābhidaghne tṛtīyam āsyadaghne tṛtīyam / na karṇadaghnam atyudgṛhṇāti
5.14.9	yady udgṛhya nigṛhṇīyān mukhena saṃmāyādadhyāt
5.14.10	nāgnim ādityaṃ ca vyaveyāt
5.14.11	dakṣiṇataḥ parigṛhya harati
5.14.12	ardhādhve yajamāno varaṃ dadāti
5.14.13	ardhādhve hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya nāko 'si bradhnaḥ pratiṣṭhā saṃkramaṇa ity atikrāmati
5.14.14	prāñcam aśvam abhyasthād viśvā iti dakṣiṇena padottarataḥ saṃbhārān ākramayati yathāhitasyāgner aṅgārāḥ padam abhyavavarterann iti
5.14.15	pradakṣiṇam āvartayitvā yad akranda iti punar evākramayati
5.14.16	purastāt pratyañcam aśvaṃ dhārayati
5.14.17	pūrvavāḍ aśvo bhavati
5.14.18	tadabhāve 'naḍvān pūrvavāḍ etāni karmāṇi karotīti paiṅgāyanibrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
5.15.1	kamaṇḍalupada ādadhīteti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇam / ajasya pada ādadhīteti vājasaneyakam
5.15.2	atha yajamānaḥ śivā japati ye te agne śive tanuvau virāṭ ca svarāṭ ca te mā viśatāṃ te mā jinvatām / ye te agne śive tanuvau samrāṭ cābhibhūś ca te mā viśatāṃ te mā jinvatām / ye te agne śive tanuvau vibhūś ca paribhūś ca te mā viśatāṃ te mā jinvatām / ye te agne śive tanuvau prabhvī ca prabhūtiś ca te mā viśatāṃ te mā jinvatām / yās te agne śivās tanuvas tābhis tvādadha iti
5.15.3	yās te agne ghorās tanuvas tābhir amuṃ gaccheti yajamāno dveṣyāya prahiṇoti tābhir enaṃ parābhāvayati
5.15.4	araṇye 'nuvākyā bhavanti
5.15.5	yad idaṃ divo yad adaḥ pṛthivyāḥ saṃvidāne rodasī saṃbabhūvatuḥ / tayoḥ pṛṣṭhe sīdatu jātavedāḥ śaṃbhūḥ prajābhyas tanuve syona ity abhimantrya purastāt pratyaṅ tiṣṭhann āhavanīyam ādadhāti
5.15.6	bṛhati gīyamāne śyaitavāravantīyayor yajñāyajñīye ca yatharṣyādhānena sarvābhir vyāhṛtībhiḥ sarvābhiḥ sarparājñībhis tṛtīyena ca gharmaśirasā yās te śivās tanuvo jātavedo yā antarikṣa uta pārthivīr yāḥ / tābhiḥ saṃbhūya sagaṇaḥ sajoṣā hiraṇyayonir vaha havyam agne // apānaṃ tvāmṛta ādadhāmy annādam annādyāya goptāraṃ guptyai / divas tvā vīryeṇa pṛthivyai mahimnāntarikṣasya poṣeṇa paśūnāṃ tejasā sarvapaśum ādadhe // agne samrāḍ ajaikapād āhavanīya divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣāl lokaṃ vinda yajamānāya / pṛthivyās tvā mūrdhan sādayāmi yajñiye loke / yo no agne niṣṭyo yo 'niṣṭyo 'bhidāsatīdam ahaṃ taṃ tvayābhinidadhāmīti saṃbhāreṣu nidadhāti
5.16.1	ānaśe vyānaśe sarvam āyur vyānaśe / ahaṃ tvad asmi mad asi tvam etan mamāsi yonis tava yonir asmi / mamaiva san vaha havyāny agne putraḥ pitre lokakṛj jātaveda ity ādhīyamānam abhimantrayate yajamānaḥ
5.16.2	vyāhṛtīḥ sarparājñīr gharmaśirāṃsīti sarveṣv ādhāneṣu yajamāno 'nuvartayate yenayenādadhāti
5.16.3	nāhitam anabhihutam agnim upaspṛśati / ājyenauṣadhībhiś ca śamayitavyaḥ
5.16.4	yā te agne paśuṣu pavamānā priyā tanūr yā pṛthivyāṃ yāgnau yā rathantare yā gāyatre chandasi tāṃ ta etenāvayaje svāhā / yā te agne 'psu pāvakā priyā tanūr yāntarikṣe yā vāyau yā vāmadevye yā traiṣṭubhe chandasi tāṃ ta etenāvayaje svāhā / yā te agne sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūr yā divi yāditye yā bṛhati yā jāgate chandasi tāṃ ta etenāvayaje svāhety etaiḥ pratimantram ājyam oṣadhīś ca juhoti
5.16.5	samidha ādadhātīty eke
5.16.6	brahmāgnyādheye sāmāni gāyati
5.16.7	pratiṣiddhāny ekeṣām
5.16.8	vyāhṛtībhir evodgīthaṃ bhavatīti vājasaneyakam
5.17.1	tataḥ sabhyāvasathyāv ādadhāti laukikam agnim āhṛtya mathitvāhavanīyād vā yatharṣyādhānena
5.17.2	agna āyūṃṣi pavase 'gne pavasva svapāḥ / agnir ṛṣiḥ pavamānaḥ pañcajanyaḥ purohitaḥ / tam īmahe mahāgayam iti tisra āśvatthyaḥ samidha ekaikasminn ādadhāti
5.17.3	āhavanīye vā tisraḥ
5.17.4	samudrād ūrmir madhumāṁ udārad upāṃśunā sam amṛtatvam ānaṭ / ghṛtasya nāma guhyaṃ yad asti jihvā devānām amṛtasya nābhiḥ // vayaṃ nāma prabravāmā ghṛtenāsmin yajñe dhārayāmā namobhiḥ / upa brahmā śṛṇavac chasyamānaṃ catuḥśṛṅgo 'vamīd gaura etat // catvāri śṛṅgā trayo asya pādā dve śīrṣe sapta hastāso asya / tridhā baddho vṛṣabho roravīti maho devo martyāṁ āviveśeti śamīmayyo ghṛtānvaktās tisṛbhis tisra ekaikasminn ādadhāti / āhavanīye vā tisraḥ
5.17.5	evaṃ nānāvṛkṣīyāḥ / preddho agne dīdihi puro na ity audumbarīṃ samidham ādadhāti / vidhema te parame janmann agna iti vaikaṅkatīm / tāṃ savitur vareṇyasya citrām iti śamīmayīm
5.17.6	tatas tūṣṇīm agnihotraṃ juhoti
5.17.7	api vā dvādaśagṛhītena srucaṃ pūrayitvā prajāpatiṃ manasā dhyāyañ juhoti / sāgnihotrasya sthāne bhavati
5.17.8	yas te agne ghorās tanuvas tābhir amuṃ gaccheti yajamāno dveṣyāya prahiṇoti tābhir enaṃ nitamayati / araṇye 'nuvākyā bhavanti
5.18.1	dvādaśagṛhītena srucaṃ pūrayitvā sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvā iti saptavatyā pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti / hutāyāṃ yajamāno varaṃ dattvā śivā japati / ye agnayo divo ye pṛthivyāḥ samāgacchantīṣam ūrjaṃ duhānāḥ / te asmā agnayo draviṇaṃ dattveṣṭāḥ prītā āhutibhājo bhūtvā yathālokaṃ punarastaṃ pareta svāheti juhoti
5.18.2	atha virāṭkramair yajamāna upatiṣṭhate 'tharva pituṃ me gopāyānnaṃ prānena saṃmitam / tvayā guptā iṣam ūrjaṃ madanto rāyaspoṣeṇa sam iṣā mademety anvāhāryapacanam // narya prajāṃ me gopāya mūlaṃ lokasya saṃtatim / ātmano hṛdayān nirmitāṃ tāṃ te paridadāmy aham iti gārhapatyam // śaṃsya paśūn me gopāya viśvarūpaṃ dhanaṃ vasu / gṛhāṇāṃ puṣṭim ānandaṃ tāṃs te paridadāmy aham ity āhavanīyam // sapratha sabhāṃ me gopāyendriyaṃ bhūtivardhanam / viśvajanasya chāyāṃ tāṃ te paridadāmy aham iti sabhyam // ahe budhniya mantraṃ me gopāya śriyaṃ ca yaśasā saha / ahaye budhniyāya mantraṃ śriyaṃ yaśaḥ paridadāmy aham ity āvasathyam // pañcadhāgnīn vyakrāmad virāṭ sṛṣṭā prajāpateḥ / ūrdhvārohad rohiṇī yonir agneḥ pratiṣṭhitir iti sarvān
5.19.1	āgneyasyāṣṭākapālasya tantraṃ prakramayati
5.19.2	niruptaṃ havir upasannam aprokṣitaṃ bhavati / atha sabhāyā madhye 'dhidevanam uddhatyāvokṣyākṣān nyupyākṣeṣu hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya samūhya vyūhya prathayitvā niṣasāda dhṛtavrata iti madhye 'dhidevane rājanyasya juhoti
5.19.3	āvasathe pariṣado madhye hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya mantravatyā hiraṇye juhoti pra nūnaṃ brahmaṇaspatir mantraṃ vadaty ukthyam / yasminn indro varuṇo mitro aryamā devā okāṃsi cakrira iti
5.19.4	uta no 'hir budhnyaḥ śṛṇotv aja ekapāt pṛthivī samudraḥ / viśve devā ṛtāvṛdho huvānāḥ stutā mantrāḥ kaviśastā avantu na ity uktvā śatam akṣān yajamānāya prayacchann āha vrīhibhyo gāṃ dīvyatāhiṃsantaḥ parūṃṣi viśasateti
5.19.5	saṃpraiṣavat kurvanti
5.20.1	kṛtaṃ yajamāno vijināti
5.20.2	tayā yaj jayanti tad annaṃ saṃskṛtya sabhāsadbhya upaharanti
5.20.3	āvasathe bhuñjate
5.20.4	kḷptisāmanasībhyām agnīn yajamāna upatiṣṭhate kalpetāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ye 'gnayaḥ samanasa iti
5.20.5	prokṣādi karma pratipadyate
5.20.6	āgneyasya dakṣiṇākāle dakṣiṇā dadāti
5.20.7	ajaṃ pūrṇapātram upabarhaṇaṃ sārvasūtram ity agnīdhe
5.20.8	vahinam aśvaṃ brahmaṇe 'dhvaryave vā
5.20.9	āhavanīyadeśe 'naḍvāham adhvaryave
5.20.10	apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ dhenuṃ hotre
5.20.11	vāso mithunau gāvau navaṃ ca rathaṃ dadāti / tāni sādhāraṇāni sarveṣām
5.20.12	ā dvādaśabhyo dadātīty uktvāha kāmam ūrdhvaṃ deyam aparimitasyāvaruddhyā iti vijñāyate
5.20.13	ūrdhvam ādiṣṭadakṣiṇābhyo vadati ṣaḍ deyā dvādaśa deyāś caturviṃśatir deyā iti
5.20.14	tā vikalpante
5.20.15	yeṣāṃ paśūnāṃ puṣṭiṃ bhūyasīṃ kāmayeta teṣāṃ vayasām
5.20.16	dityauhīṃ dadyād dityavāhaṃ ca muṣkaram
5.20.17	vardhamānāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
5.20.18	yady anāḍhyo 'gnīn ādadhīta kāmam evaikāṃ gāṃ dadyāt sā gavāṃ pratyāmnāyo bhavatīti vijñāyate
5.20.19	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.21.1	pavamānahavīṃṣi sadyo nirvapet
5.21.2	dvādaśāhe dvyahe tryahe caturahe 'rdhamāse māsy ṛtau saṃvatsare vā
5.21.3	na somenāyakṣyamāṇaḥ purā saṃvatsarān nirvapet
5.21.4	nirvaped ity eke
5.21.5	yadi nirvaped agnaye pavamānāyāgnaye pāvakāyāgnaye śucaya iti tisra ājyāhutīḥ somadevatābhyo vā hutvā nirvapet
5.21.6	samānatantrāṇi nānātantrāṇi vāgneyena vā samānatantrāṇi
5.21.7	yaṃ kāmayeta pāpīyān syād iti tasyaikamekam etāni havīṃṣi nirvapet / na vasīyān na pāpīyān iti tasya sākaṃ sarvāṇi / yaṃ kāmayetottaraṃ vasīyāñ chreyān syād iti tasyāgnaye pavamānāya nirupya pāvakaśucibhyāṃ samānabarhiṣī nirvapet
5.21.8	śatamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇā
5.21.9	pūrvayor haviṣor dve triṃśanmāne uttarasmiṃś catvāriṃśanmānam
5.21.10	yena hiraṇyaṃ mimate tena mītvā dadāti
5.21.11	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.22.1	aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapaty ādityaṃ ca ghṛte carum
5.22.2	saptadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ
5.22.3	caturdhākaraṇakāla ādityaṃ brahmaṇe pariharati
5.22.4	taṃ catvāra ārṣeyāḥ prāśnanti
5.22.5	prāśitavadbhyaḥ samānaṃ varaṃ dadāti / dhenvanaḍuhor dānam eke samāmananti / siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.22.6	āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapaty agnīṣomīyam ekādaśakapālaṃ viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya tryuddhau ghṛte carum
5.22.7	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.22.8	ādityaṃ ghṛte caruṃ saptadaśasāmidhenīkaṃ dhenudakṣiṇaṃ sarveṣām anunirvāpyāṇāṃ sthāne vājasneyinaḥ samāmananti
5.22.9	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.22.10	agnihotram ārapsyamāno daśahotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ hutvātha sāyam agnihotraṃ juhoti
5.22.11	vyāhṛtībhir upasādayet
5.22.12	saṃvatsare paryāgata etābhir evopasādayet
5.22.13	dvādaśāham ajasreṣv agniṣu yajamānaḥ svayam agnihotraṃ juhuyād apravasann ahataṃ vāso bibharti
5.23.1	yāṃ prathamām agnihotrāya dogdhi tāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
5.23.2	athaikeṣām / agnīn ādhāya hastāv avanijya saṃvatsaram agnihotraṃ hutvātha darśapūrṇamāsāv ārabhate tābhyāṃ saṃvatsaram iṣṭvā somena paśunā vā yajate tata ūrdhvam anyāni karmāṇi kurute
5.23.3	trayodaśarātram ahatavāsā yajamānaḥ svayam agnihotraṃ juhuyād apravasann atraiva somena paśunā veṣṭvāgnīn utsṛjati yathā suyavasān kṛtvā prājyāt tādṛk tad iti śāṭyāyanibrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
5.23.4	pūrṇā paścād yat te devā adadhur iti sārasvatau homau hutvānvārambhaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapati
5.23.5	āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ sarasvatyai caruṃ sarasvate dvādaśakapālam
5.23.6	agnaye bhagine 'ṣṭākapālaṃ yaḥ kāmayeta bhagy annādaḥ syām iti
5.23.7	nityavad eke samāmananti
5.23.8	nānātantram eke
5.23.9	tvad viśvā subhaga saubhagāny agne vi yanti vanino na vayāḥ / śruṣṭī rayir vājo vṛtratūrye divo vṛṣṭir īḍyo rītir apām // tvaṃ bhago na ā hi ratnam iṣe parijmeva kṣayasi dasmavarcāḥ / agne mitro na bṛhata ṛtasyāsi kṣattā vāmasya deva bhūrer iti yājyānuvākye
5.24.1	cittaṃ ca cittiś ceti purastāt sviṣṭakṛto jayāñ juhoti
5.24.2	cittāya svāhā cittyai svāhety eke samāmananti
5.24.3	prajāpatir jayān iti trayodaśīm
5.24.4	agne balada saha ojaḥ kramamāṇāya me dāḥ / abhiśastikṛte 'nabhiśastenyāyāsyai janatāyai śraiṣṭyāyeti caturdaśīṃ yaḥ kāmayeta citraṃ janatāyāṃ syām iti / citraṃ bhavati śabalaṃ tv asya mukhe jāyate
5.24.5	mithunau gāvau dakṣiṇā
5.24.6	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.24.7	darśapūrṇamāsāv ārapsyamānaś caturhotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ hutvātha darśapūrṇamāsāv ārabhate
5.24.8	vyāhṛtībhir havīṃṣy āsādayet saṃvatsare paryāgata etābhir evāsādayet
5.24.9	amāvāsyāyām ādadhānasyaitat / paurṇamāsyāṃ tu pūrvasmin parvaṇi seṣṭi sānvārambhaṇīyam ādhānam apavṛjya
5.25.1	śvo bhūte paurṇamāsena yajate
5.25.2	anantaram ādhānād āhitāgnivratāni
5.25.3	nānṛtaṃ vadet
5.25.4	nāsya brāhmaṇo 'nāśvān gṛhe vaset
5.25.5	sūryoḍham atithiṃ vasatyai nāparundhīta
5.25.6	narbīsapakvasyāśnīyāt
5.25.7	klinnaṃ dāru nādadhyāt
5.25.8	antar nāvy apāṃ nāśnīyāt
5.25.9	svakṛta iriṇe nāvasyet
5.25.10	puṇyaḥ syāt
5.25.11	hiṅkṛtya vāgyataḥ striyam upeyāt
5.25.12	vyāhared vā
5.25.13	na sāyam āhutāv ahutāyām aśnīyāt
5.25.14	evaṃ prātaḥ
5.25.15	āhitāgner gṛhe na sāyamahute bhoktavyaṃ tathā prātar ity anyeṣāṃ vratam
5.25.16	naktaṃ nānyad annād dadyāt
5.25.17	dadyād ity eke
5.25.18	annaṃ tu dadan na dayīta
5.25.19	naitasmin saṃvatsare paśunāniṣṭvā māṃsaṃ bhakṣayet
5.25.20	manasāgnibhyaḥ prahiṇomi bhakṣaṃ mama vācā taṃ saha bhakṣayantu / apramādyann apramattaś carāmi śivena manasā saha bhakṣayateti yady ādiṣṭo bhakṣayed etaṃ mantram uktvā bhakṣayet
5.26.1	punarādheyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
5.26.2	tasyāgnyādheyavatkalpaḥ
5.26.3	agnīn ādhāyaitasmin saṃvatsare yo nardhnuyāt sa punar ādadhīta prajākāmaḥ paśukāmaḥ puṣṭikāmo jyānyāṃ putramartyāyāṃ sveṣv ārudhyamāneṣu yadā vāṅgena vidhuratāṃ nīyāt
5.26.4	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ vāruṇaṃ daśakapālam agnaye 'psumate 'ṣṭākapālaṃ maitraṃ carum agnim udvāsayiṣyan
5.26.5	yā te agna utsīdataḥ pavamānā priyā tanūḥ / tayā saha pṛthivīm āviśa rathaṃtareṇa sāmnā gāyatreṇa ca chandasā // yā te agne pāvakā yā manasā preyasī priyā tanūḥ / tayā sahāntarikṣam āviśa vāmadevyena sāmnā traiṣṭubhena ca chandasā / tato na ūrjam ā kṛdhi gṛhamedhaṃ ca vardhaya // yā te agne sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūḥ śukre 'dhyadhi saṃbhṛtā / tayā saha divam āviśa bṛhatā sāmnā jāgatena ca chandasā tato no vṛṣṭyāvata // yās te agne kāmadughā vibhaktīr anusaṃbhṛtāḥ / tābhir naḥ kāmān dhukṣveha prajāṃ puṣṭim atho dhanam // yās te agne saṃbhṛtīr indraḥ sūkara ābharat / tāsu śociṣu sīdeha bhasma vaiśvānarasya yat
5.27.1	ye te agne vānaspatyāḥ saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhṛtāḥ saha / tebhir gaccha vanaspatīn svāṃ yoniṃ yathāyatham // agann agnir yathālokam asadat sadane sve / avīrahatyaṃ deveṣūpāgāṃ manasā saheti purastāt sviṣṭakṛtaḥ saptāhutīr juhoti
5.27.2	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.27.3	paurṇamāsīm iṣṭvā jvalato 'gnīn utsṛjati
5.27.4	saṃvatsaraṃ parārdhyam utsṛṣṭāgnir bhavati
5.27.5	rohiṇī punarvasū anurādhā iti nakṣatrāṇi
5.27.6	varṣāsu śaradi vādadhīta
5.27.7	kṛtākṛtāḥ saṃbhārā yajūṃṣi ca bhavanti
5.27.8	api vā pañca pārthivān saṃbhārān āharati / evaṃ vānaspatyān
5.27.9	āyataneṣu purāṇān darbhān saṃstīrya bhūmir bhūmneti sarparājñībhir gārhapatyam ādadhāti
5.27.10	madhyaṃdina itarān
5.27.11	upolavair darbhaiḥ parutkaiḥ saṃvatsarapravātair āhavanīyaṃ jvalantam uddharati
5.27.12	yat tvā kruddhaḥ parovapeti dakṣiṇāgnim / yat te manyuparoptasyetītarān
5.27.13	mano jyotir juṣatām iti bṛhaspativatyarcopatiṣṭhate
5.27.14	sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvā ity agnihotraṃ juhoti
5.28.1	āgneyaṃ pañcakapālaṃ nirvapaty aṣṭākapālaṃ vā
5.28.2	yadi pañcakapālo gāyatryau saṃyājye / yady aṣṭākapālaḥ paṅktyau
5.28.3	sarvam āgneyaṃ bhavati
5.28.4	pañcadaśa saptadaśa vā sāmidhenyaḥ
5.28.5	sāmidhenīprabhṛty upāṃśu yajaty ottamād anūyājād uccaiḥ sviṣṭakṛtam
5.28.6	agnāgne 'gnāv agne 'gnināgne 'gnim agna iti caturṣu prayājeṣu catasro vibhaktīr dadhāti
5.28.7	nottame
5.28.8	vibhaktim uktvā prayājena vaṣaṭkaroti
5.28.9	yaṃ kāmayetardhnuyād iti tasyopariṣṭād yeyajāmahād vibhaktiṃ dadhyāt purā vā vaṣaṭkārāt
5.28.10	agniṃ stomena bodhayety āgneyasyājyabhāgasya puro'nuvākyā bhavati / agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti saumyasya
5.28.11	agnir mūrdheti vā saumyasya kuryāt
5.28.12	prajākāmapaśukāmasya prajāvyṛddhapaśuvyṛddhasya vā
5.28.13	agninyaktāḥ patnīsaṃyājānām ṛco bhavanti
5.28.14	api vā yathāpūrvam ājyabhāgāv evaṃ patnīsaṃyājāḥ
5.28.15	agne tam adyāśvam ity akṣarapaṅktyo yājyānuvākyā bhavanti / dve āgneyasya dve sviṣṭakṛtaḥ
5.28.16	punar ūrjā saha rayyety abhitaḥ puroḍāśam āhutīr juhoti
5.28.17	punar ūrjeti vā purastāt prayājānāṃ saha rayyety upariṣṭād anūyājānām
5.28.18	etad vā viparītam
5.28.19	ubhayīr dakṣiṇā dadāti
5.29.1	āgnyādheyikīḥ paunarādheyikīś ca punarniṣkṛto ratha ity etāḥ śatamānaṃ ca hiraṇyam
5.29.2	tasmād rajataṃ hiraṇyam ity uktam
5.29.3	punarabhihito rathaḥ punarutsyūtaṃ syāmūlaṃ punaḥkāmasyāptyā ity ekeṣām
5.29.4	yadītarāṇi na vidyerann apy anaḍvāham eva dadyāt / anaḍuhi ha vā ete ca kāmā ataś ca bhūyāṃsa iti paiṅgāyanibrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
5.29.5	deve agnau devo agnir iti dvayor anūyājayor vibhaktī dadhāti
5.29.6	nottame
5.29.7	uccair uttamaṃ saṃpreṣyati
5.29.8	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
5.29.9	āgnivāruṇam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapati sarveṣām anunirvāpyāṇāṃ sthāne dvidevatyānāṃ vā
5.29.10	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate / saṃtiṣṭhate punarādheyam
5.29.11	yas tṛtīyam ādadhīta sa etān homāñ juhuyāl lekaḥ salekaḥ suleka iti
5.29.12	yad araṇyoḥ samārūḍho naśyet
5.29.13	yasya vobhāv anugatāv abhinimroced abhyudiyād vā punarādheyaṃ tasya prāyaścittiḥ
5.29.14	punarādheyam ity āśmarathyo 'gnyādheyam ity ālekhana ālekhanaḥ
6.1.1	agnihotraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
6.1.2	adhivṛkṣasūrya āviḥsūrye vā dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety upaveṣam ādāya gārhapatyam abhimantrayate sugārhapatya iti
6.1.3	athainaṃ bodhayaty udbudhyasvāgne prati jāgṛhy enam iṣṭāpūrte saṃsṛjethām ayaṃ ca / asmin sadhasthe adhy uttarasmin viśve devā yajamānaś ca sīdateti
6.1.4	uddharety eva sāyam āha yajamānaḥ / uddhareti prātaḥ
6.1.5	sahasraṃ tena kāmadugho 'varunddhe
6.1.6	vācā tvā hotrā prāṇenodgātrā cakṣuṣādhvaryuṇā manasā brahmaṇā śrotreṇāgnīdhaitais tvā pañcabhir daivyair ṛtvigbhir uddharāmīti gārhapatyād āhavanīyaṃ jvalantam uddharati
6.1.7	bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar uddhriyamāṇa uddhara pāpmano mā yad avidvān yac ca vidvāṃś cakāra / ahnā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmād ity uddhriyamāṇam abhimantrayate yajamānaḥ sāyam / rātryā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmād iti prātaḥ
6.1.8	agnipataye 'gnaye me viddhy agnipataye 'gnaye me mṛḍa / amṛtāhutim amṛtāyāṃ juhomy agniṃ pṛthivyām amṛtasya jityai / tayānantaṃ kāmam ahaṃ jayāni prajāpatir yaṃ prathamo jigāyāgnim agnau svāhā
6.2.1	agne samrāḍ ajaikapād āhavanīya divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ paryantarikṣāl lokaṃ vinda yajamānāya / pṛthivyās tvā mūrdhan sādayāmi yajñiye loke / yo no agne niṣṭyo yo 'niṣṭyo 'bhidāsatīdam ahaṃ taṃ tvayābhinidadhāmīti purastāt parikramyodaṅmukhaḥ pratyaṅmukho vā sāyam āyatane 'gniṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati / prāṅmukhaḥ prātaḥ
6.2.2	svayaṃ yajamāna idhmān āharati viśvadānīm ābharanto nātureṇa manasā / agne mā te prativeśā riṣāmety etayā
6.2.3	yad agne yāni kāni cety etābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ pratimantram agniṣu mahata idhmān ādadhāti
6.2.4	āhavanīye varṣiṣṭham
6.2.5	yathāhitās tenānupūrvyeṇāhavanīyād vā prakramya
6.2.6	tathāgnir ādheyo yathāhutir na vyaveyāt
6.2.7	nāntarāgnī saṃcarati
6.2.8	yadi pūrvo 'nugataḥ saṃcaryam
6.2.9	paścād dhi sa tarhi gataḥ
6.2.10	kāmaṃ hute saṃcaryam ity eke
6.2.11	naktam āhavanīyaṃ dhārayati
6.2.12	nityo gataśriyo dhriyate
6.2.13	nityaṃ gārhapatyam
6.2.14	tathānvāhāryapacanaṃ yadi mathitvāhito bhavati
6.2.15	yady āhāryo 'harahar enaṃ dakṣiṇata āharanti
6.2.16	upavasatha evainam āhareyur navāvasāna evainam āhareyur iti vājasaneyakam
6.3.1	parisamūhanenāgnīn alaṃkurvanti
6.3.2	purastād alaṃkārāḥ sāyam upariṣṭād alaṃkārāḥ prātaḥ
6.3.3	etad vā viparītam / ubhayato 'laṃkārāḥ sāyaṃ tathā prātar ity eke
6.3.4	agne gṛhapate śundhasveti gārhapatyam agne vahne śundhasveti dakṣiṇāgnim ange samrāṭ śundhasvety āhavanīyam agne sabhya śundhasveti sabhyam agne pariṣadya śundhasvety āvasathyam
6.3.5	udagagraiḥ prāgagraiś ca darbhais tṛṇair vāgnīn paristṛṇāty agnim agnī vā
6.3.6	khādiraḥ sruvo vaikaṅkaty agnihotrahavaṇī bāhumātry aratnimātrī vā
6.3.7	prasṛtākṛtir āryakṛtāgnihotrasthāly ūrdhvakapālācakravartā bhavati
6.3.8	dakṣiṇena vihāram agnihotrī tiṣṭhati tāṃ yajamāno 'bhimantrayata iḍāsi vratabhṛd ahaṃ nāv ubhayor vrataṃ cariṣyāmi surohiṇy ahaṃ nāv ubhayor vrataṃ cariṣyāmīḍa ehi mayi śrayasvera ehy adita ehi gaur ehi śraddha ehi satyena tvāhvayāmīti
6.3.9	atha vedideśam abhimṛśatīyam asi tasyās te 'gnir vatsaḥ sā me svargaṃ ca lokam amṛtaṃ ca dhukṣveti
6.3.10	pūṣāsīti dakṣiṇato vatsam upasṛjya prācīm āvṛtya dogdhy udīcīṃ prācīm udīcīṃ vā
6.3.11	na śūdro duhyāt
6.3.12	asato vā eṣa saṃbhūto yac chūdraḥ
6.3.13	duhyād vā
6.3.14	yad eva gārhapatye 'dhiśrayati pavayaty evainat
6.3.15	agnihotrasthālyā dohanena ca dogdhi
6.4.1	pūrvau duhyāj jyeṣṭhasya jyaiṣṭhineyasya yo vā gataśrīḥ syāt / aparau duhyāt kaniṣṭhasya kāniṣṭhaneyasya yo vānujāvaro yo vā bubhūṣet
6.4.2	na stanān saṃmṛśati
6.4.3	yathopalambhaṃ nitye kalpe dogdhi
6.4.4	pūrvavad upasṛṣṭāṃ duhyamānāṃ dhārāghoṣaṃ ca yajamāno 'numantrayate
6.4.5	astamite dogdhi
6.4.6	amnar astamite hotavyam
6.4.7	samudro vā eṣa yad ahorātras tasyaite gādhe tīrthe yat saṃdhī tasmāt samdhau hotavyam iti śailālibrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
6.4.8	nakṣatraṃ dṛṣṭvā pradoṣe niśāyāṃ vā sāyam
6.4.9	uṣasy upodayaṃ samayāviṣita udite vā prātaḥ
6.4.10	yad udite juhoty agniṣṭomaṃ tenāvarunddhe yan madhyaṃdine juhoty ukthyaṃ tenāvarunddhe yad aparāhṇe juhoti ṣoḍaśinaṃ tenāvarunddhe yat pūrvarātre juhoti prathamaṃ tena rātriparyāyam āpnoti yan madhyarātre juhoti madhyamaṃ tena rātriparyāyam āpnoti yad apararātre juhoti jaghanyaṃ tena rātriparyāyam āpnoti
6.4.11	sa na manyeta sarveṣv eteṣu kāleṣu hotavyam āpadi hutam ity eva pratīyād iti vijñāyate
6.4.12	yo homakālaḥ so 'ṅgānām
6.5.1	patnīvad asyāgnihotraṃ bhavati
6.5.2	sva āyatane patny upaviśati
6.5.3	apareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramyopaviśya yajamāno vidyud asi vidya me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upaimi mayi śraddhety apa ācāmati
6.5.4	ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmīti sāyaṃ pariṣiñcati / satyaṃ tvartena pariṣiñcāmīti prātaḥ / āhavanīyam agre 'tha gārhapatyam atha dakṣiṇāgnim api vā gārhapatyam āhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇāgniṃ yathā vāhitāḥ
6.5.5	yajñasya saṃtatir asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatim anusaṃtanomīti gārhapatayāt prakramya saṃtatām udakadhārāṃ srāvayaty āhavanīyāt
6.5.6	dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety upaveṣam ādāya bhūtakṛta sthāpoḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam apoḍhāḥ senā abhītvarīr iti gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān nirūhya vyantān gārhapatyena kṛtvā sagarā sthety abhimantrya japaty agnaya ādityaṃ gṛhṇāmy ahne rātrim iti sāyam / ādityāyāgniṃ gṛhṇāmi rātryā ahar iti prātaḥ
6.5.7	iḍāyāḥ padaṃ ghṛtavac carācaraṃ jātavedo havir idaṃ juṣasva / ye grāmyāḥ paśavo viśvarūpā virūpās teṣāṃ saptānām iha rantir astu / rāyaspoṣāya suprajāstvāya suvīryāyeti teṣv agnihotram adhiśrayati
6.6.1	reto vā agnihotram / na suśṛtaṃ kuryād retaḥ kūlayen no 'śṛtam antarevaiva syāt
6.6.2	samudantaṃ hotavyam
6.6.3	udantīkṛtya pratiṣicyam
6.6.4	apratiṣekyaṃ syāt tejaskāmasya brahmavarcasakāmasya pāpmānaṃ tustūrṣamāṇasyātho sarvebhyaḥ kāmebhyo 'tho yaḥ kāmayeta vīro ma ājāyeteti
6.6.5	amnar adhiśritaṃ vā
6.6.6	adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣāvekṣa iti tṛṇena jvalatāvekṣate
6.6.7	dohanasaṃkṣālanaṃ sruva ānīya haras te mā vinaiṣam iti tena pratiṣiñcaty apāṃ vā stokena
6.6.8	udbhava sthodahaṃ prajayā pra paśubhir bhūyāsaṃ haras te mā vigād udyan suvargo lokas triṣu lokeṣu rocayeti punar evāvekṣyāntaritaṃ rakṣo 'ntaritā arātayo 'pahatā vyṛddhir apahataṃ pāpaṃ karmāpahataṃ pāpasya pāpakṛtaḥ pāpaṃ karma yo naḥ pāpaṃ karma cikīrṣati pratyag enam ṛccheti triḥ paryagnikṛtvā gharmo 'si rāyaspoṣavanir ihorjaṃ dṛṃheti vartma kurvan prāg udvāsayaty udak prāgudag vā
6.6.9	na vartma karotīty eke
6.6.10	iha prajāṃ paśūn dṛṃheti trir bhūmau pratiṣṭhāpya subhūtakṛta stha pratyūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayaṃ pratyūḍhāḥ senā abhītvarīr iti gārhapatye 'ṅgārān pratyūhya
6.7.1	devasya tvā savituḥ prasava iti sruksruvam ādāya pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya ity āhavanīye gārhapatye vā pratitapyāriṣṭo yajamānaḥ patnī ceti saṃmṛśya hiraṇyayaṣṭir asy amṛtapalāśā sroto yajñānām ity agnihotrahavaṇīm abhimantryom unneṣyāmi havyaṃ devebhyaḥ pāpmano yajamānam iti sāyam āha / om unnayāmīti prātaḥ
6.7.2	havir devānām asi mṛtyor me 'bhayaṃ svasti me 'stv abhayaṃ me astv ity upāṃśūktvom unnayety uccair anujānāti / apacāre yajamānasya svayam ātmānam anujānīyāt
6.7.3	unnīyamāna ubau vācaṃ yacchata ā homāt
6.7.4	na cābhimīlate tiṣṭhati ca yajamānaḥ
6.7.5	unnīta upaviśati
6.7.6	catur unnayati
6.7.7	yaṃ kāmayeta putrāṇām ayam ṛdhnuyād iti taṃ prati pūrṇam unnayet
6.7.8	yadi kāmayeta jyeṣṭhato 'sya prajārdhukā syād iti pūrṇaṃ prathamam unnayet tata ūnataramūnataram / kaniṣṭhata ity etad viparītam / sarve samāvad vīryā iti samam
6.7.9	yathopalambhaṃ nitye kalpa unnayati
6.8.1	agnaye ca tvā pṛthivyai connayāmīti prathamaṃ vāyave ca tvāntarikṣāya ceti dvitīyaṃ sūryāya ca tvā dive ceti tṛtīyaṃ candramase ca tvā nakṣatrebhyaś ceti caturtham
6.8.2	adbhyaś ca tvauṣadībhyaś ceti pañcamaṃ jamadagnīnām
6.8.3	bhūr iḍā bhuva iḍā suvar iḍā karad iḍā pṛthag iḍeti vā pratimantram
6.8.4	paśūn me yacchety apareṇa gārhapatyam unnayanadeśe 'bhitarāṃ vā sādayitvā gārhapatye hastaṃ pratāpya saṃmṛśati sajūr devaiḥ sāyaṃyāvabhiḥ sāyaṃyāvāno devāḥ svasti saṃpārayantu paśubhiḥ saṃpṛcīya prajāṃ dṛṃheti sāyam / sajūr devaiḥ prātaryāvabhiḥ prātaryāvāṇo devāḥ svasti saṃpārayantu paśubhiḥ saṃpṛcīya prajāṃ dṛṃheti prātaḥ
6.8.5	daśahotrā cābhimṛśya pālāśīṃ samidhaṃ prādeśamātrīm upari dhārayan gārhapatyasya samayārcir harati
6.8.6	urv antarikṣaṃ vīhīty uddravati
6.8.7	uddravan daśahotāraṃ vyācaṣṭe
6.8.8	samaṃ prāṇair harati
6.8.9	svāhāganaye vaiśvānarāyeti madhyadeśe niyacchati
6.8.10	vātāya tvety udgṛhṇāti
6.8.11	upapreta saṃyatadhvaṃ māntargāta bhāginaṃ bhāgadheyāt saptarṣīṇāṃ sukṛtāṃ yatra lokas tatremaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānaṃ ca dhehy upapratnam upa bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar āyur me yacchety apareṇāhavanīyaṃ darbheṣu sādayati
6.9.1	yasyāgnāv uddhriyamāṇe hūyate vasuṣu hutaṃ bhavati / nihito dhūpāyañ chete rudreṣu / prathamam idhmam arcir ālabhata ādityeṣu / sarva eva sarvaśa idhma ādīpto bhavati viśveṣu deveṣu / nitarām arcir upāvaiti lohinīkeva bhavatīndre hutaṃ bhavati / aṅgārā bhavanti tebhyo 'ṅgārebhyo 'rcir udeti prajāpatāv eva / śaro 'ṅgārā adhyūhante tato nīlopakāśo 'rcir udeti brahmaṇi hutaṃ bhavati
6.9.2	yad aṅgāreṣu vyavaśānteṣu lelāyad vīva bhāti tad devānām āsyaṃ tasmāt tathā hotavyaṃ yathāsye 'pidadhāty evaṃ tad iti vijñāyate
6.9.3	vidyud asi vidya me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upaimīti hoṣyann apa upaspṛśya pālāśīṃ samidham ādadhāty ekāṃ dve tisro vā
6.9.4	eṣā te agne samid iti / hiraṇyayaṃ tvā vaṃśaṃ svargasya lokasya saṃkramaṇaṃ dadhāmīti dvitīyām / rajatāṃ tvā haritagarbhām agnijyotiṣam akṣitiṃ kāmadughāṃ svargyāṃ svargāya lokāya rātrim iṣṭakām upadadhe tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdeti sāyaṃ tṛtīyām / hariṇīṃ tvā rajatagarbhāṃ sūryajyotiṣam akṣitiṃ kāmadughāṃ svargyāṃ svargāya lokāyāhar iṣṭakām upadadha iti prātaḥ
6.10.1	samidham ādhāya prāṇyāpānya nimīlya vīkṣya hutvā dhyāyed yat kāmaḥ syāt
6.10.2	hutvā mahad abhivīkṣate
6.10.3	ādīptāyāṃ juhoti śyāvāyāṃ vā yadā vā samatītārcir lelāyatīva / dhūpāyatyāṃ grāmakāmasya jvalatyāṃ brahmavarcasakāmasyāṅgāreṣu tejaskāmasya
6.10.4	dvyaṅgule mūlāt samidham abhijuhoti
6.10.5	abhikrāmaṃ sāyaṃ juhoty avakrāmaṃ prātaḥ
6.10.6	ubhayatra vābhikrāmam
6.10.7	bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar iti hoṣyañ japati
6.10.8	agnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti sāyam agnihotraṃ juhoti / sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti prātaḥ
6.10.9	saṃsṛṣṭahomaṃ vāgnir jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti sāyaṃ / sūryo jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti prātaḥ
6.10.10	iṣe tveti sruṅmukhād avācīnaṃ sāyaṃ lepam avamārṣṭy ūrje tveti / ūrdhvaṃ prātaḥ
6.10.11	oṣadhībhyas tvauṣadhīr jinveti barhiṣi lepaṃ nimṛjya varco me yaccheti srucaṃ sādayitvāgne gṛhapate mā mā saṃtāpsīr ātmann amṛtam adhiṣi prajā jyotir adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣā pratīkṣa iti gārhapatyaṃ pratīkṣya bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar ity uttarām āhutiṃ pūrvārdhe samidhi juhoti tūṣṇīṃ vā
6.10.12	na samid abhihotavā ity eke
6.11.1	varṣīyasīm uttarām āhutiṃ hutvā bhūyo bhakṣāyāvaśinaṣṭi
6.11.2	yaṃ kāmayeta pāpīyān syād iti bhūyas tasya pūrvaṃ hutvottaraṃ kanīyo juhuyāt
6.11.3	hutvā srucam udgṛhya rudra mṛḍānārbhava mṛḍa dhūrta namas te astu paśupate trāyasvainam iti triḥ srucāgnim udañcam ativalgayati
6.11.4	pūrvaval lepam avamṛjya prācīnāvītī svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pitṝñ jinveti dakṣiṇena vediṃ bhūmyāṃ lepaṃ nimṛjya prajāṃ me yaccheti srucaṃ sādayitvā vṛṣṭir asi vṛśca me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upāgām iti hutvāpa upaspṛśyāntarvedi sruk / athāṅgulyāpādāya pūṣāsīti lepaṃ prāśnāty aśabdaṃ kurvann atihāya dataḥ
6.11.5	apa ācamyaivaṃ punaḥ prāśyācamya barhiṣopayamyodaṅṅ āvṛtyotsṛpya garbhebhyas tvā garbhān prīṇīhy āgneyaṃ haviḥ prajānanaṃ me astu daśavīraṃ sarvagaṇaṃ svastaye / ātmasani prajāsani paśusany abhayasani lokasani vṛṣṭisani / agniḥ prajāṃ bahulāṃ me karotv annaṃ payo reto asmāsu dhehi / rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharat svāhety udagdaṇḍayā prāgdaṇḍayā vā srucācāmati
6.12.1	sauryaṃ havir iti prātarmantraṃ saṃnamati
6.12.2	dviḥ srucaṃ nirlihyādbhiḥ pūrayitvocchiṣṭabhājo jinveti parācīnaṃ ninīyācamyāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ darbhair agnihotrahavaṇīṃ prakṣālayati
6.12.3	na māṃsadhautasya devā bhuñjata iti vijñāyate
6.12.4	adbhiḥ srucaṃ pūrayitvā sarpebhyas tvā sarpāñ jinveti pratidiśaṃ vyutsicya sarpān pipīlikā jinva sarpetarajanāñ jinva sarpadevajanāñ jinveti tisraḥ sruca utsicya caturthīṃ pūrayitvā pṛthivyām amṛtaṃ juhomi svāhety apareṇāhavanīyaṃ ninīya śeṣaṃ patnyā añjalau gṛhebhyas tvā gṛhāñ jinveti
6.12.5	yadi patnī nānuṣyād devānāṃ patnībhyo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi svāheti patnyāyatane ninayet
6.12.6	aparaṃ srucy ānīya vipruṣāṃ śāntir asīty unnayanadeśe ninīyāhavanīye srucaṃ pratāpya hasto 'vadheyo hasto vā pratāpya srucy avadheyaḥ
6.12.7	tayodag uddiśati saptarṣibhyas tvā saptarṣīñ jinveti
6.13.1	agne gṛhapate pariṣadya juṣasva svāheti sruveṇa gārhapatye juhoty ekāṃ dve tisraś catasro vā
6.13.2	agnaye gṛhapataye rayipataye puṣṭipataye kāmāyānnādyāya svāhety etām eke samāmananti
6.13.3	samabhyuccayavad eke
6.13.4	agne 'dābhya pariṣadya juṣasva svāheti sruveṇānvāhāryapacane juhoty ekāṃ dve tisraś catasro vā
6.13.5	annapate annasya no dehīti dvitīyām
6.13.6	aprāśya vāparayor juhuyāt
6.13.7	āhavanīye homo nāparayoḥ
6.13.8	yad āhavanīye hutvāparayor juhuyād yathā svargāl lokāt pratyavarohet tādṛk tad iti vijñāyate
6.13.9	sarve vā ete homārthā ādhīyante / catasro gārhapatye juhoti catasro 'nvāhāryapacane dve āhavanīye / daśa saṃpadyante / daśākṣarā virāḍ virājā yajñaḥ saṃmita iti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
6.13.10	dīdihi dīdidāsi dīdāyety eṣo 'gnyupasamindhana āmnātaḥ
6.13.11	dīdihi dīdidāsi dīdāya dīdyāsaṃ dīdyasveti vā pratimantram
6.13.12	yathāhitās tenānupūrvyeṇāhavanīyād vā prakramya
6.13.13	antarvedy apo ninīya
6.14.1	pūrvavad agnīn pariṣiñcati / na dhārām
6.14.2	apiprer agne svāṃ tanvam ayāḍ dyāvāpṛthivī ūrjam asmāsu dhehīty agnihotrasthālyāṃ tṛṇam aṅktvānupraharati
6.14.3	sā hy agnihotrasya saṃsthitiḥ
6.14.4	na barhir anupraharet / asaṃsthito vā eṣa yajño yad agnihotram ity uktam
6.14.5	agnihotrasthālīṃ prakṣālyākṣitam akṣityai juhomi svāhety unnayanadeśe ninayati / antarvedi vā
6.14.6	vṛṣṭir asi vṛśca me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upāgām apsu śraddhety apa ācamya yajamāno 'ntarvedi mārjayate 'nnādāḥ sthānnādo bhūyāsaṃ yaśaḥ stha yaśasvī bhūyāsaṃ śraddhā stha śraddhiṣīyeti
6.14.7	āpo ha śleṣma prathamaṃ saṃbabhūva yena dhṛto varuṇo yena mitraḥ / yenendraṃ devā abhyaṣiñcanta rājyāya tenāhaṃ mām abhiṣiñcāmi varcasa iti śirasy apa ānayate
6.14.8	dvayoḥ payasā paśukāmasya juhuyāt
6.14.9	agnihotrasthālyā pūrvāṃ dogdhi / dohanenottarām
6.14.10	adhiśritya pūrvam uttaram ānayati
6.14.11	yasya rudraḥ paśūñ chamāyetaitayaivāvṛtā dvayoḥ payasā sāyaṃprātar juhuyāt
6.14.12	tac ced atihanyāt sajūr jātavedo diva ā pṛthivyā asya haviṣo ghṛtasya vīhi svāheti sāyaṃprātar ājyena juhuyāt
6.14.13	anāramaty agne duḥśīrtatano juṣasva svāheti dvādaśāham ājyena hutvā tata ūrdhvaṃ na sūrkṣet
6.15.1	payasā paśukāmasya juhuyād dadhnendriyakāmasya yavāgvā grāmakāmasyaudanenānnādyakāmasya taṇḍulair ojaskāmasya / balakāmasyety eke / māṃsena yaśaskāmasya somena brahmavarcasakāmasyājyena tejaskāmasya
6.15.2	pratiṣekaṃ yavāgūṃ śrapayati
6.15.3	śṛtāṃ yajuṣā pratiṣiñcati
6.15.4	evaṃ māṃsam
6.15.5	nājyaṃ pratiṣiñcati haras te mā vinaiṣam iti / dve darbhāgre pratyasyaty ekaṃ vā
6.15.6	na dadhy adhiśrayati / śṛtaṃ hi tan na pratiṣiñcati pratiṣiktaṃ hi tad ātañcaneneti vijñāyate
6.15.7	evaṃ taṇḍulān odanaṃ somaṃ ca
6.15.8	ājyena taṇḍulair odanena somena vā juhuyād yasyāpratiṣekyaṃ syāt
6.15.9	ājyena tejaskāmaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ juhuyād dvādaśāhaṃ vā
6.15.10	na rājanyasya juhuyāt
6.15.11	homakāle gṛhebhyo brāhmaṇāyānnaṃ prahiṇuyāt teno haivāsya hutaṃ bhavati
6.15.12	nityam agnyupasthānaṃ vācayitavyaḥ
6.15.13	yo vā somayājī satyavādī tasya juhuyāt
6.15.14	aharahar yajamānaḥ svayam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt
6.15.15	parvaṇi vā
6.15.16	brahmacārī vā juhuyād brahmaṇā hi sa parikrīto bhavati / kṣīrahotā vā juhuyād dhanena hi sa parikrīto bhavatīti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇam
6.16.1	agnyupasthānaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
6.16.2	upatiṣṭhata iti codyamāna āhavanīyam evopatiṣṭheta / vacanād anyam
6.16.3	uttarām āhutim upotthāya kavātiryaṅṅ ivopatiṣṭheta
6.16.4	upaprayanto adhvaram iti ṣaḍbhiḥ
6.16.5	agnīṣomāv imaṃ su ma iti saptamyā pūrvapakṣe / aindrāgnyā saptamyāparapakṣe
6.16.6	dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam ity ubhayatrāṣṭamyā
6.16.7	mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv iti catasraḥ purastād agnīṣomīyāyāḥ pūrvapakṣe / tathaindrāgnyā aparapakṣe
6.16.8	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti ṣaḍbhiḥ saṃvatsaresaṃvatsare sadā vā
6.16.9	pavamānahavīṃṣi vā saṃvatsaresaṃvasare nirvaped etāsāṃ sthāne
6.16.10	āyurdā agna iti siddham ā citrāvasoḥ
6.16.11	triś citrāvasunā sāyam upatiṣṭhate / trir arvāg vasunā prātar arvāg vaso svasti te pāram aśīya
6.16.12	indhānās tvā śataṃ himā ity upasthāyendhānās tvā śataṃ himāḥ / agneḥ samid asy abhiśastyā mā pāhi somasya samid asi paraspā ma edhi yamasya samid asi mṛtyor mā pāhīti catasraḥ samidha ekaikasminn ādhāya saṃ tvam agne sūryasya varcasāgathā ity anuvākaśeṣeṇopasthāya vayaṃ soma vrate tava manas tanūṣu bibhrataḥ prajāvanto aśīmahīti mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe
6.17.1	saṃpaśyāmi prajā aham iti gṛhān prekṣate
6.17.2	ambhaḥ sthāmbho vo bhakṣīyeti goṣṭham upatiṣṭhate
6.17.3	revatī ramadhvam ity antarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japati
6.17.4	saṃhitāsi viśvarūpīr iti vatsam abhimṛśati
6.17.5	saṃhitāsi viśvarūpeti vatsām
6.17.6	bhuvanam asi sahasrapoṣaṃ puṣeti vā vatsam
6.17.7	upa tvāgne divediva iti tisṛbhir gāyatrībhir gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate 'gne tvaṃ no antama iti catasṛbhiś ca dvipadābhiḥ
6.17.8	sa no bodhi śrudhī havam uruṣyā ṇo aghāyataḥ samasmād ity eṣā caturthī bhavati
6.17.9	ūrjā vaḥ paśyāmy ūrjā mā paśyateti gṛhān prekṣate paśūn vā
6.17.10	mahi trīṇām avo 'stu dyukṣaṃ mitrasyāryamṇaḥ / durādharṣaṃ varuṇasya // nahi teṣām amā cana nādhvasu vāraṇeṣvā / īśe ripur aghaśaṃsaḥ // te hi putrāso aditeś chardir yacchanty ajasram / vi dāśuṣe vāryāṇīti prājāpatyena tṛcenopatiṣṭhate
6.17.11	yaṃ kāmayeta svasti punar āgacched iti tam etābhir anvīkṣeta / svasty eva punar āgacchatīty ayajñasaṃyuktaḥ kalpaḥ
6.17.12	mā naḥ śaṃso araruṣo dhūrtiḥ praṇaṅ martyasya / rakṣā ṇo brahmaṇaspate // yo revān yo amīvahā vasuvit puṣṭivardhanaḥ / sa naḥ siṣaktu yas turaḥ // pari te dūḍabho ratho 'smāṁ aśnotu viśvataḥ / yena rakṣasi dāśuṣaḥ
6.18.1	tat savitur vareṇyaṃ somānaṃ svaraṇaṃ mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ pra sa mitra kadā cana starīr asi kadā cana prayucchasi pari tvāgne puraṃ vayam ity upasthāya
6.18.2	nimṛdo 'si ny ahaṃ taṃ mṛdyāsaṃ yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇasya padaḥ pārṣṇyā nimṛdnīyād yadi pāpīyasā spardheta / prabhūr asi prāhaṃ tam abhibhūyāsaṃ yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇataḥ pado nigṛhṇīyād yadi sadṛśena / abhibhūr asy abhy ahaṃ taṃ bhūyāsaṃ yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti prapadena yadi śreyasā
6.18.3	pūṣā mā paśupāḥ pātu pūṣā mā pathipāḥ pātu pūṣā mādhipāḥ pātu pūṣā mādhipatiḥ pātv iti lokān upasthāya prācī dig agnir devatāgniṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati / dakṣiṇā dig indro devatendraṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati / pratīcī dik somo devatā somaṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati / udīcī diṅ mitrāvaruṇau devatā mitrāvaruṇau sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati / ūrdhvā dig bṛhaspatir devatā bṛhaspatiṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati / iyaṃ dig aditir devatāditiṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsatīti yathāliṅgaṃ diśa upasthāya
6.19.1	agnīn upasamādhāya dharmo mā dharmaṇaḥ pātu vidharmo mā vidharmaṇaḥ pātv āyuś ca prāyuś ca cakṣuś ca vicakṣuś ca prāṅ cāvāṅ coruga urugasya te vācā vayaṃ saṃ bhaktena gamemahīty upasthāyāgna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity āgnipāvamānībhyāṃ gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate
6.19.2	agne gṛhapata iti ca / putrasya nāma gṛhṇāti tām āśiṣam āśāse tantava ity ajātasya / amuṣmā iti jātasya
6.19.3	yat kiṃcāgnihotrī kāmayeta tad agnīn yāceta / upainaṃ tan namatīti vijñāyate
6.19.4	upastheyo 'gnī3r nopastheyā3 ity uktam
6.19.5	naktam upatiṣṭhate na prātaḥ
6.19.6	na prātar agnim upa canāvarohen na prātar āhitāgniś cana manyeteti vājasaneyakam
6.19.7	bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ suprajāḥ prajayā bhūyāsaṃ suvīro vīraiḥ suvarcā varcasā supoṣaḥ poṣair ity evopatiṣṭheteti vājasaneyakam / bhartuṃ vaḥ śakeyaṃ śraddhā me mā vyāgād iti vā
6.19.8	vātsapreṇaiva sāyaṃprātar upatiṣṭhetety eke
6.19.9	goṣūktenāśvasūktena vā
6.20.1	prātaravanekena prātar upastheyaḥ
6.20.2	adhiśrita unnīyamāne vā mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv iti catasro japitvāpāṃ pate yo 'pāṃ bhāgaḥ sa ta eṣa pratiṣiktā arātayaḥ pratiṣiktā arātayaḥ pratiṣiktā arātaya iti trir bhūmau pratiṣicya kālāya vāṃ jaitriyāya vām audbhettriyāya vām avanenije sukṛtāya vām / idam ahaṃ duradmanyāṃ niṣplāvayāmi bhrātṛvyāṇāṃ sapatnānām ahaṃ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ / apāṃ maitrād ivodakam iti hastau prakṣālya śriyaṃ dhātar mayi dhehi śriyo mādhipatiṃ kuru / viśām īśāno maghavendro mā yaśasā nayad iti japitvātharvyuṣṭā devajūtā vīḍu chapathajambhanīḥ / āpo malam iva prāṇijann asmatsu śapathāṃ adhītyācamyendriyāvatīm adyāhaṃ vācam udyāsaṃ dīrghaprāṇo 'cchinno 'dabdho gopāḥ / ajasraṃ daivyaṃ jyotiḥ sauparṇaṃ cakṣuḥ suśrutau karṇau devaśrutau karṇau keśā barhiḥ śikhā prastaro yathāsthānaṃ kalpayadhvaṃ śaṃ hṛdayāyādo mā mā hāsiṣṭeti yathāliṅgam aṅgāni saṃmṛśya
6.21.1	varco 'si varco mayi dhehy āyukṛd āyuḥpatnī svadhā vo goptryo me stha gopāyata mā rakṣata mātmasado me stha / mā naḥ kaścit praghān mā prameṣmahy upa pratnam upa bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar āyur me yacchateti sarvān upasthāyottareṇānuvākenāhavanīyaṃ gharmā jaṭharānnādaṃ mām adyāsmiñ jane kurutam annādo 'ham adyāsmiñ jane bhūyāsam anannādaḥ sa yo 'smān dveṣṭi / kavī mātariśvānā paśumantaṃ mām adyāsmiñ jane kurutaṃ paśumān aham adyāsmiñ jane bhūyāsam apaśuḥ sa yo 'smān dveṣṭi / yamāṅgirasā yaśasvinaṃ mām adyāsmiñ jane kurutaṃ yaśasvy aham adyāsmiñ jane bhūyāsam ayaśāḥ sa yo 'smān dveṣṭi // agne yo no anti śapati yaś ca dūre samāno agne araṇo durasyuḥ / vaiśvānareṇa sayujā sajoṣās taṃ pratyañcaṃ saṃdaha jātavedaḥ // agne yat te 'rcis tena taṃ pratyarca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te śocis tena taṃ pratiśoca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te tapas tena taṃ pratitapa yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te haras tena taṃ pratihara yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te tejas tena taṃ pratititigdhi yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
6.22.1	agne rucāṃ pate namas te ruce rucaṃ mayi dhehi / arvāgvaso svasti te pāram aśīyārvāgvaso svasti te pāram aśīyārvāgvaso svasti te pāram aśīya / tantur asi tato mā cchitthā asau svasti te 'stv asau svasti te 'stv asau svasti te 'stv iti putrāṇāṃ nāmāni gṛhṇāti tristrir ekaikasya / svasti vo 'stu ye mām anustha ṣaṇ morvīr aṃhasas pāntu dyauś ca pṛthivī cāpaś cauṣadhayaś cork ca sūnṛtā ca / yathā ha tyad vasavo gauryaṃ citpadi ṣitāmamuñcatā yajatrāḥ / evo ṣvasmanmuñcatā vyaṃhaḥ pra tāry agne prataraṃ na āyuḥ // vayaḥ suparṇā upa sedur indraṃ priyamedhā ṛṣayo nādhamānāḥ / apa dhvāntam ūrṇuhi pūrdhi cakṣur mumugdhy asmān nidhayeva baddhān // agna āyūṃṣi pavase dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam iti dve mamāgne varco vihaviṣv astv iti catasro 'gnīṣomāv imaṃ su ma ity eṣā / tat savitur vṛṇīmahe vayaṃ devasya bhojanam / śreṣṭhaṃ sarvadhātamaṃ turaṃ bhagasya dhīmahi // asya hi svayaśastaraṃ savituḥ kaccana priyam / na minanti svarājyam
6.23.1	adyā no deva savitaḥ prajāvatsāvīḥ saubhagaṃ / parā duḥṣvapniyaṃ suva // viśvāni deva savitar duritāni parā suva / yad bhadraṃ tan ma ā suva // anāgaso aditaye vayaṃ devasya savituḥ save / viśvā vāmāni dhīmahi // sa hi ratnāni daśuṣe suvāti savitā bhagaḥ / taṃ citraṃ bhāgam īmahe // vāmam adya savitar vāmam u śvo divedive vāmam asmabhyaṃ sāvīḥ saubhagam / vāmasya hi kṣayasya deva bhūrer ayā dhiyā vāmabhājaḥ syāma // dīkṣā tapo manaso mātariśvā bṛhaspatir vāco asyāḥ sa yoniḥ / vedāṃsi vidyā mayi santu cāravo 'gnīṣomā yaśo asmāsu dhattam // agnir yena virājati somo yena virājati sūryo yena virājati virāḍ yena virājati tenāhaṃ viśvatas pari virājyāsam ihaikavṛd ity upasthāyāgnes tṛṇāny apacinoti / tejasvīha brahmavarcasī bhavatīti vijñāyate
6.24.1	pravatsyan saṃpreṣyaty agnīn samādhehīti
6.24.2	jvalata upatiṣṭhate
6.24.3	paśūn naḥ śaṃsya pāhi tān no gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity āhavanīyam / prajāṃ no narya pāhi tāṃ no gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād iti gārhapatyam / annaṃ no budhnya pāhi tan no gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity anvāhāryapacanam
6.24.4	antarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japatīmān no mitrāvaruṇā gṛhān gopāyataṃ yuvam / avinaṣṭān avihṛtān pūṣainān abhirakṣatv āsmākaṃ punarāgamād iti
6.24.5	pūrvavad virāṭkramair upasthāyāśitvā pravasatham eṣyann āhāgnīn samādhehīti
6.24.6	jvalata upatiṣṭhate prajāṃ me narya pāhi tāṃ me gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād iti gārhapatyam / annaṃ me budhnya pāhi tan me gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity anvāhāryapacanam / paśūn me śaṃsya pāhi tān me gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity āhavanīyam
6.24.7	mama nāma prathamaṃ jātaveda iti ca
6.24.8	vāgyato 'bhipravrajati mā pragāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñād indra sominaḥ / māntaḥsthur no arātayaḥ / ud asmāṁ uttarān nayāgne ghṛtenāhuta / rāyaspoṣeṇa saṃsṛja prajayā ca bahūn kṛdhīti
6.24.9	ārād agnibhyo vācaṃ visṛjate
6.25.1	pravasan kāle vihāram abhimukho 'gnyupasthānaṃ japati
6.25.2	ihaiva san tatra sato vo agnayaḥ prāṇena vācā manasā bibharmi / tiro mā santam āyur mā prahāsīj jyotiṣā vo vaiśvānareṇopatiṣṭha iti yady anupasthāya pravased etayaivopatiṣṭhate
6.25.3	samidhaḥ kṛtvā pratyeti
6.25.4	yathā ha vā itaṃ pitaraṃ proṣivāṃsaṃ putrāḥ pratyādhāvanty evaṃ ha vā etam agnayaḥ pratyādhāvanti / sa śakalān dārūṇi vāharann eti yathaiva tat putrebhya āharann eti / tādṛk tad iti vijñāyate
6.25.5	ārād agnibhyo vācaṃ yacchati
6.25.6	yady enaṃ rājā pitācāryo vāntareṇāgnīn syāc chadir darśe nainam ādriyeta
6.25.7	viśvadānīm ābharanto 'nātureṇa manasā / agne mā te prativeśā riṣāma // namas te astu mīḍhuṣe namas ta upasadvane / agne śumbhasva tanvaḥ saṃ mā rayyā sṛjety abhyaiti
6.25.8	agnīn samādhehīti
6.25.9	jvalata upatiṣṭhate
6.25.10	paśūn naḥ śaṃsyājūgupas tān naḥ punar dehīty āhavanīyam abhiprānyāgne sahasrākṣa śatamūrdhañ chataṃ te prāṇāḥ sahasram apānāḥ / tvaṃ sāhasrasya rāya īśiṣe sahasradhārasya payasaḥ / tasya no rāsva tasya te bhakṣīya tasya te vayaṃ bhūyiṣṭhabhājo bhūyāsmety āhavanīyam
6.26.1	prajāṃ no naryājūgupas tāṃ naḥ punar dehīti gārhapatyam abhiprāṇyāgne gṛhapate sugṛhapatir ahaṃ tvayā gṛhapatinā bhṛyāsaṃ sugṛhapatir mayā tvaṃ gṛhapatinā bhūyāḥ / śataṃ himā dvā yū rādhāṃsīt saṃpṛñcānāv asaṃpṛñcānau tanva iti gārhapatyam
6.26.2	annaṃ no budhnyājūgupas tan naḥ punar dehīty anvāhāryapacanam abhiprāṇyāntarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japati yathā pravatsyad upasthāne
6.26.3	ajūgupatam abhyarākṣīd iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
6.26.4	mama nāma tava ca jātaveda iti catasṛbhir āhavanīyam
6.26.5	prajāṃ me naryājūgupas tāṃ me punar dehīti gārhapatyam abhyapānyānnaṃ me budhnyājūgupas tan me punar dehīty anvāhāryapacanam abhyapānya paśūn me śaṃsyājūgupas tān me punar dehīty āhavanīyam abhyapānya pūrvavad virāṭkramair upatiṣṭhate / ajūgupa iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
6.26.6	agnyupasthānavad atra samidho diśāṃ copasthānam
6.26.7	navamīṃ ced atipravasen mitro janān yātayati prajānann iti maitryopasthāya mano jyotir juṣatām ity āhutiṃ juhuyāt
6.26.8	samidha āhutim upasthānam ity evam anupūrvāṇy eke samāmananti
6.27.1	tad āhur nāgnir upastheyaḥ kaḥ śreyāṃsaṃ viṣuptaṃ bodhayiṣyatīti / abhayaṃkarābhayaṃ me kuru svasti me 'stv abhayaṃ me astv ity eva brūyāt / pravatsyad upasthānam āgatopasthānaṃ cādhikṛtya vājasaneyinaḥ samāmananti
6.27.2	namo vo 'stu pravatsyāmi namo vo 'stu prāvātsyam iti bahvṛcāḥ
6.27.3	gṛhā mā bibhīta mā vepiḍhvam ūrjaṃ bibhrata emasi / ūrjaṃ bibhrad vaḥ suvaniḥ sumedhā gṛhān aimi manasā modamanaḥ // yeṣām adhyeti pravasan yeṣu saumanaso bahuḥ / gṛhān upahvayāmahe te no jānantu jānataḥ // upahūtā bhūridhanāḥ sakhāyaḥ svādusaṃmudaḥ / ariṣṭāḥ sarvapūruṣā gṛhā naḥ santu sarvadā // upahūtā iha gāva upahūtā ajāvayaḥ / atho annasya kīlāla upahūto gṛheṣu na iti gṛhān abhyeti
6.27.4	kṣemāya vaḥ śāntyai prapadye śivaṃ śagmaṃ śaṃyoḥ śaṃyor iti praviśati
6.27.5	ūrjaṃ bibhrad vaḥ sumanāḥ sumedhā gṛhān āgāṃ manasā modamānaḥ / irāṃ vahanto ghṛtam ukṣamāṇās teṣv ahaṃ sumanāḥ saṃviśāmīti praviśya japati / saṃviśan vā
6.28.1	sagṛhaḥ prayāsyan vāstoṣpatīyaṃ juhoti
6.28.2	ahute yāneṣu bhaṇḍāny āropayanti
6.28.3	na hīnam anvāhareyuḥ
6.28.4	yady anovāhyaṃ syāt pūrvaṃ taṃ pravaheyur apa voddhareyuḥ
6.28.5	yatra saṃhitā rātrīr vaset pañca sapta nava daśa vā tat prayāsyañ juhuyāt
6.28.6	navarātravastau vā punar etyaikām uṣitvā prayāsyañ juhuyāt
6.28.7	dakṣiṇo yukto bhavati savyo 'yuktaḥ / api vāgniṣṭhasya dakṣiṇo yuktaḥ savyasya yoktraṃ parihṛtam / sarveṣu vā yukteṣu
6.28.8	vāstoṣpata ity anudrutyottarayā gārhapatye hutvāvakṣāṇāni saṃprakṣāpya pṛthag araṇīṣv agnīn samāropayate ye dhāryante
6.28.9	upary agnāv araṇī dhārayañ japaty ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti
6.28.10	api vā yajamāna evātman samāropayate
6.28.11	yā te agne yajñiyā tanūs tayehy ārohātmātmānam acchā vasūni kṛṇvann asme naryā purūṇi / yajño bhūtvā yajñam āsīda svāṃ yoniṃ jātavedo bhuva ājāyamānaḥ sa kṣaya ehīti hastaṃ pratāpya mukhāyāharate
6.28.12	vāsa upāvaroha jātavedaḥ punas tvaṃ devebhyo havyaṃ vaha naḥ prajānan / āyuḥ prajāṃ rayim asmāsu dhehy ajasro dīdihi no duroṇa iti laukike 'gnāv upāvarohayati
6.28.13	araṇyor vopāvarohya manthet
6.28.14	yad araṇyoḥ samārūḍhaḥ syān nirvartamāna etaṃ mantraṃ japet
6.29.1	idaṃ śreyo 'vasānaṃ yad āgāṃ syone me dyāvāpṛthivī abhūtām / anamīvāḥ pradiśaḥ santu mahyam / gomad dhanavad aśvavat puruṣavad dhiraṇyavat suvīravat svāhety avasite juhoti
6.29.2	nāniṣṭvāgrayaṇenāhitāgnir navasyāśnīyāt
6.29.3	vrīhīṇāṃ yavānāṃ śyāmākānam ity agrapākasya yajeta
6.29.4	amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā
6.29.5	āmāvāsyaṃ tantram
6.29.6	saptadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ
6.29.7	nirvapaṇakāla āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati purāṇānāṃ vrīhīṇām
6.29.8	yathā dāntenādāntaṃ saṃyunakti tādṛk tad iti vijñāyate
6.29.9	yena yajñenertset kuryād eva tatrāgneyam aṣṭākapālam iti vijñāyate
6.29.10	navānām itarāṇy aindrāgnaṃ dvādaśakapālam āgnendraṃ vā vaiśvadevaṃ payasi caruṃ saumyaṃ śyāmākaṃ caruṃ dyāvāpṛthivyam ekakapālam
6.29.11	purastāt saumyād dyāvāpṛthivyam eke samāmananti
6.29.12	niruptaṃ havirupasannam aprokṣitaṃ bhavati / atha pañcājyānīr juhoti śatāyudhāya śatavīryāyeti
6.29.13	purastād vā sviṣṭakṛtaḥ
6.29.14	prokṣādi karma pratipadyate
6.29.15	ekam ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ pratibījaṃ vā
6.29.16	sarveṣu haviṣkṛd avahananamantraḥ
6.29.17	tuṣopavapanam
6.29.18	uttamam opya vācaṃ visṛjate
6.29.19	eṣo 'nyeṣāṃ nānābījānāṃ samavetānāṃ kalpaḥ
6.29.20	alaṃkaraṇakāla ājyenaikakapālam abhipūrayati
6.29.21	āviḥpṛṣṭhaṃ vā kṛtvāsādayati
6.29.22	pracaraṇakāla uddhṛtya barhiṣadaṃ kṛtvā juhvām upastīryādhāyāśayam anvānīyābhighāryopāṃśu pracarati
6.30.1	sarvahutam aparyāvartayann ṛjuṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ na hastena juhuyāt
6.30.2	yadi hutaḥ paryāvarteta sruco 'greṇa kalpayet
6.30.3	na pāṇinā
6.30.4	vare datte kalpayitavyaḥ
6.30.5	ādhāyābhighārya punarhotavya ity eke

6.30.7	ye prācīnam ekāṣṭakāyā vatsā jāyante teṣāṃ prathamajaṃ dadāti / vāsaḥ śyāmāke
6.30.8	bhadrānnaḥ śreyaḥ samanaiṣṭa devā iti yajamānabhāgaṃ prāśnāti

6.30.10	agniḥ prathāmaḥ prāśnātu sa hi veda yathā haviḥ / śivā asmabhyam oṣadhīḥ kṛṇotu viśvacarṣaṇir iti śyāmākānām
6.30.11	siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate

6.30.13	api vāmāvāsyāṃ paurṇamāsīṃ vā navair yajeta
6.30.14	api vāgnihotrīṃ vrīhistambaṃ yavastambaṃ vā grāsayitvā tasyāḥ payasā sāyaṃprātar juhuyāt
6.30.15	api vā navānāṃ yavāgvā sāyaṃprātar juhuyāt
6.30.16	api vā navānāṃ gārhapatye sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvāhavanīye juhuyād āgrayaṇadevatābhyaḥ sviṣṭakṛccaturthābhyaḥ
6.30.17	api vā navānāṃ catuḥśarāvam odanaṃ paktvā caturo brāhmaṇān bhojayet
6.30.18	evaṃ yavair yajeta
6.30.19	tatrāgneyaśyāmākau na bhavataḥ
6.30.20	ya ūrdhvam ekāṣṭakāyā vatsā jāyante teṣāṃ prathamajaṃ dadāti // etam u tyaṃ madhunā saṃyutaṃ yavaṃ sarasvatyā adhi manāv acarkṛṣuḥ indra āsīt sīrapatiḥ śatakratuḥ kīnāśā āsan marutaḥ sudānava iti yajamānabhāgaṃ prāśnāti // sarveṣāṃ vā bhakṣāṇāṃ mantravatāṃ pratyāmnāyaḥ syāt

6.31.2	tasyāḥ saptadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ
6.31.3	sadvantāv ājyabhāgau / virājau saṃyājaye
6.31.4	tvam agne saprathā asi juṣṭo hotā vareṇyaḥ / tvayā yajñaṃ vitanvate / soma yās te mayobhuva iti sadvantau / preddho agna imo agna iti virājau
6.31.5	vāso dakṣiṇā dadhimantho madhumantho madhuparko madhugluntho babhrur vā piṅgalaḥ

7.4.1	uttarasmād vedyaṃsād udakprakrame cātvālaḥ
7.4.2	tam uttaravedivat tūṣṇīṃ śamyayā parimitya devasya tvā savituḥ prasava ity abhrim ādāya parilikhitaṃ rakṣaḥ parilikhitā arātaya iti triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parilikhya tūṣṇīṃ jānudaghnaṃ trivitastaṃ vā khātvottaravedyarthān pāṃsūn harati vider iti
7.4.3	siṃhīr asīty uttaravedyāṃ nivapati
7.4.4	etenaiva yo dvitīyasyām iti dvitīyaṃ yas tṛtīyasyām iti tṛtīyam
7.4.5	tūṣṇīṃ caturthaṃ hṛtvoru prathasvoru te yajñapatiḥ prathatām iti prathayitvā dhruvāsīti śamyayā saṃhatya devebhyaḥ kalpasvety abhimantrya devebhyaḥ śundhasvety adbhir avokṣya devebhyaḥ śumbhasveti sikatābhir avakīrya prokṣaṇīśeṣam uttarata uttaravedyai ninīyāpo ripraṃ nirvahateti sphyenodīcīm ekasphyāṃ niḥsārya vibhrāḍ bṛhat pibatu somyaṃ madhv āyur dadhad yajñapatāv avihrutam / vātajūto yo abhirakṣati tmanā prajāḥ piparti bahudhā virājatīty uttaravedyā antān kalpayati

7.5.1	athāsyā madhye prādeśamātrīṃ gopadamātrīm aśvaśaphamātrīṃ vottaranābhiṃ catuḥsraktiṃ kṛtvā catuḥśikhaṇḍe yuvatī kanīne ghṛtapratīke bhuvanasya madhye / tayor devā adhisaṃvasanta uttame nāka iha mādayantām ity ubhe abhimantryendraghoṣas tvā vasubhiḥ purastāt pātv ity etair yathāliṅgam uttaravediṃ prokṣati

7.11.1	un nambhaya pṛthivīm ity adbhiḥ pariṣiñcati
