11.9.11	yūpavad audumbaryā avaṭasaṃskāraḥ śakalavarjam
11.9.12	agreṇāvaṭaṃ prācīṃ nidhāya tūṣṇīṃ prakṣālyāthaināṃ yavamatībhiḥ prokṣati / dive tvety agram / antarikṣāya tveti madhyam / pṛthivyai tveti mūlam
11.9.13	ud divaṃ stabhānānatarikṣaṃ pṛṇeti prācīnakarṇāṃ sahodgātrocchrayati / ucchrayasva vanaspate sajūr devena barhiṣeti vā
11.10.1	dyutānas tvā māruto minotv iti prācīnakarṇāṃ sahodgātrā minoti
11.10.2	ūrdhvaṃ nikhātād yajamānasaṃmitā
11.10.3	paryūhaṇaparidṛṃhaṇapariṣecanāni yūpavat
11.10.4	tasyā viśākhe hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī āpṛṇethām iti sruveṇa hiraṇye juhvad āntam audumbarīm anvavasrāvayati
11.10.5	eṣā sadasaḥ sthūṇānāṃ varṣiṣṭhā
11.10.6	nābhidaghnyaḥ paryantīyāḥ
11.10.7	nīcaiḥ sado minuyād vṛṣṭikāmasya / uccair avṛṣṭikāmasyety eke
11.10.8	udañcaḥ prācaś ca vaṃśān atyādhāyaindram asīti teṣu madhyamāni trīni chadīṃṣy adhyūhati
11.10.9	viśvajanasya chāyeti trīṇi dakṣiṇāni / indrasya sado 'sīti trīṇy uttarāṇi
11.10.10	dakṣiṇāny uttarāṇi caudumbarīm abhyagrāṇi bhavanti
11.10.11	dakṣiṇāny uttarāṇi karotīti vijñāyate
11.10.12	navacchadīti kāmyāni
11.10.13	navāgniṣṭome / pañcadaśokthye / ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśini / saptadaśa vājapeye 'tirātre ca / ekaviṃśatiḥ sattrāhīnānām
11.10.14	antarvartāḥ pariśrayaṇaṃ sāṃkāśinaṃ dvārāv iti havirdhānavat
11.10.15	indrasya syūr asīti sīvyati / indrasya dhruvam asīti prajñātaṃ granthiṃ kṛtvaindram asīndrāya tveti saṃmitam abhimṛśati
11.10.16	nādhvaryuḥ pratyaṅ sado 'tīyāt / dhiṣṇiyān hotāraṃ vā
11.10.17	yady atīyād aindriyarcā saṃcaret // ā ghā ye agnim indhate stṛṇanti barhir ānuṣak / yeṣām indro yuvā sakheti staraṇīm etām eke samāmananti
11.10.18	kṣaitrapatyā vā saṃcaret
11.10.19	uparavakarmaike pūrvaṃ samāmananti / sadaḥkarmaike
11.11.1	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyādhastāt puro'kṣaṃ catura uparavān avāntaradeśeṣu prādeśamukhān prādeśāntarālān karoti
11.11.2	devasya tvā savituḥ prasava ity abhrim ādāya parilikhitaṃ rakṣaḥ parilikhitā arātaya iti trir dakṣiṇapūrvaṃ parilikhati
11.11.3	evam itarān pradakṣiṇam uttarāpavargam
11.11.4	evam anupūrvāṇy evaiṣv ata ūrdhvaṃ karmāṇi kriyante
11.11.5	adhastāt saṃtṛṇṇā bhavanti / upariṣṭād asaṃbhinnāḥ
11.11.6	tūṣṇīṃ bāhumātrān khātvā rakṣohaṇo valagahano vaiṣṇavān khanāmīti khanati
11.11.7	ekavad uparavamantrān eke samāmananti
11.11.8	virāḍ asīti bāhum upāvahṛtyedam ahaṃ taṃ valagam udvapāmīty udupyoparavanyante 'vabādhate gāyatreṇa chandasāvabāḍho valaga iti
11.11.9	harāmi vaiṣṇavān iti harati / avabāḍho durasyur ity agreṇopastambhanaṃ nivapati
11.11.10	evaṃ sarvān karoti
11.11.11	etāvan nānā / pūrveṇapūrveṇa mantreṇa bāhum upāvahṛtyottareṇottareṇa chandasāvabādhate
11.11.12	gāyatraṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatam ānuṣṭubhaṃ pāṅktam ity āmnātāni bhavanti
11.12.1	prathamaṃ vā sarveṣu
11.12.2	virāḍ asi sapatnahā bhrātṛvyahā svarāḍ asy abhimātihā viśvārāḍ asi viśvāsāṃ nāṣṭrāṇāṃ hanteti bāhū upāvaharato 'dhvaryur yajamānaś ca
11.12.3	saṃmṛśa imān āyuṣe varcase ca devānāṃ nidhir asi dveṣoyavanaḥ / yuyodhy asmad dveṣāṃsi yāni kāni ca cakṛma // devānām idaṃ nihitaṃ yad asty athābhāhi pradiśaś catasraḥ / kṛṇvāno anyāṁ adharān sapatnān ity uparavān saṃmṛśya dakṣiṇapūrvaṃ yajamāno 'vamṛśati / uttarāparam adhvaryuḥ
11.12.4	atha yajamānaḥ pṛcchaty adhvaryo kim atreti / bhadram itītaraḥ pratyāha / tan nau sahety uktvottarapūrvaṃ yajamāno 'vamṛśati / dakṣiṇāparam adhvaryuḥ / tathaiva praśnaḥ prativacanaṃ ca / tan ma ity āha yajamānaḥ
11.12.5	rakṣohaṇo valagahanaḥ prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavān iti yavamatībhir uparavān prokṣyottarair mantrair avanayāmīti prokṣaṇīśeṣam avaṭe 'vanīya yavo 'sīti yavam avāsyāvastṝṇāmīti barhiṣāvastīryābhijuhomīty ājyenābhijuhoti
11.12.6	evaṃ sarvān karoti
11.12.7	rakṣohaṇau valagahanau prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavī ity adhiṣavaṇaphalake prokṣati
11.13.1	audumbare kārṣmaryamaye pālāśe vā śuṣke taṣṭe pradhimukhe purastāt samāvikarte paścāt
11.13.2	na saṃtṛṇatty ekāhe / tata ūrdhvaṃ saṃtṛdye
11.13.3	ukthyādiṣu vā saṃtṛṇatti
11.13.4	athaine uparaveṣūpadadhāti rakṣohaṇau valagahanāv upadadhāmi vaiṣṇavī iti
11.13.5	dvau dakṣiṇenāpidadhāti / dvāv uttareṇa
11.13.6	saṃhite purastād dvyaṅgulena paścād asaṃhite bhavataḥ
11.13.7	athaine uttarair mantraiḥ paryūhāmīti pradakṣiṇam uparavapāṃsubhiḥ paryuhya paristṝṇāmīti barhiṣā paristīryottamenābhimantrayate
11.13.8	etasyaiva havirdhānasyāgreṇopastambhanam uparavapāṃsubhiś caturaśraṃ kharaṃ karoti somapātrebhya āptam
11.13.9	purastāt saṃcaraṃ śinaṣṭi
11.13.10	antarā cātvālotkarāv āgnīdhracātvālau vādhvaryur dṛśīkavaś ca saṃcareyuḥ
11.13.11	sarvataḥ prasute dṛśīkavaḥ saṃcareyur ity eke
11.14.1	cātvālād dhiṣṇiyān upavapati
11.14.2	antarāgnīdhra āgnīdhrīyam uttare vedyanta uttarataḥ saṃcaraṃ śiṣṭvā
11.14.3	sadasītarān pūrvārdhe purastāt saṃcaraṃ śiṣṭvā
11.14.4	pṛṣṭhyāyāṃ hotrīyam / taṃ dakṣiṇena praśāstrīyam
11.14.5	uttareṇa hotrīyam itarān udīca āyātayati / brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ potur neṣṭur acchāvākasyeti
11.14.6	bahiḥ sadaso mārjālīyaṃ dakṣiṇe vedyante dakṣiṇataḥ saṃcaraṃ śiṣṭvā samam āgnīdhrīyeṇa
11.14.7	vibhūr asīty aṣṭābhiḥ pratimantram
11.14.8	etān evopasthānān vyāghāraṇāṃś caike samāmananti
11.14.9	anudiśatītarān adhvanām adhvapate namas te astu mā mā hiṃsīr iti taṃtam abhikrāmam
11.14.10	samrāḍ asi kṛśānur ity āhavanīyam / pariṣadyo 'si pavamāna iti bahiṣpavamānāstāvam / pratakvāsi nabhasvān iti cātvālam / asaṃmṛṣṭo 'si havyasūda iti śāmitram / samūhyo 'si viśvabharā ity utkaram / ṛtadhāmāsi suvarjyotir ity audumbarīm
11.15.1	brahmajyotir asi suvardhāmeti brahmāṇam / sadasyo 'si malimluca iti sadasyam / samudro 'si viśvabharā iti sadaḥ / ajo 'sy ekapād iti śālāmukhīyam / ahir asi budhniya iti prājahitam / kavyo 'si kavyavāhana iti dakṣiṇāgnim / āyur bṛhat tad aśīya tan māvatu tasya nāmnā vṛścāmi yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ / viśvāyur vāmadevyaṃ tad aśīya tan māvatu tasya nāmnā vṛścāmi yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ / āyuḥpati rathamtaraṃ tad aśīya tan māvatu tasya nāmnā vṛścāmi yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma ity etaiś ca pratimantraṃ havirdhānāgnīdhrasadāṃsīti
11.15.2	raudreṇānīkeneti sarvatrānuṣajati
11.15.3	stṛṇīta barhiḥ pra vrataṃ yacchateti saṃpreṣyati
11.15.4	pūrvasmin vā staraṇa etaṃ saṃpraiṣaṃ brūyāt
11.15.5	atra stṛṇann uttaravedikharoparavadhiṣṇiyān nābhistṛṇīyāt
11.15.6	atraikastanaṃ vrataṃ yajamānāya prayacchati
11.15.7	ardhavratam atra vājasaneyinaḥ samāmananti / ardham antareṇottame pravargyopasadau
11.16.1	agnīṣomīyasya paśos tantraṃ prakramayati
11.16.2	tasya nirūḍhapaśubandhavat kalpaḥ
11.16.3	ṣaḍḍhotā paśviṣṭiś cāṅgabhūteṣu na vidyate
11.16.4	ātithyābarhis tūṣṇīm upasaṃnahyati
11.16.5	tāṃś ca paridhīn pāśuka idhme
11.16.6	pātrasaṃsādanakāle pracaraṇīṃ srucaṃ saptamīṃ prayunakti
11.16.7	tasyā juhūvat kalpaḥ
11.16.8	ājyagrahaṇakāle pracaraṇyām āditas tūṣṇīṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā pāśukāny ājyāni gṛhṇāti
11.16.9	praitu brahmaṇaspatnīti pratiprasthātā patnīm udānayati
11.16.10	athāham anukāminīti patnī śālāmukhīyam upopaviśya suprajasas tvā vayam iti japati
11.16.11	upasthe brahmā rājānaṃ kurute
11.16.12	sam apivratān hvayadhvam iti saṃpreṣyati
11.16.13	yajamānasyāmātyān saṃhvayanti
11.16.14	adhvaryuṃ yajamāno 'nvārabhate / yajamānaṃ patnī / patnīm itare putrabhrātaraḥ
11.16.15	ahatena vāsasāmātyān saṃpracchādya vāsaso 'nte srugdaṇḍam upaniyamya pracarṇyā vaisarjanāni juhoti
11.16.16	tvaṃ soma tanūkṛdbhyo juṣāṇa ity etābhyām ardhaṃ gārhapatye
11.16.17	ā somaṃ dadate
11.17.1	ā grāvṇa ā vāyavyāny ā droṇakalaśam / ut patnīm ānayanti / anv anāṃsi pravartayanti / yāyāvarasya yāny aparasmin gārhapatye bhavanti / ajam anunayanti / idhmābarhir ājyāni prokṣaṇīr ity anuharanti
11.17.2	śālāmukhīye praṇayanīyam idhmam ādīpya sikatābhir upayamyāgnīṣomābhyāṃ praṇīyamānābhyām anubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati / praṇīyamānābhyām anubrūhīti vā
11.17.3	prathamāyāṃ trir anūktāyām ayaṃ no agnir varivaḥ kṛṇotv ity agniprathamāḥ somaprathamā vā prāñco 'bhipravrajanti
11.17.4	āgnīdhrīye 'gniṃ pratiṣṭhāpyāgne nayety ardham ājyaśeṣasya juhoti
11.17.5	grāvṇo vāyavyāni droṇakalaśam āgnīdhra upavāsayati
11.17.6	uttareṇāgnīdhrīyam āhavanīyaṃ gatvoru viṣṇo vikramasveti sarvam ājyaśeṣaṃ juhoti
11.17.7	hute 'mātyāḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya yathetam upāvartante
11.17.8	somo jigāti gātuvid ity aparayā dvārā havirdhānaṃ rājānaṃ prapādayati / pūrvayā gataśriyaḥ
11.17.9	pūrvayā yajamānaḥ prapadyate
11.17.10	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya nīḍe pūrvavat kṛṣṇājināstaraṇaṃ rājñaś cāsādanam
11.18.1	athainaṃ yajamāno devatābhyaḥ saṃprayacchaty eṣa vo deva savitaḥ soma iti
11.18.2	etat tvaṃ soma devo devān upāgā ity abhimantryedam ahaṃ manuṣyo manuṣyān iti pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya namo devebhya iti prācīnam añjaliṃ kṛtvā svadhā pitṛbhya iti dakṣiṇedam ahaṃ nir varuṇasya pāśād ity upaniṣkramya svar abhivyakhyam iti prāṅ prekṣate / suvar abhivikhyeṣam iti / sarvaṃ vihāram anuvīkṣate / vaiśvānaraṃ jyotir ity āhavanīyam
11.18.3	atra yajamāno 'vāntaradīkṣāṃ visṛjate
11.18.4	agne vratapate tvaṃ vratānāṃ vratapatir asīty āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate / etenaivāsmin samidham ādadhātīti vājasaneyakam
11.18.5	vitarāṃ mekhalāṃ visraṃsate / vitarāṃ muṣṭī karṣate
11.18.6	atra daṇḍapradānam eke samāmananti
11.18.7	svāhā yajñaṃ manasā svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ svāhoror antarikṣāt svāhā yajñaṃ vātād ārabha iti muṣṭī visṛjate
11.18.8	svāhā vāci vāte visṛja iti vācam
11.18.9	nivartate vratam
11.18.10	somān haviḥśeṣān iti sutye 'hani bhakṣayati
11.18.11	uttareṇāhavanīyaṃ prāgagram idhmābarhir upasādayati / dakṣiṇam idhamam uttaraṃ barhiḥ
11.19.1	prokṣaṇīnām abhimantraṇādi karma pratipadyate
11.19.2	staraṇakāle 'pareṇottaravediṃ barhiḥ stṛṇāti
11.19.3	staraṇamantro 'bhyāvartate
11.19.4	ājyānāṃ sādanādi pāśukaṃ karma pratipadyate samānam ā pravarāt
11.19.5	daivaṃ ca mānuṣaṃ ca hotārau vṛtvāśrāvamāśrāvam ṛtupraiṣādibhiḥ saumikān ṛtvijo vṛṇīte
11.19.6	indraṃ hotrāt sajūr diva ā pṛthivyā iti hotāram
11.19.7	apisṛjya tṛṇam asphya uttarān
11.19.8	agnim āgnīdhrād ity āgnīdhram / aśvinādhvaryū ādhvaryavād ity adhvaryū / mitrāvaruṇau praśāstārau praśāstrād iti maitrāvaruṇam / indro brahmā brāhmaṇād iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsinam / marutaḥ potrād iti potāram / gnāvo neṣṭrād iti neṣṭāram / agnir daivīnāṃ viśāṃ puraetāyaṃ yajamāno manuṣyāṇāṃ tayor nāv asthūri gārhapatyaṃ dīdayac chataṃ himā dvā yū rādhāṃsīt saṃpṛñcānāv asaṃpṛñcānau tanva iti yajamānam
11.19.9	ayaṃ sunvan yajamāno manuṣyāṇām iti vā
11.19.10	savanīye varaṇam eke samāmananti / tatra sunvann iti brūyāt
11.19.11	sarvatropāṃśu nāmagrahaṇam / mānuṣa ity uccaiḥ
11.20.1	pravṛtaḥpravṛtaḥ pravṛtahomau juhoti juṣṭo vāco bhūyāsam ṛcā stomaṃ samardhayety etābhyām
11.20.2	divā prayājaiḥ pracaryāstaṃyantam anūyājair upāsate
11.20.3	hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ mārjayitvā subrahmaṇya pitāputrīyāṃ subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti saṃpreṣyati
11.20.4	pitāputrīyaivāta ūrdhvaṃ subrahmaṇyā bhavati
11.20.5	āhūtāyāṃ vasatīvarīḥ kumbhena giribhidāṃ vahantīnāṃ pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan gṛhṇāti
11.20.6	nāntamā vahantīr atīyāt
11.20.7	chāyāyai cātapataś ca saṃdhau gṛhṇāti
11.20.8	yady abhicchāyāṃ na vinded ātmano vṛkṣasya kūlasya vā chāyāyām
11.20.9	pratīpam upamārayan haviṣmatīr imā āpa iti gṛhṇāti
11.20.10	yasyāgṛhītā abhinimrocet suvarna gharmaḥ svāheti pañcārkāhutīr hutvā vare datta ulkām upariṣṭād dhārayamāṇo gṛhṇīyāt / hiraṇyaṃ vāvadhāya
11.20.11	yo vā brāhmaṇo bahuyājī tasya kumbhyānāṃ gṛhṇīyāt
11.20.12	somayājī bahuyājī bhavatīti vijñāyate
11.20.13	agner vo 'pannagṛhasya sadasi sādayāmīty apareṇa śālāmukhīyam upasādayati / sumnāya sumninīḥ sumne mā dhatteti sarveṣu vasatīvarīṇāṃ sādaneṣu yajamāno japati / agnīṣomīyasya paśupuroḍāśasya pātrasaṃsādanādi karma pratipadyate
11.20.14	na yajamāno 'gnīṣomīyasyāśnāti / aśnīyād vā
11.20.15	na svaruṃ juhoti / na hṛdayaśūlam udvāsayati / evaṃ savanīye
11.20.16	patnīsaṃyājānto 'gnīṣomīyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
11.21.1	niśāyāṃ vasatīvarīḥ pariharaty antarvedy āsīne yajamāne patnyāṃ ca
11.21.2	nādīkṣitam abhipariharet
11.21.3	savye 'ṃse 'tyādhāyāpareṇa prājahitaṃ parikramya pūrvayā dvāropanirhṛtya dakṣiṇena vediṃ gatvā dakṣiṇena mārjālīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītya dakṣiṇasyām uttaravediśroṇyāṃ sādayatīndrāgniyor bhāgadheyī stheti
11.21.4	dakṣiṇe 'ṃse 'tyādhāya yathetaṃ gatvā pūrvayā dvāropanirhṛtyottareṇa vediṃ gatvottareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītyottarasyām uttaravediśroṇyāṃ sādayati mitrāvaruṇayor bhāgadheyī stheti
11.21.5	savye 'ṃse 'tyādhāya yathetaṃ gatvāpareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyam upasādayati viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ bhāgadheyī stheti
11.21.6	yajñe jāgṛteti sannā abhimantrayate
11.21.7	atra pratiprasthātā payasyārthaṃ sāyaṃdohaṃ dohayati
11.21.8	adhvaryuḥ saṃpreṣyati yā yajamānasya vratadhuk tasyā āśiraṃ kuruta yā patniyai tasyai dadhigrahāya yā gharmadhuk tasyai dadhigharmāya taptam anātaktaṃ maitrāvaruṇāya śṛtātaṅkyaṃ dadhi kurutād ity agrahāya subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvaya na sadasy upavastavā iti
11.21.9	saṃpraiṣavat kurvanti
11.21.10	atra savanīyasya savanīyānām itīdhmābarhiḥ saṃnahyati
11.21.11	na vā barhiḥ / prastaram eva
11.21.12	āgnīdhre havirdhāne vā yajamānaṃ jāgarayanti / prāgvaṃśe patnīm
11.21.13	āgnīdhra etāṃ rātrim ṛtvijo vasanti
11.21.14	yajamāno rājānaṃ gopayati gopayati
12.1.1	mahārātre buddhvāgne nayety āgnīdhram abhimṛśati
12.1.2	idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti havirdhānam / agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti srucaḥ / ā vāyo bhūṣa śucipā iti vāyavyāni / ā ghā ye agnim indhata iti sadaḥ
12.1.3	prajāpatir manasāndho 'ccheta iti trayastriṃśatam āgnīdhre yajñatanūr juhoti / prathamena mantreṇa hutvā pūrvaṃ pūrvam anudrutyottareṇottareṇa juhoti
12.1.4	prādeśamātrāṇy ūrdhvasānūny upariṣṭād āsecanavanti madhye saṃnatāni vāyavyāni bhavanti
12.1.5	teṣāṃ yāny anādiṣṭavṛkṣāṇi vaikaṅkatāni syuḥ / yo vā yajñiyo vṛkṣaḥ phalagrahiḥ
12.1.6	ko vo yunakti sa vo yunaktv iti khare pātrāṇi prayunakti yāny anāmnātamantrāṇi bhavanti
12.1.7	agnir devateti dakṣiṇe 'ṃsa upāṃśupātram
12.1.8	somo devatety uttaram antaryāmasya
12.1.9	bṛhann asīti te antareṇa grāvāṇam upāṃśusavanaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaṃ saṃspṛṣṭaṃ pātrābhyām
12.1.10	tam apareṇa pratyañci dvidevatyapātrāṇi
12.1.11	indro devateti parisrag aindravāyavasya / bṛhaspatir devatety ajagāvaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya / aśvinau devateti dvisrakty āśvinasya
12.1.12	tāny apareṇa prabāhuk śukrāmanthinoḥ pātre / sūryo devateti dakṣiṇaṃ bailvaṃ śukrasya / candramā devatety uttaraṃ vaikaṅkataṃ manthinaḥ
12.1.13	te apareṇa prabāhug ṛtupātre āśvatthe aśvaśaphabudhne ubhayatomukhe / dakṣiṇam adhvaryoḥ / uttaraṃ pratiprasthātuḥ
12.1.14	viśve devā devateti dakṣiṇasyāṃ śroṇyām āgrayaṇasthālīm / indro devatety uttarasyām ukthyasthālīm / ukthyapātraṃ ca tasyā uttaram
12.1.15	sthālyāv antareṇa trīṇy udañcy atigrāhyapātrāṇi / āgneyam aindraṃ sauryam iti
12.2.1	uttare 'ṃse dadhigrahapātram audumbaraṃ catuḥsrakti
12.2.2	evaṃrūpam evāṃśvadābhyayoḥ
12.2.3	yadi somagrahaṃ gṛhṇīyād etad eva vibhavet
12.2.4	etasyaiva havirdhānasyāgreṇopastambhanam ādityasthālīm / ādityapātraṃ ca tasyā uttaram
12.2.5	pṛthivī devatety uttarasya havirdhānasyāgreṇopastambhanam anupopte dhruvasthālīm
12.2.6	khare ṣoḍaśipātraṃ khādiraṃ catuḥsrakti yadi ṣoḍaśī
12.2.7	madhye pariplavāṃ yathā srugadaṇḍaivam
12.2.8	yathāvakāśaṃ daśa camasān naiyyagrodhān rauhītakān vātsarumato 'tsarukān vā
12.2.9	daśaiva camasādhvaryavaḥ
12.2.10	yunajmi te pṛthivīṃ jyotiṣā saheti dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyādhastāt paścād akṣaṃ droṇakalaśaṃ sadaśāpavitram
12.2.11	tasya vāyavyair vṛkṣaniyogaḥ
12.2.12	yunajmi vāyum antarikṣeṇa te sahety uttarasya havirdhānasyopariṣṭān nīḍa ādhavanīyam / yunajmi vācaṃ saha sūryeṇa ta iti pradhure pūtabhṛtam
12.2.13	etasyaiva havirdhānasyādhastāt paścād akṣaṃ trīn ekadhanān ghaṭān / pañca sapta navaikādaśa vā
12.2.14	yasmin mimīte tasyādhiṣavaṇacarma kharaṃ parikṛttaṃ catuṣpuṭam upariṣṭād āsecanavat
12.2.15	rakṣohaṇo valagahanaḥ prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavam ity adhiṣavaṇacarma prokṣya rakṣoghno valagaghnaḥ prokṣāmi vaiṣṇavān iti grāvṇo rakṣohā tvā valagahā vaiṣṇavam āstṝṇāmīty adhiṣavaṇaphalakayor uttaralomāstīrya rakṣoghno vo valagaghnaḥ saṃsādayāmi vaiṣṇavān iti tasmiṃś caturo grāvṇaḥ prādeśamātrān ūrdhvasānūn āhananaprakārān aśmanaḥ saṃsādayati / uparaṃ prathiṣṭhaṃ madhye pañcamam
12.2.16	tam abhisaṃmukhā bhavanti
12.3.1	sthavīyāṃsi mukhāni
12.3.2	apāṃ kṣayā ṛtasya garbhā bhuvanasya gopāḥ śyenā atithayaḥ parvatānāṃ kakubhaḥ prayuto na pātāraḥ / vagnunendraṃ hvayata ghoṣeṇāmīvāṃś cātayata / yuktā stha vahata svargaṃ lokaṃ yajamānam abhivahateti sannān abhimantryāgnīṣomīyavat savanīyapātrāṇi prayunakti / agnīṣomīyavad ājyāni gṛhṇāti
12.3.3	athaikeṣām / prāgvaṃśe 'gnīṣomīyasyājyāni gṛhṇāti / āgnīdhre savanīyasya / uttaravedyām anūbandhyāyāḥ
12.3.4	apareṇottaravediṃ savanīyasyānūbandhyāyāś cājyāni gṛhṇātīty eke
12.3.5	yāni kāṣṭhāni tad ahar abhyādhāsyan syāt tāni sahedhmena prokṣet
12.3.6	samānam ā srucāṃ sādanāt
12.3.7	yunajmi tisro vipṛcaḥ sūryasya ta iti srucaḥ sannā abhimantrayate
12.3.8	atra saumikānāṃ pātrāṇāṃ saṃsādanam eke samāmananti
12.3.9	āsanyān mā mantrāt pāhi kasyāś cid abhiśastyā iti purā prātaranuvākāj juhuyāt
12.3.10	pañcahotāraṃ cāgnīdhre svargakāmasya
12.3.11	nityavad eke samāmananti
12.3.12	madhye 'gner ājyāhutīḥ paśvāhutīḥ puroḍāśāhutīr iti juhoti / abhitaḥ somāhutīḥ
12.3.13	atra rājānam antareṣe grāvasūpāvaharati hṛde tvā soma rājann ity etābhyām
12.3.14	purā vācaḥ purā vā vayobhyaḥ pravaditoḥ prātaranuvākam upākaroti
12.3.15	prātaryāvabhyo devebhyo 'nubrūhi brahman vācaṃ yaccha pratiprasthātaḥ savanīyān nirvapa subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti saṃpreṣyati
12.3.16	subrahmaṇye subrahmaṇyām āhvayety eke samāmananti
12.3.17	manasā te vācaṃ pratigṛṇāmīty adhvaryur hotāram āha
12.3.18	atra pratiprasthātā savanīyānāṃ pāṇiprakṣālanādi karma pratipadyate
12.3.19	yathārthaṃ pātrāṇi prayunakti
12.4.1	dve bharjanārthe kapāle aṣṭau puroḍāśakapālāni / ekādaśa mādhyaṃdine / dvādaśa tṛtīyasavane
12.4.2	sarvān aindrān ekādaśakapālān anusavanam eke samāmananti
12.4.3	prātardohapātrāṇīti
12.4.4	prāgvaṃśe pratiprasthātā savanīyān nirvapati
12.4.5	sarve yavā bhavanti lājārthān parihāpya
12.4.6	indrāya harivate dhānā indrāya pūṣaṇvate karambhaṃ sarasvatyai bhāratyai parivāpam indrāya puroḍāśaṃ mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ payasyām iti
12.4.7	nirupteṣv anvopyedaṃ devānām ity etadādi karma pratipadyate
12.4.8	avahananakāle lājārthān parihāpyetarān avahanti
12.4.9	kapālānām upadhānakāle prathamena kapālamantreṇa dhānārthaṃ lājārthaṃ ca kapāle adhiśrayati
12.4.10	adhiśrayaṇakāle 'dhiśrayaṇamantreṇa taṇḍulān opya dhānāḥ karoti / vrīhīn opya lājān karoti
12.4.11	puroḍāśam adhiśrityāmikṣāvat payasyāṃ karoti
12.4.12	udvāsanakāle dhānā udvāsya vibhāgamantreṇa vibhajyārdhā ājyena saṃyauti / ardhāḥ piṣṭānām āvṛtā saktūn karoti
12.4.13	manthaṃ saṃyutaṃ karambha ity ācakṣate / lājān parivāpa iti
12.4.14	nakhair lājebhyas tuṣān saṃharati
12.4.15	nakheṣūlūkhaladharmān musaladharmāṃś ca karoti
12.5.1	yatrābhijānāty abhūd uṣā ruśat paśur iti tat pracaraṇyā juhoti śṛṇotv agniḥ samidhā havaṃ ma iti
12.5.2	aparaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā saṃpreṣyaty apa iṣya hotar maitrāvaruṇasya camasādhvaryav ādravaikadhanina ādravata neṣṭaḥ patnīm udānayonnetar hotṛcamasena vasatīvarībhiś ca cātvālaṃ pratyāsveti
12.5.3	prehy udehīti neṣṭā patnīm udānayati / ehy udehīti vā / pānnejanīṃ sthālīṃ dhārayamāṇām
12.5.4	tīrthenābhipravrajanti
12.5.5	yatra hotuḥ prātaranuvākam anubruvata upaśṛṇuyus tad apo 'dhvaryur vahantīnāṃ gṛhṇāti
12.5.6	yadi na śṛṇoti badhiro ha bhavati vāco ha chidyate
12.5.7	yadi dūre syuḥ pratyudūhya gṛhṇīyāt
12.5.8	devīr āpa iti tṛṇam antardhāyābhijuhoti
12.5.9	yadi vā purā tṛṇaṃ syāt tasmiñ juhuyāt
12.5.10	kārṣir asīti darbhair āhutim apaplāvya samudrasya vo 'kṣityā unnaya ity abhihutānāṃ maitrāvaruṇacamasena gṛhṇāti
12.5.11	somasya tvā mūjavato rasaṃ gṛhṇāmīty ekadhanāḥ
12.5.12	patnī pannejanīr gṛhṇāti pratyaṅtiṣṭhantī vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhya iti
12.5.13	prehy udehīti neṣṭā patnīm udānayati / ehy udehīti vā
12.5.14	apareṇa neṣṭrīyaṃ patnī pannejanīḥ sādayati pratyaṅ tiṣṭhantī vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhya iti
12.5.15	tā evam evācchāvākaṃ sīdantam anūpasādayati
12.6.1	hotṛcamasena vasatīvarībhyo niṣicyopari cātvāle hotṛcamasaṃ maitrāvaruṇacamasaṃ ca saṃsparśya vasatīvarīr vyānayati
12.6.2	sam anyā yantīty abhijñāya hotṛcamasān maitrāvaruṇacamasa ānayati / maitrāvaruṇacamasād dhotṛcamase / etad vā viparītam
12.6.3	upari cātvāle dhāryamāṇā ubhayīḥ pracaraṇyā samanakti saṃ vo 'naktu varuṇaḥ sam indraḥ saṃ pūṣā saṃ dhātā saṃ bṛhaspatiḥ / tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ prajayā saṃrārāṇo yajamānāya draviṇaṃ dadhātv iti / yathāyathaṃ dhuro dhurbhiḥ kalpantām iti
12.6.4	adhvaryo 'verapā iti hotādhvaryuṃ pṛcchati
12.6.5	utem anannamur iti pratyuktvā pracaraṇīśeṣāt kratukaraṇaṃ juhoti yam agne pṛtsu martyam iti
12.6.6	tad abhāve caturgṛhītena
12.6.7	yady agniṣṭomo juhotīty uktam
12.6.8	athaikeṣām / yady agniṣṭomo juhoti / yady ukthyaḥ paridhau nimārṣṭi / yadi ṣoḍaśī hutvā paridhau lepaṃ nimṛjya droṇakalaśaṃ rarāṭīṃ copaspṛśati / na juhoti nopaspṛśati vājapeye 'tirātre ca / etad yajur vadan samudyaiva prapadyate
12.6.9	aparayā dvārā havirdhānam apaḥ prapādayati / pūrvayā gataśriyaḥ
12.6.10	pūrvayā yajamānaḥ prapadyate
12.6.11	dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya pradhure pracaraṇīṃ sādayati
12.7.1	yaṃ kāmayeta paṇḍakaḥ syād iti taṃ pracaraṇyopaspṛśet
12.7.2	etasyaiva havirdhānasyādhastāt puro'kṣaṃ maitrāvaruṇacamasam / uttarasyāṃ vartanyāṃ puraścakraṃ hotṛcamasam / uttarasya havirdhānasyādhastāt puro'kṣaṃ vasatīvarīḥ / paścādakṣam ekadhanāḥ
12.7.3	etad vā viparītam
12.7.4	apo yajamāno 'nuprapadyate / yaśa evainam ṛcchatīti vijñāyate
12.7.5	atra dadhigraheṇa carati
12.7.6	audumbareṇa gṛhṇāti
12.7.7	upayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpataye tvā jyotiṣmate jyotiṣmantaṃ gṛhṇāmīti dadhi gṛhītvāpendra dviṣato mana iti harati / prāṇāya tvāpānāya tveti juhoti
12.7.8	dadhigraho nityaḥ kāmyaś ca / kāmyāv itarau
12.7.9	ājyagrahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tejaskāmasyety uktam
12.7.10	yadi somagrahaṃ gṛhṇīyād ekagrahāyāptaṃ rājānam upare nyupya vasatīvarībhir upasṛjyāvīvṛdhaṃ vo manasā sujātā ity abhimantrya tisro yahvasya samidhaḥ parijmano devā akṛṇvann uśijo amartyave / tāsām ekām adadhur martye bhujaṃ lokam id dve upa jāmī īyatur iti somakaraṇyābhiṣuṇoti
12.7.11	ā māskān iti prathamaplutam aṃśum abhimantrayate / drapsaś caskandeti vipruṣaḥ
12.7.12	hiraṇyapāṇir abhiṣuṇoti gṛhṇāti juhotīty atyantapradeśaḥ
12.7.13	tisro yahvasyety etad varjaṃ ca
12.7.14	taṃ hutvā sadasi pratyaṅmukho bhakṣayati bhakṣehīti yathāliṅgam
12.7.15	anadhikṛto vā somadharmair dadhigrahavikāratvāt
12.7.16	yad anyat somakaraṇyās te somadharmāḥ
12.7.17	aṃśum adābhyaṃ vā prathamaṃ gṛhṇāti
12.7.18	śukraṃ te śukreṇa gṛhṇāmīti dadhnaḥ payaso nigrābhyāṇāṃ vā
12.7.19	upanaddhasya rājñas trīn aṃśūn pravṛhati
12.8.1	vasavas tvā pravṛhantu gāyatreṇa chandasety etaiḥ pratimantram
12.8.2	tair enaṃ catur ādhūnoti / pañcakṛtvaḥ saptakṛtvo vā / māndāsu ta ity etān prativibhajya
12.8.3	āsminn ugrā acucyavur ity ādāya kakuhaṃ rūpam iti harati / yat te somādābhyaṃ nāma jāgṛvīti juhoti
12.8.4	ādhavanān aṃśūn prajñātān nidhāyośik tvaṃ deva soma gāyatreṇa chandasety etaiḥ pratimantram anusavanam ekaikaṃ mahābhiṣaveṣv apisṛjati
12.8.5	aṃśuṃ gṛhṇann ekagrahāyāptaṃ rājānam upare nyupya sakṛd abhiṣutya vāmadevyaṃ manasā gāyamāno 'navānaṃ gṛhṇāti / vāmadevyasya varcā kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti
12.8.6	parācīnena grāhyaḥ prāṇatāpānatā vā prāṇyāpānya vyanatā vā
12.8.7	yadi vyavāned ā naḥ prāṇa etu parāvata iti śatamānaṃ hiraṇyam abhivyaneyātām adhvaryur yajamānaś ca
12.8.8	athainau pratiprasthātā hiraṇyena saṃsparśyaty adbhiś ca pratyukṣati
12.8.9	indrāgnī me varcaḥ kṛṇutām ity adhvaryur apa upaspṛśya dadhanve vā yad īm anv ity aniruktayāprājāpatyayā prāṇyāpānya vyanañ juhoti
12.8.10	yadi na śaknuyād grahītuṃ hotuṃ vā vare datte gṛhṇīyāj juhuyād vā
12.8.11	aṃśau dvādaśa prathamagarbhāḥ paṣṭhauhīr dadāti kṛttyadhīvāsaṃ ca / evam adābhye
12.8.12	bhrātṛvyavatādābhyo grahītavyaḥ / bubhūṣatāṃśuḥ
12.8.13	tau na sarvatra grahītavyau / vājapeye rājasūye sattre sarvavedase vā
12.8.14	yo 'sya supriyaḥ suvicita iva syāt tasya grahītavyau
12.9.1	uttarasyāṃ vartanyāṃ hotṛcamasaṃ vasatīvarībhir abhipūrya nigrābhyāsu yajamānaṃ vācayati nigrābhyā stha devaśruta iti
12.9.2	devasya tvā savituḥ prasava iti grāvāṇam upāṃśusavanam ādāya grāvāsy adhvarakṛd ity abhimantrayate / tam ādadāno vācaṃ yatvāgrayaṇaṃ gṛhītvā visṛjate
12.9.3	athainam upare nidhāyāṃśubhir abhimimīte krayavat
12.9.4	etāvan nānā / indrāya tvā vṛtraghna ity etaiḥ pratimantram
12.9.5	pañcakṛtvo yajuṣā mimīte / pañcakṛtvas tūṣṇīm
12.9.6	nāṃśūn upasamūhati
12.9.7	bhūyāṃsaṃ prātaḥsavanāya rājānaṃ prakalpayati / alpīyāṃsaṃ mādhyaṃdināya
12.9.8	upanahya pratyāropyaikagrahāyāptaṃ rājānam upare nyupya hotṛcamase 'ṃśūn avadhāya tasmin grāvāṇam upāṃśusavanam upari dhārayaṃs triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ pariplāvayan nigrābham upaiti prāg apāg udag adharāg iti
12.9.9	yāṃ bhāryāṃ kāmayeta tāṃ manasā dhyāyed amba niṣvareti / sā hainaṃ kāmayate
12.9.10	śvātrā stha vṛtratura iti tāsām ekadeśenopasṛjyopaspṛṣṭasya rājñaḥ ṣaḍ aṃśūn ārdrān saṃśliṣṭān ādāya carmaṇi nidhāya yat te soma divi jyotir iti rājānam abhimantrayate
12.10.1	dhiṣaṇe vīḍū ity adhiṣavaṇaphalake
12.10.2	avīvṛdhaṃ vo manasā sujātā iti rājānam evābhimantrya mā bher mā saṃvikthā iti grāvāṇam udyamyānāgasas tvā vayam indreṇa preṣitā upa vāyuṣ ṭe astv aṃśa bhūr mitras te astv aṃśa bhūr varuṇas te astv aṃśa bhūr ahataḥ somo rājeti tṛṇam antardhāyābhiṣuṇoti
12.10.3	yadi vā purā tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ mūlaṃ vā syāt tasmin praharet
12.10.4	aṣṭaukṛtvo 'gre 'bhiṣuṇoti
12.10.5	atha pratiprasthātopāṃśupātraṃ dhārayann apāttānām upari dvāv aṃśū antardadhāti
12.10.6	tasminn abhiṣutam adhvaryur añjalinā gṛhṇāti vācaspataye pavasva vājinn iti
12.10.7	pavitram upayāmaḥ sādanaṃ ca na vidyate
12.10.8	eṣa prathamaḥ paryāyaḥ / evaṃ vihito dvitīyas tṛtīyaś ca
12.10.9	api vaikādaśakṛtvo dvitīyam abhiṣuṇoti / dvādaśakṛtvas tṛtīyam
12.10.10	dvir ādito 'ntato vā nigrābhopāyanam upasargaś ca
12.10.11	hotṛcamasīyān aṃśūn uttame paryāye 'bhiṣuṇoti
12.10.12	avaśiṣṭānāṃ pratiprasthātā dvau dvāv aṃśū antardadhāti
12.10.13	svāṃkṛto 'sīty adhvaryur graham ādāyorv antarikṣam anvitīti dakṣiṇena hotāram atikrāmati
12.10.14	yena vā hotā pratipādayet
12.10.15	manas tvāṣṭv iti dakṣiṇato 'vasthāya dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavahṛtya
12.11.1	svāhā tvā subhavaḥ sūryāyeti dakṣiṇataḥ prāñcam ṛjuṃ saṃtataṃ dīrghaṃ hutvā devebhyas tvā marīcipebhya iti madhyame paridhau lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
12.11.2	yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya prahvo juhuyāt
12.11.3	yadi kāmayeta varṣukaḥ prajanyaḥ syād ity abhyantaraṃ pātrasyāvamṛjyābhyantaraṃ paridher nīcā hastena nimṛjyāt
12.11.4	yadi kāmayetāvarṣukaḥ syād iti bāhyataḥ pātrasyordhvam unmṛjya bāhyataḥ paridher uttānena hastenordhvam unmṛjyāt
12.11.5	sarvam āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ saṃpātam avanīyaiṣa te yoniḥ prāṇāya tveti riktaṃ pātram āyatane sādayitvā tasminn aṃśum avāsya taṃ tṛtīyasavane 'pisṛjyābhiṣuṇuyāt
12.11.6	athaitāny abhicarataḥ
12.11.7	upāṃśuṃ gṛhītvāmuṣya tvā prāṇe sādayāmīti sādayitvā devasya tvā savituḥ prasava ity ādāyāmuṣya tvā prāṇam apidadhāmīti hastenāpidhāyāmuṃ jahy atha tvā hoṣyāmīti brūyāt
12.11.8	yadi dūre syād ā tamitos tiṣṭhet
12.11.9	praharṣiṇo madirasya made mṛṣāsāv astv iti jihmas tiṣṭhan hutvāmuṣya tvā prāṇe sādayāmīti sādayet
12.11.10	yo vastre bāhāv urasi vāṃśur āśliṣṭas tam abhicarato juhotīty eke devāṃśo yasmai tveḍe tat satyam apariplutā bhaṅgyena hato 'sau phaḍ iti
12.11.11	yat te somādābhyaṃ nāma jāgṛvīty upāṃśupāvanānām anusavanaṃ dvaudvāv aṃśū mahābhiṣaveṣv apisṛjati
12.12.1	adābhyāṃśum upāṃśupāvanau cāpisṛjya sarve 'dhvaryavo digbhyo mahābhiṣavam abhiṣuṇvanti
12.12.2	purastād adhvaryur dakṣiṇataḥ pratiprasthātā paścān neṣṭottarata unnetā / paścād adhvaryuḥ purastān neṣṭety eke
12.12.3	upare rājānaṃ nyupya hotṛcamase 'ṃśūn avadhāyety etadādyopasargād upāṃśusavanavarjam / tūṣṇīm itarair grāvabhir abhiṣuṇvanti
12.12.4	evaṃ dvitīyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ copasṛjyābhiṣuṇvanti
12.12.5	abhiṣutam adhvaryur añjalinā saṃsiñcati
12.12.6	tam unnetāntareṣeṇoddhṛtyottarata ādhavanīye 'vanayati
12.12.7	eṣa evāpāṃ somasya ca panthāḥ
12.12.8	eṣa prathamaḥ paryāyaḥ
12.12.9	evaṃ vihito dvitīyas tṛtīyaś ca
12.12.10	triparyāyaḥ
12.12.11	saṃbhṛtya rājānam upare grāvṇaḥ saṃmukhān kṛtvā prapīḍyarjīṣaṃ mukheṣūpohati / ghāsamebhyaḥ prayacchatīti vijñāyate
12.12.12	teṣūdgātāro droṇakalaśaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya tasminn udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitraṃ vitanvanti
12.12.13	pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspate prabhur gātrāṇi paryeṣi viśvataḥ / ataptatanūr na tad āmo aśnute śṛtāsa id vahantas tat samāśateti vitatamānam abhimantrayate yajamānaḥ
12.13.1	pavitrasya yajamāno nābhiṃ kṛtvā tasmin hotṛcamasena dhārāṃ srāvayati
12.13.2	udacanenonnetādhavanīyād dhotṛcamasa ānayati
12.13.3	saṃtatā dhārā srāvayitavyā / kāmo hāsya samardhuko bhavatīti vijñāyate
12.13.4	yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya vicchindyāt
12.13.5	dhārāyā antaryāmaṃ gṛhṇāti / sarvāṃś cāto grahān ā dhruvāt
12.13.6	samānabrāhmaṇāv upāṃśvantaryāmau sābhicaraṇikau
12.13.7	etāvan nānā / upayāmagṛhīto 'sy antar yaccheti gṛhītvottareṇa hotāram atikrāmati / yena vā hotā pratipādayed uttarato 'vasthāyottaraṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavahṛtyottarārdhe juhoti
12.13.8	viparītau deśāv eke samāmananti
12.13.9	asarvam āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ saṃpātam avanīyaiṣa te yonir apānāya tvety ariktaṃ pātram āyatane sādayitvā vyānāya tveti te antareṇa grāvāṇam upāṃśusavanaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaṃ saṃspṛṣṭaṃ pātrābhyām
12.13.10	yaṃ kāmayeta pramāyukaḥ syād ity asaṃspṛṣṭau tasyety uktam
12.13.11	nānudite sūrya upāṃśuṃ juhuyād udite 'ntaryāmam
12.13.12	yadi tvaretānudita upāṃśuṃ juhuyād udite 'ntaryāmam
12.13.13	ubhāv anudite hotavyāv ity eke
12.14.1	yadi rathaṃtarasāmā somaḥ syād aindravāyavāgrān gṛhṇīyāt / yadi bṛhatsāmā śukrāgrān / yadi jagatsāmāgrayaṇāgrān
12.14.2	yady ubhayasāmā yāthākāmī
12.14.3	api vaindravāyavāgrān eva
12.14.4	aindravāyavāgrān gṛhṇīyād yaḥ kāmayeta yathāpūrvaṃ prajāḥ kalperann iti / kāmyāni grahāgrāṇi
12.14.5	yān prācīnam āgrayaṇād ity uktam
12.14.6	yaṃ kāmyam aindravāyavāt pūrvaṃ gṛhṇīyān na sādayet
12.14.7	aindravāyavasya sādanam anusādyate
12.14.8	aindravāyavaṃ gṛhṇāti
12.14.9	ā vāyo bhūṣa śucipā ity anudrutyopayāmagṛhīto 'si vāyave tveti gṛhītvopayamyendravāyū ime sutā ity anudrutyopayāmagṛhīto 'sīndravāyubhyāṃ tveti gṛhītvā pavitradaśābhiḥ parimṛjyaiṣa te yoniḥ sajoṣābhyāṃ tveti sādayati
12.14.10	sarvān grahān pavitradaśābhiḥ parimṛjyaiṣa te yonir iti yathādevaṃ yathāyatanaṃ sādayati
12.14.11	etadarthaṃ vā dvitīyaṃ pavitraṃ daśāvat syāt
12.14.12	ayaṃ vāṃ mitrāvaruṇeti maitrāvaruṇaṃ gṛhītvā rāyā vayaṃ sasavāṃso madema havyena devā yavasena gāvaḥ / tāṃ dhenuṃ mitrāvaruṇā yuvaṃ no viśvāhā dhattam anapasphurantīm iti śṛtaśītena payasā śrītvaiṣa te yonir ṛtāyubhyāṃ tveti sādayati
12.14.13	ayaṃ venaś codayad iti śukraṃ gṛhītvā hiraṇyena śrītvaiṣa te yonir vīratāṃ pāhīti sādayati
12.14.14	śaṇḍāya tveti dveṣyasya
12.14.15	taṃ pratnatheti manthinaṃ gṛhītvā mano na yeṣu havaneṣu juhvad vipaḥ śacyā vanutho dravantā / ā yaḥ śaryābhistuvinṛmṇo asyāśrīṇītādiśaṃ gabhastāv iti saktubhiḥ śrīṇāty anabhidhvaṃsayann ātmānam / itarāṃś ca grahān
12.14.16	eṣa te yoniḥ prajāḥ pāhīti sādayati
12.15.1	markāya tveti dveṣyasya
12.15.2	yadi kāmayeta yo grāme taṃ grāmān nirūheyaṃ yo bahir grāmāt taṃ grāme kuryām itīdam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyā viśa udūhāmīti śukram udūhyedam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyāṃ viśi sādayāmīti tasmin manthinaṃ sādayet
12.15.3	ye devā divīty upariṣṭād upayāmayā purastād upayāmena vā yajuṣā dvābhyāṃ dhārābhyāṃ sthālyāgrayaṇaṃ gṛhṇāti
12.15.4	ya āgrayaṇasthālyāṃ somas tam anyasmin pātra ānīya tāṃ dvitīyāṃ dhārāṃ karoti
12.15.5	triṃśat trayaś ceti rugṇavatyarcā bhrātṛvyavato 'bhicarato vā gṛhṇīyāt
12.15.6	vidad yatī saramā rugṇam adrer mahi pāthaḥ pūrvyaṃ sadhriyakkaḥ / agraṃ nayat supady akṣarāṇām acchā ravaṃ prathamā jānatī gād iti vābhicarataḥ
12.15.7	āgrayaṇaṃ gṛhītvā trir hiṅkṛtya vācaṃ visṛjate
12.15.8	somaḥ pavate somaḥ pavate somaḥ pavate subhūtāya pavate brahmavarcasāya pavate 'smai brahmaṇe pavate 'smai kṣatrāya pavate 'syai viśe pavate 'dbhyaḥ pavata oṣadhībhyaḥ pavate vanaspatibhyaḥ pavate dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ pavate 'smai sunvate yajamānāya pavate mahyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyāya pavate / yathā devebhyo 'pavathā evaṃ mahyaṃ pavasveti trir udvadati śanair uccair atha sūccaiḥ
12.15.9	eṣa te yonir viśvebhyas tvā devebhya iti sādayitvā trīn agniṣṭome 'tigrāhyān gṛhṇāti / āgneyam aindraṃ sauryam iti
12.15.10	agna āyūṃṣy uttiṣṭhaṃs taraṇir iti grahaṇasādanāḥ
12.15.11	sthālyokthyaṃ gṛhṇāti / upayāmagṛhīto 'sīndrāya tvā bṛhadvate vayasvata iti grahaṇasādanau
12.16.1	mūrdhānaṃ divo aratiṃ pṛthivyā iti sthālyā dhruvaṃ pūrṇaṃ gṛhṇāti
12.16.2	alpaṃ gṛhṇīyād yaṃ kāmayeta pramāyukaḥ syād iti / uparyardhaṃ yaṃ kāmayetottaram āyur iyād iti
12.16.3	eṣa te yonir agnaye tvā vaiśvānarāyety āyatane hiraṇye sādayed āyuṣkāmasya
12.16.4	taṃ rājaputro gopāyāty āvanayanāt
12.16.5	yadi kāmayetāvagatam aparundhyur aparuddho 'vagacched itīdam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyā viśa utkhidāmīti dhruvam utkhidyedam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyāṃ viśi sādayāmīti tatraiva punaḥ sādayet
12.16.6	yad evaṃ kuryād āyuḥ prajānāṃ vicālayet / tṛṇam etena mantreṇoparyupary atiharet
12.16.7	yady abhicared idam aham amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasyāyuḥ pravartayāmīti dhruvaṃ pravartayet
12.16.8	dhruvaṃ tvā dhruvakṣitim amum ā sthānāc cyāvayāmīti vā vyaṅgayet
12.16.9	atra dhārā viramati
12.16.10	prapīḍya pavitraṃ nidadhāti
12.16.11	ekadhanānāṃ yathārthaṃ sarvāś ca maitrāvaruṇacamasīyā ādhavanīye 'vanīya pūtabhṛto bila udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitraṃ vitatya ya ādhavanīye rājā tam asarvaṃ pūtabhṛty avanīyopayāmagṛhīto 'si prajāpataye tveti droṇakalaśam abhimṛśet / indrāya tvety ādhavanīyam / viśvebhyas tvā devebhya iti pūtabhṛtam
12.16.12	te pavamānagrahāḥ
12.16.13	purastād upayāmāḥ sarve
12.16.14	pañcahotrā yajamānaḥ sarvān grahān abhimṛśati
12.16.15	drapsaś caskanda yas te drapso yo drapso yas te drapsa ity etaiḥ pratimantraṃ vaipruṣān homāñ juhoti
12.16.16	prathamaṃ sarvatrānuṣaktam uttarāṃs trīn vihṛtān anusavanam eke samāmananti
12.16.17	saptahotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ hutvodañcaḥ prahvā bahiṣpavamānāya pañcartvijaḥ samanvārabdhāḥ sarpanti
12.17.1	adhvaryuṃ prastotānvārabhate prastotāraṃ pratihartā pratihartāram udgātodgātāraṃ brahmā brahmāṇaṃ yajamānaḥ
12.17.2	yady u vai svayaṃ hotā yajamānaḥ syāt sarped eva / aupagātraṃ hy asyeti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
12.17.3	tsaranta iva rehāṇā iva nyaṅṅ iva śīrṣāṇi kṛtvā sarpanti
12.17.4	mṛga iva hi yajñaḥ / pūrvo 'dhvaryur barhirmuṣṭiṃ dhūnvan sarpati vāg agregā agra etv iti gāyatraḥ panthā vasavo devatāvṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasti vasūn aśīyeti
12.17.5	cātvālam avekṣamāṇāḥ stuvate / uttare vā vedyaṃse
12.17.6	athādhvaryuḥ stotram upākaroti
12.17.7	vāyur hiṅkarteti prastotre barhirmuṣṭiṃ prayacchati
12.17.8	sarveṣu pavamāneṣv evam upākaraṇaḥ
12.17.9	asarjy asarji vāg asarjy aindraṃ saho 'sarjy upāvartadhvam iti barhirbhyām anyāni pavamānebhyaḥ stotrāṇy upākaroti
12.17.10	tasmād brāhmaṇena bahiṣpavamāna upasadyaḥ / pavitraṃ hi / yaṃ dviṣyāt taṃ bahiṣpavamānāt paribādheteti vijñāyate
12.17.11	stūyamānaṃ yajamāna upagāyati / catvāro 'varārdhyā upagātāraḥ
12.17.12	nādhvaryuḥ
12.17.13	vasvyai hiṅkuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai stuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastād bahiṣpavamānād yajamāno japati
12.17.14	daśahotāraṃ ca vyācaṣṭe / stūyamāne ca daśahotāraṃ japati
12.17.15	śyeno 'si gāyatracchandā iti madhyamāyāṃ ca stotrīyāyām anvāroham
12.17.16	dvitīye pavamāne dvitīyena mantreṇa / tṛtīye tṛtīyena
12.17.17	athātyantapradeśaḥ / stutasya stutam asīti stotram anumantrayate / śastrasya śastram asīti śastram
12.17.18	indriyāvanto vanāmaha ity ubhayatrānuṣajati
12.17.19	stute 'dhvaryuḥ sampreṣyaty agnīd agnīn vihara barhi stṛṇāhi puroḍāśāṁ alaṃkurv iti
12.17.20	athaikeṣām / stuta uttiṣṭhann āhāgnīd agnīn vihara barhi stṛṇīhi puroḍāśāṁ alaṃkuru pratiprasthātaḥ paśunehīti
12.17.21	saṃpraiṣavat kurvanti
12.18.1	āgnīdhrād dhiṣṇiyān viharati
12.18.2	aṅgārair dve savane / śalākābhis tṛtīyam
12.18.3	pāṃsudhiṣṇiyeṣu nivapati
12.18.4	tenānupūrvyeṇa yathānyuptā bhavanti
12.18.5	pracaraṇyāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā droṇakalaśāc ca pariplavayā rājānaṃ purastāt pratyaṅṅ āsīno dhiṣṇiyān vyāghārayati tair eva mantraiḥ / tūṣṇīṃ vā
12.18.6	āhavanīyam āgnīdhrīyaṃ hotrīyaṃ mārjālīyam iti somena / ājyenetarān
12.18.7	yajñasya saṃtatir asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatyai stṝṇāmi saṃtatyai tvā yajñasyeti gārhapatyāt prakramya saṃtatam anupṛṣṭhyaṃ barhiḥ stṛṇāty āhavanīyāt
12.18.8	vaiṣṇavyarcā punar etya yajamāno rājānam upatiṣṭhate viṣṇo tvaṃ no antama iti
12.18.9	etayaivādhvaryuḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśyāśvinaṃ gṛhṇāti
12.18.10	yā vāṃ kaśeti grahaṇasādanau
12.18.11	droṇakalaśād adhārāgrahāḥ pariplavayā gṛhyante / vacanād anyataḥ
12.18.12	trivṛtā yūpaṃ parivīyāgneyaṃ savanīyaṃ paśum upākaroti
12.18.13	aindrāgnam ukthye / aindraṃ ṣoḍaśini / sārasvatam atirātre
12.18.14	samabhyuccayavad eke samāmananti / āgneyam agniṣṭoma ālabhate / aindrāgnam ukthye dvitīyam / aindraṃ vṛṣṇiṃ ṣoḍaśini tṛtīyam / sārasvatīṃ meṣīṃ caturthīm atirātre
12.18.15	ā vapāyāḥ kṛtvā hutāyāṃ vapāyāṃ mārjayitvā prātaḥsavanāya saṃprasarpanti
12.18.16	prasrapsyanto grahān avekṣante
12.18.17	dvau samudrāv iti pūtabhṛdādhavanīyau
12.18.18	dve dradhasī iti droṇakalaśam
12.18.19	paribhūr agnim iti sarvaṃ rājānam
12.18.20	prāṇāya ma ity upāṃśum / apānāya ma ity antaryāmam / vyānāya ma ity upāṃśusavanam / vāce ma ity aindravāyavam / dakṣakratubhyām ma iti maitrāvaruṇam / cakṣurbhyāṃ na iti śukrāmanthinau / śrotrāya ma ity āśvinam / ātmane ma ity āgrayaṇam / aṅgebhyo ma ity ukthyam / āyuṣe ma iti dhruvam / tejase me varcodā varcase pavasvety ājyāni / paśubhyo me varcodā varcase pavasveti pṛṣadājyam / puṣṭyai me varcodāḥ pavadhvam iti sarvān grahān / stanābhyāṃ me varcodau varcase me pavethām ity ṛtupātre / tejase ma ojase me varcase me vīryāya me varcodā varcase pavasvety etaiḥ pratimantram atigrāhyān ṣoḍaśinam iti / viṣṇor jaṭharam asīti droṇakalaśam / indrasyety ādhavanīyam / viśveṣāṃ devānām iti pūtabhṛtam
12.19.1	ko 'si ko nāmety āhavanīyam
12.19.2	soma tvāṃ vṛṇīmaha udgātāraṃ nṛcakṣasaṃ pārayā ṇa svastaye / viśvebhyo me rūpebhya iti sarvaṃ rājānam
12.19.3	bubhūṣann avekṣeta / brahmavarcasakāma āmayāvy abhicaran vā
12.19.4	śṛtaṃkārair yajamānaḥ sarvān grahān upatiṣṭhate
12.19.5	śṛtau sthaḥ prāṇāpānau me śrīṇītam ity upāṃśvantaryāmau / śṛto 'si vyānaṃ me śrīṇāhīty upāṃśusavanam / śṛto 'si vācaṃ me śrīṇāhīty aindravāyavam / śṛto 'si dakṣakratū me śrīṇāhīti maitrāvaruṇam / śṛtau sthaś cakṣuṣī me śrīṇītam iti śukrāmanthinau / śṛto 'si śrotraṃ me śrīṇāhīty āśvinam / śṛto 'sy ātmānaṃ me śrīṇāhīty āgrayaṇam / śṛto 'sy aṅgāni me śrīṇāhīty ukthyam / śṛto 'sy āyur me śrīṇāhīti dhruvam / śṛtam asi tejo me śrīṇāhīty ājyāni / śṛtam asi paśūn me śrīṇāhīti pṛṣadājyam / śṛtā stha puṣṭiṃ me śrīṇīyeti sarvān grahān / prajāpater jaṭharam asi śṛto 'si sa mā śrīṇāhīti droṇakalaśam / indrasya jaṭharam asi śṛto 'si sa mā śrīṇāhīty ādhavanīyam / viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ jaṭharam asi śṛto 'si sa mā śrīṇāhīti pūtabhṛtam / śṛtas tvaṃ śṛto 'haṃ śṛto me prāṇaḥ śṛto me 'pānaḥ śṛto me vyānaḥ śṛtaṃ me cakṣuḥ śṛtaṃ me śrotraṃ śṛtā me vāk śṛto ma ātmā śṛtaṃ me haviḥ śṛto me somaḥ śṛtā me grahāḥ // imam indra sutaṃ piba jyeṣṭham amartyaṃ madam / śukrasya tvābhyakṣaran dhārā ṛtasya sādane // vṛṣā soma dyumāṁ asi vṛṣā deva vṛṣavrataḥ / vṛṣā dharmāṇi dadhiṣe // vṛṣṇas te vṛṣṇyaṃ śavo vṛṣā vane vṛṣā made / sa tvaṃ vṛṣan vṛṣed asi // aśvo na cakrado vṛṣā saṃ gā indo samarvataḥ / vi no rāye duro vṛdhīti sarvaṃ rājānam
12.19.6	agniḥ pavitraṃ sa mā punātu / somaḥ pavitraṃ sa mā punātu / sūryaḥ pavitraṃ sa mā punātu / upahūtā gāva upahūto 'haṃ gavām ity etair yathāliṅgam upasthāya sphyaḥ svastir ity utkare vedikaraṇāni parāsyopatiṣṭhate
12.19.7	upa mā dyāvāpṛthivī iti dyāvāpṛthivī / upāstāva iti bahiṣpavamānāstāvam
12.20.1	kalaśa iti kalaśam / soma iti somam / agnir ity agnim / upa devā iti devān / upa yajña iti yajñam / upa mā hotrā iti hotrakān
12.20.2	hvayetāṃ hvayatāṃ hvayantām iti yathāliṅgaṃ sarvatrānuṣajati
12.20.3	namo 'ganaye makhaghna ity āhavanīyam / namo rudrāya makhaghna ity āgnīdhrīyam / nama indrāya makhaghna iti hotrīyam
12.20.4	dṛḍhe sthaḥ śithire samīcī iti dyāvāpṛthivī upatiṣṭhate / sūryaṃ vāyum agniṃ yamaṃ sarasvatīṃ sadaso dvārāv iti
12.20.5	pātaṃ pātv iti yathāliṅgaṃ sarvatrānuṣajati
12.20.6	draṣṭre nama iti prasrapsyañ japati / upadraṣṭre nama iti prasṛpya
12.20.7	apareṇa brahmasadanaṃ yajamānāyatanam / pūrveṇa vā
12.20.8	namaḥ sadasa iti sado namaḥ sadasaspataya iti brahmāṇaṃ namaḥ sakhīnāṃ purogāṇām ity ṛtvijo namo dive namaḥ pṛthivyā iti dyāvāpṛthivī upasthāyāhe daidhiṣavyety āyatanāt tṛṇaṃ nirasyonnivata ududvataś ca geṣam ity upaviśati
12.20.9	pātaṃ mā dyāvāpṛthivī adyāhna ity upaviśya japati
12.20.10	āganta pitaraḥ pitṛmān iti dakṣiṇārdhaṃ parekṣate
12.20.11	ubhāv etāni japato 'dhvaryur yajamānaś ca / api vā yajamāna eva
12.20.12	atra pratiprasthātā savanīyān āsādayati
12.20.13	tair adhvaryuḥ pracarati
12.20.14	sarveṣāṃ puroḍāśānāṃ juhvāṃ daivatāni samavadyati / upabhṛti sauviṣṭakṛtāni
12.20.15	prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśānām anubrūhi prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśānāṃ preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau / prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśānām avadīyamānānām anubrūhi prātaḥ prātahsāvasyendrāya puroḍāśān prasthitān preṣyeti vā
12.20.16	agnaye 'nubrūhy agnaye preṣyeti sviṣṭakṛtaḥ saṃpraiṣo
12.20.17	prāśitram avadāyeḍāṃ na yajamānabhāgam
12.20.18	hotra iḍāṃ hṛtvā havirdhānaṃ gacchan saṃpreṣyati vāyava indravāyubhyām anubrūhīti
12.20.19	upayāmagṛhīto 'si vākṣasad asīty ādityapātreṇa pratiprasthātā droṇakalaśād aindravāyavasya pratinigrāhyaṃ gṛhītvā na sādayati
12.20.20	aindravāyavam ādāyādhvaryur droṇakalaśāc ca pariplavayā rājānam ubhau niṣkramya dakṣiṇato 'vasthāya dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavahṛtyādhvaro yajño 'yam astu devā iti pariplavayāghāram āghārayati yathopāṃśur huto bhavati
12.20.21	atra sarvāḥ somāhutīr juhoti
12.20.22	yato manyetānabhikramya hoṣyāmīti tat tiṣṭhan srucaṃ vāyavyaṃ camasaṃ vānvārabhyāśrāvayet / grahaṃ vā gṛhītvā camasaṃ vonnīya stotram upākuryād ity atyantapradeśaḥ
12.20.23	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati vāyava indravāyubhyāṃ preṣyeti
12.20.24	vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti / punarvaṣaṭkṛte juhutaḥ
12.20.25	yadi manyeta yajamānaḥ pūrvo mātikrānto bhrātṛvya iti
12.21.1	prāg ghomād aṅguṣṭhenāṅgulim avagṛhṇīyād yo na indravāyū abhidāsatīti / yadi vāparo 'ṅgulyāṅguṣṭham
12.21.2	hute cādityam upatiṣṭhate bhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmīnāṃ prāṇapāḥ prāṇaṃ me pāhīti
12.21.3	athādhvaryoḥ pātre pratiprasthātā saṃpātam avanayati / adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātuḥ / etad vā viparītam
12.21.4	devebhyas tvety ādityapātreṇa pratiprasthātādityasthālyāṃ saṃpātam avanayati
12.21.5	graham adhvaryur ādāya kṣipraṃ hotāram abhidrutya mayi vasur iti grahaṃ hotre prayacchati
12.21.6	etenaiva hotā pratigṛhya dakṣiṇa ūrāv āsādya hastābhyāṃ nigṛhyāste
12.21.7	evam uttarābhyāṃ grahābhyāṃ pracarataḥ
12.21.8	āghārapunarvaṣaṭkārau na bhavataḥ
12.21.9	yathādevataṃ saṃpraiṣāḥ
12.21.10	grahaṇaṃ pratinigrāhyāṇām avagrahaṇādityopasthānāvanayanapradānāny uttarottarair mantraiḥ
12.21.11	vibhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmīnāṃ vyānapā vyānaṃ me pāhīti tṛtīya ādityopasthānaḥ
12.21.12	viṣṇav urukramaiṣa te somas taṃ rakṣasvety ādityapātreṇa pratiprasthātādityasthālīm apidadhāti
12.21.13	āśvinaṃ hotre pradāya havirdhānaṃ gacchan saṃpreṣyaty unnīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhīti
12.21.14	hotṛcamasamukhyān nava camasān unnayati
12.21.15	droṇakalaśād upastīrya pūtabhṛta unnīya droṇakalaśād abhighārayati
12.21.16	sarvacamasānām eṣa kalpaḥ
12.21.17	dhārāgrahaṇakāle dvidevatyānāṃ kāmyāḥ kalpāḥ
12.21.18	yadi manyeta yajamānaḥ pūrvo mātikrānto bhrātṛvya iti pratiprasthānena pūrvo gṛhītvā pūrvo hutvā pūrvaḥ sādayet
12.21.19	yadi kāmayeta samāvadvīryam enaṃ bhrātṛvyeṇa kuryām iti prabāhug gṛhītvā prabāhuk tiṣṭhadbhyāṃ hotavyam / prabāhug ghutvā prabāhuk sādayeyātām
12.21.20	samam ity arthaḥ
12.21.21	yadi kāmayetāvagatam aparundhyur aparuddho 'vagacched itīdam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyā viśa udūhāmīty adhvaryupātram udūhyedam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣya putram amuṣyāṃ viśi sādayāmīti tasmin pratiprasthānaṃ sādayet
12.21.22	kāmyāś cet pṛthakyātraiḥ pratinigrāhyā gṛhyeran
12.22.1	tataḥ śukrāmanthibhyāṃ pracarataḥ / stuto 'si janadhā devās tvā śukrapāḥ praṇayantv iti śukram adhvaryur ādatte / stuto 'si janadhā devās tvā manthipāḥ praṇayantv iti manthinaṃ pratiprasthātā / camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ
12.22.2	tau prokṣitābhyāṃ śakalābhyām apidhāyāprokṣitābhyām adhastāt pāṃsūn apadhvaṃsayato 'panuttau śaṇḍāmarkau sahāmuneti / apanuttaḥ śaṇḍa iti vādhvaryur dveṣyaṃ manasā dhyāyan / apanutto marka iti pratiprasthātā
12.22.3	tāv apigṛhya prāñcau niṣkrāmataḥ
12.22.4	urv antarikṣam anvihīty abhipravrajataḥ
12.22.5	indreṇa manyunā yujāvabādhe pṛtanyatā / ghnatā vṛtrāṇy apratīti śukraṃ yajamāno 'nvārabhata ā homāt
12.22.6	apareṇottaravediṃ grahāv aratnī vā saṃdhatto brahma saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ kṣattraṃ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvatam iṣaṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam ūrjaṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvataṃ rayiṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvataṃ puṣṭiṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvataṃ prajāṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvataṃ paśūn saṃdhattaṃ tān me jinvatam iti
12.22.7	anādhṛṣṭāsīty aṅguṣṭhābhyām uttaravedim avagṛhya vyapariphantāv ivottaravediṃ parikrāmataḥ
12.22.8	suvīrāḥ prajāḥ prajanayan parīhi śukraḥ śukraśociṣeti dakṣiṇenādhvaryuḥ pratipadyate / suprajāḥ prajāḥ prajanayan parīhi manthī manthiśociṣety uttareṇa pratiprasthātā / agreṇottaravediṃ grahāv aratnī vā saṃdhattaḥ saṃjagmānau diva ā pṛthivyā āyuḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ prāṇaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvatam apānaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvataṃ vyānaṃ saṃdhattaṃ taṃ me jinvataṃ cakṣuḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ śrotraṃ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ manaḥ saṃdhattaṃ tan me jinvataṃ vācaṃ saṃdhattaṃ tāṃ me jinvatam iti
12.22.9	athaināv adhvaryur abhimantrayata āyu stha āyur me dhattam āyur yajñāya dhattam āyur yajñapataye dhattaṃ prāṇa sthaḥ prāṇaṃ me dhattaṃ prāṇaṃ yajñāya dhattaṃ prāṇaṃ yajñapataye dhattaṃ cakṣu sthaś cakṣur me dhattaṃ cakṣur yajñāya dhattaṃ cakṣur yajñapataye dhattaṃ śrotraṃ sthaḥ śrotraṃ me dhattaṃ śrotraṃ yajñāya dhattaṃ śrotraṃ yajñapataye dhattam
12.23.1	tau devau śukrāmanthinau kalpayataṃ daivīr viśaḥ kalpayataṃ mānuṣīr iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dhattaṃ prāṇān paśuṣu prajāṃ mayi ca yajamāne ceti
12.23.2	aprokṣitau śakalau bahirvedi nirasyato nirastau śaṇḍāmarkau sahāmuneti / nirastaḥ śaṇḍa iti vādhvaryur dveṣyaṃ manasā dhyāyan / nirasto marka iti pratiprasthātā
12.23.3	prokṣitāv ādhattaḥ / śukrasya samid asīty adhvaryuḥ / manthinaḥ samid asīti pratiprasthātā
12.23.4	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati prātaḥ prātaḥsāvasya śukravato manthivato madhuścuta indrāya somān prasthitān preṣya madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasādhvaryavo vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛtāñ juhuta hotrakāṇāṃ camasādhvaryavaḥ sakṛtsakṛddhutvā śukrasyābhyunnīyopāvartadhvam iti
12.23.5	saṃpraiṣavat kurvanti
12.23.6	purastāt pratyañcāv adhvaryū juhutaḥ / paścāt prāñcaś camasaiś camasādhvaryavo juhvati
12.23.7	śukrāmanthinoḥ pratinigadya homaḥ
12.23.8	sa prathamaḥ saṃkṛtir viśvakarmā sa prathamo mitro varuṇo agniḥ / sa prathamo bṛhaspatiś cikitvāṃs tasmā indrāya sutam ājuhomi svāhety adhvaryur juhoti / tasmai sūryāya sutam ājuhomi svāheti pratiprasthātā
12.23.9	sānuvaṣaṭkārāv ananuvaṣaṭkārau vā
12.23.10	sarvahutau
12.23.11	api vā sūdavac chukrapātram āyatane sādayitvottarārdhāt pratiprasthātā bahiḥparidhy aṅgāraṃ nirvartya tasmin manthinaḥ saṃsrāvaṃ juhoty eṣa te rudra bhāgo yaṃ nirayācathā iti
12.23.12	ārtapātram etad yan manthipātram / yam ṛtvijāṃ dviṣyāt tasmai haret / ārchatīhaiveti vijñāyate
12.23.13	tataḥ saṃpreṣyati praitu hotuś camasaḥ pra brahmaṇaḥ prodgātuḥ pra yajamānasya / prodgātṝṇām ity eke samāmananti / pra sadasyasya / prayantu sadasyānām iti vā
12.23.14	atha hotrāḥ saṃyājayanti
12.23.15	tasmai camasādhvaryavaḥ svaṃ svaṃ camasaṃ droṇakalaśād abhyunnīya haranti
12.23.16	maitrāvaruṇacamasam ādāyāhavanīyaṃ gatvāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati hotar yaja praśāstar iti vā
12.23.17	vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā harati bhakṣam
12.23.18	evam uttaraiḥ pracarati / etāvan nānā
12.24.1	brahman yajeti dvitīye saṃpreṣyati / potar yajeti tṛtīye / neṣṭar yajeti caturthe / agnīd yajeti pañcame
12.24.2	sarvatrānuvaṣaṭkāro dvidevatyartugrahādityasāvitrapātnīvatavarjam
12.24.3	āgnīdhracamasam ādāya sada etyāyāḍ agnīd ity ācaṣṭe
12.24.4	sa bhadram akar yo naḥ somaṃ pāyayiṣyatītītare pratyāhuḥ
12.24.5	yadi rājanyaṃ vaiśyaṃ vā yājayet sa yadi somaṃ bibhakṣayiṣen nyagrodhastibhinīr āhṛtya saṃpiṣya dadhany unmṛjya camaseṣu hūyamāneṣv antaḥparidhy aṅgāraṃ nirvartyaitasya camasasya darbhataruṇenopahatyāhaṃ tvad asmi mad asi tvam ity aṅgāre hutvā tam asmai bhakṣaṃ prayacchet
12.24.6	pātre samavetānāṃ vaṣaṭkartā pūrvo bhakṣayati
12.24.7	bhakṣehīti bhakṣam āhriyamāṇaṃ pratīkṣyāśvinos tvā bāhubhyāṃ saghyāsam iti pratigṛhya nṛcakṣasaṃ tvā deva somety avekṣya mandrābhibhūtir iti prātaḥsavane sarvān aindrān bhakṣayati / narāśaṃsapītasyeti nārāśaṃsān / rudravadgaṇasyeti mādhyaṃdine savane sarvān aindrān bhakṣayati / narāśaṃsapītasyeti nārāśaṃsān / ādityavadgaṇasyeti tṛtīyasavane sarvān aindrān bhakṣayati / narāśaṃsapītasyeti nārāśaṃsān
12.24.8	yat prāg vasumadgaṇāt tat sarvatrānuṣajati
12.24.9	apy anyadevatān indrapītasyeti
12.24.10	yathādevataṃ vā
12.24.11	vāg juṣāṇā somasya tṛpyatv iti sarvasomānāṃ bhakṣaṇam eke samāmananti
12.24.12	vāg devī somasya tṛpyatv iti vā
12.24.13	hinva me gātrā hariva iti bhakṣayitvā nābhideśān abhimṛśante
12.24.14	nānupahūtena somaḥ pātavai / somapīthena ha vyardhuko bhavati
12.24.15	asāvasāv upahvayasveti karmanāmadheyenāmantrayate / upahūta iti prativacanaḥ
12.24.16	ye samāne prāye bhakṣayanti teṣūpahavam icchate
12.24.17	ye vaikapātram
12.25.1	purastād aindravāyavaṃ bhakṣayati prāṇeṣūpanigrāham / purastān maitrāvaruṇaṃ cakṣuṣor upanigrāham / sarvataḥ parihāram āśvinaṃ śrotrayor upanigrāham
12.25.2	avyutsṛjantau pātraṃ dvir aindravāyavaṃ bhakṣayato bhakṣayanti bhakṣayati vā / sakṛtsakṛd itarau
12.25.3	tad yeṣāṃ bhakṣayata ity adhvaryur hotā cety arthaḥ / bhakṣayantīty adhvaryū hotā cety arthaḥ / bhakṣayatīti sasa ity arthaḥ
12.25.4	bhakṣayitvā hotṛcamase saṃpātān avanayato bhakṣitān abhakṣite
12.25.5	atra pātraṃ vyutsṛjataḥ
12.25.6	puroḍāśaśakalam aindravāyavasya pātre 'vadadhāti / payasyāṃ maitrāvaruṇasya / dhānā āśvinasya
12.25.7	tāni dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyottarasyāṃ vartanyāṃ sādayati / ā tṛtīyasavanāt pariśere yajñasya saṃtatyā iti vijñāyate
12.25.8	atreḍāyā niravadānam eke samāmananti
12.25.9	atra hoteḍām upahvayate / upodyacchante camasāṃś camasinaḥ / hotṛcamasam iḍāyām āspṛṣṭam
12.25.10	upahūtāṃ prāśnanti ye prakṛtau
12.25.11	puroḍāśaśakalam acchāvākāya nidadhāti
12.25.12	āgnīdhre haviḥśeṣān bhakṣayanti
12.25.13	atra savanīyānāṃ śākhāpraharaṇaṃ vājinacaryāntarvedi yajamānasya vedābhimarśanaṃ piṣṭalepaphalīkaraṇahomau patnyā vedaprāsanaṃ praṇītāsu mārjanam upaveṣodasanaṃ kapālavimocanam iti kriyante
12.25.14	nahy eteṣāṃ prāsaṅgikaṃ vaiśeṣikam utkarṣati
12.25.15	utkarṣed ity aparam
12.25.16	vaṣaṭkāreṇa hotā bhakṣaṃ labhate
12.25.17	homābhiṣavābhyām adhvaryuḥ / nānyatareṇa
12.25.18	samākhyānenāpi bhakṣaṃ labhante
12.25.19	sarvāṃś camasān sakṛddhotā bhakṣayati
12.25.20	dviḥ svaṃ camasam
12.25.21	hotrakāḥ svaṃ svaṃ camasaṃ dvir bhakṣayanti
12.25.22	tān adhvaryuḥ sakṛdbhakṣitān yathāpūrvaṃ pratibhakṣayati
12.25.23	antata itare
12.25.24	bhakṣitān āpyāyayanty āpyāyasva sametu ta iti
12.25.25	te nārāśaṃsāḥ
12.25.26	dvinārāśaṃse pūrve savane bhavataḥ / ekanārāśaṃsaṃ tṛtīyasavanam
12.25.27	bhakṣitāpyāyitān sādayanti dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyādhastād avālambe
12.26.1	upaviśaty acchāvāko bahiḥ sadaso 'greṇa svaṃ dhiṣṇiyam
12.26.2	tasmai puroḍāśaśakalam ādadhad āhācchāvāka vadasva yat te vādyam iti
12.26.3	yadāsya vijānāty upo asmān brāhmaṇān brāhmaṇā hvayadhvam ity athainaṃ hotra āvedayaty acchāvāko vā ayam upahavam icchate taṃ hotar upahvayasveti
12.26.4	uta no gāva upahūtā upahūteti hotur abhijñāyonnīyamānāyānubrūhy acchāvākasya camasādhvaryo unnayasvobhayataḥ śukraṃ kuruṣveti
12.26.5	tam ādāyāhavanīyaṃ gatvāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyaty acchāvāka yajeti
12.26.6	vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā harati bhakṣam
12.26.7	tena na saṃbhakṣayati / nāsminn upahavam icchate / yady asminn upahavam iccheta bhakṣayety enaṃ brūyāt
12.26.8	bhakṣitāpyāyitam antarā neṣṭur āgnīdhrasya ca camasau sādayitvartugrahaiḥ pracarataḥ
12.26.9	droṇakalaśād gṛhyante / na sādyante
12.26.10	pūrveṣāṃ śeṣeṣūttarān abhigṛhṇītaḥ
12.26.11	pūrvo 'dhvaryur gṛhṇāti jaghanyaḥ pratiprasthātopayāmagṛhīto 'si madhuś cety etaiḥ pratimantram
12.26.12	madhave tvā mādhavāya tvety eke samāmananti
12.26.13	purastād upayāmāḥ sarve
12.26.14	nānyo'nyam anuprapadyeta / prasiddham evādhvaryur dakṣiṇena prapadyate / prasiddhaṃ pratiprasthātottareṇa
12.26.15	dvāry eva vyatītaḥ
12.26.16	praviśantam evādhvaryuṃ pratiprasthātā graheṇa paripragṛhṇāti / niṣkrāmantaṃ pātreṇa
12.26.17	ṛtunā preṣyeti triṣv ādyeṣv adhvaryuḥ saṃpreṣyati / evaṃ pratiprasthātā
12.26.18	pātrayor mukhe paryāvṛtyartubhiḥ preṣyeti dvayor adhvaryuḥ / evaṃ pratiprasthātā
12.26.19	punaḥ paryāvṛtyartunā preṣyeti sakṛd adhvaryuḥ / evaṃ pratiprasthātā
12.27.1	dvādaśa trayodaśa caturdaśa vā gṛhyante
12.27.2	dvādaśasu saha prathamau gṛhyete / sahottamau
12.27.3	trayodaśasūttamayoḥ saha grahaṇapradāne
12.27.4	tathā caturdaśasu prathamottamayoḥ
12.27.5	saṃsarpo 'sy aṃhaspatyāya tveti trayodaśacaturdaśau vāvagṛhyete
12.27.6	adhvaryū yajataṃ gṛhapate yajety abhijñāyobhayatrātipreṣyati hotar etad yajeti
12.27.7	evaṃ gṛhapatiḥ sve praiṣānte
12.27.8	dvidevatyavat saṃpātau vyavanīyābhikṣitena pātreṇādhvaryur aindrāgnaṃ gṛhṇāti / indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti grahaṇasādanau / pratiprasthātā harati bhakṣam
12.27.9	ubhāv adhvaryū yathāvaṣaṭkṛtaṃ pratibhakṣayataḥ
12.27.10	sarveṣāṃ somapātrāṇāṃ bhakṣitānāṃ mārjālīye prakṣālanam
12.27.11	etat pātram ādāyādhvaryuḥ sadobile prāṅmukha upaviśyeḍā devahūr iti śastraṃ pratigariṣyañ japati
12.27.12	adhvaryo śoṃsāvom iti hotur abhijñāya pradakṣiṇam āvartamānaḥ śoṃsā moda iveti pratyāhvayate / śaṃsā moda iveti vā
12.27.13	ṛtupātraṃ dhārayamāṇaḥ sadobile pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan pratigṛṇāti / prahvo vā
12.27.14	othā moda ivety ardharceṣu / om othā moda ivety avasāneṣu / praṇava evāntaḥ
12.27.15	othā moda ivaṃ hotar moda ivam othā moda ivom iti vikalpante
12.27.16	nārdharcāl lupyate / nābhipratigṛṇāti
12.27.17	śoṃsā moda ivauthā moda iveti vyāhāveṣūbhayaṃ karoti
12.27.18	śastraṃ pratigīrya graham adhvaryur ādatte / camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ
12.27.19	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyaty ukthaśā yaja somasyeti / vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
12.28.1	anuprakampayanti nārāśaṃsān vaṣaṭkārānuvaṣaṭkārau
12.28.2	bhakṣān haranti
12.28.3	vyākhyāto grahasya bhakṣaḥ / tathā nārāśaṃsānāṃ bhakṣaṇāpyāyanasādanāni
12.28.4	vaiśvadevaṃ śukrapātreṇa gṛhṇāti / omāsaś carṣaṇīdhṛta iti grahaṇasādanau
12.28.5	asarjy asarjīti barhirbhyāṃ stotram upākaroti
12.28.6	iḍāyai hiṅkuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai stuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastād ājyānāṃ yajamāno japati caturhotāraṃ ca vyācaṣṭe
12.28.7	stūyamāne ca caturhotāraṃ japati
12.28.8	caturhotṝn vyākhyāyājyair udgāyatīti vijñāyate
12.28.9	stuta ṛtupātravarjam aindrāgnavac chastrapratigaro grahanārāśaṃsāś ca
12.28.10	sarvabhakṣāś camasā bhavanti
12.28.11	upayāmagṛhīto 'si mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmi devebhyo devāyuvam ukthyebhya ukthyāyuvam ity ukthyapātreṇokthyatṛtīyaṃ gṛhītvaiṣa te yonir mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tveti sādayitvā punar havir asīti sthālīm abhimṛśati
12.28.12	yan mukhyāś camasā bhavanti tasya pratigṛṇāti taṃ ca pratibhakṣayati
12.28.13	maitrāvaruṇacamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnīya pūrvavat stotram upākaroti
12.28.14	stute pūrvavac chastraṃ pratigīrya graham adhvaryur ādatte / camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ / āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyaty ukthaśā yaja somānām iti / vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛte juhvati / bhakṣān haranti
12.28.15	evam ata ūrdhvaṃ nārāśaṃsavarjaṃ gaṇeṣu caryā
12.28.16	devebhyas tvā devāyuvaṃ pṛṇajmi yajñasyāyuṣa iti mukhye saṃpātam avanayati
12.29.1	yadi kāmayetādhvaryur ātmānaṃ yajñayaśasenārpayeyam ity uktam
12.29.2	evaṃ vihitāv uttarau paryāyau
12.29.3	tābhyāṃ pratiprasthātā carati / etāvan nānā
12.29.4	indrāya tveti dvitīye grahaṇasādanau saṃnamaty ardhaṃ cokthyaśeṣasya gṛhṇāti / pūrvavat sthālīm abhimṛśati / brāhmaṇācchaṃsicamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnayati
12.29.5	nābhakṣitaṃ camasaṃ stotreṇābhyupākaroti
12.29.6	na pratiprasthātordhvapātrasya bhakṣayati
12.29.7	mukhye saṃpātam avanayati
12.29.8	indrāgnibhyāṃ tveti tṛtīye grahaṇasādanau saṃnamati sarvaṃ cokthyaśeṣaṃ gṛhṇāti / na sthālīm abhimṛśati
12.29.9	pūtabhṛto bila udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitraṃ vitatya ya ādhavanīye rājā taṃ sarvaṃ pūtabhṛty avanīyācchāvākacamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnayan sarvaṃ rājānam unnīya daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjati
12.29.10	mukhye saṃpātam avanayati
12.29.11	ukthaśā ity āha prātaḥsavanaṃ pratigīrya śastraṃśastraṃ vā
12.29.12	asaṃtvaramāṇāḥ pūrvābhyāṃ savanābhyāṃ caranti / saṃtvaramāṇās tṛtīyasavanena
12.29.13	agniḥ prātaḥsavane pātv asmān iti saṃsthite savana āhutiṃ juhoti
12.29.14	praśāstaḥ prasuva prasuhīti vā saṃpreṣyati
12.29.15	sarpateti pratyāha
12.29.16	yena prasarpanti tena niḥsarpanti
12.29.17	saṃtiṣṭhate prātaḥsavanaṃ prātaḥsavanam
13.1.1	abhiṣavādi mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ tāyate
13.1.2	tasya prātaḥsavanena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
13.1.3	hotṛcamasena vasatīvarībhyo niḥṣicya nigrābhyāḥ karoti
13.1.4	dvidevatyartugrahā darvihomāś ca na vidyante
13.1.5	visrasya rājānaṃ grāvastute somoṣṇīṣaṃ prayacchati
13.1.6	asaṃpreṣito grāvastotrīyā anvāha
13.1.7	tathaiva mahābhiṣavaḥ
13.1.8	ghoṣavāṃs tu
13.1.9	saṃrādhayantaś cābhiṣuṇvantīhā3 iheti
13.1.10	uttamasyābhiṣavasya madhyame paryāye bṛhad dadhati bṛhad bṛhad iti
13.1.11	uttame 'bhiṣave 'bhiṣave rājanyasaṃbhṛte devā grāvāṇa indur indra ity avādiṣuḥ / endram acucyavuḥ paramasyāḥ parāvataḥ / āsmāt sadhastād oror antarikṣāt / ā subhūtam asuṣavur brahmavarcasaṃ ma āsuṣavuḥ samare rakṣāṃsy avadhiṣur apahataṃ brahmajyasyeti pratiprasthātā grāvṇo 'numodate
13.1.12	paśupuroḍāśaṃ nirupya payasyāvarjaṃ savanīyāḥ
13.1.13	tena pracarya savanīyaiḥ pracarati
13.1.14	samānaṃ tu sviṣṭakṛdiḍam
13.1.15	sa kṛtākṛtaḥ
13.1.16	saṃbharaṇādy ā dhārāyāḥ kṛte 'dhvaryur grahān gṛhṇāti
13.2.1	śukrāmanthināv athāgrayaṇaṃ tisṛbhyo dhārābhyaḥ
13.2.2	āgrayaṇād utsicya dvitīyāṃ dhārāṃ karoti / udacanāt tṛtīyām
13.2.3	ukthyaṃ gṛhītvā marutvatīyau / etad vā viparītam / madhya ukthyam abhito marutvatīyāv ity eke
13.2.4	marutvantam iti svenartupātreṇādhvaryuḥ pūrvaṃ marutvatīyaṃ gṛhṇāti / indra marutva iti svena pratiprasthātottaram
13.2.5	tayor anyadevatāni grahaṇāni dveṣyasyaike samāmananti
13.2.6	viramati dhāraikadhanānāṃ yathārtham ity etadādy ā pañcahotuḥ
13.2.7	grahāvakāśaiḥ śṛtaṃkāraiś copasthāya vaipruṣān saptahotāraṃ ca hutvā bahiṣpavamānavan mādhyaṃdinaṃ pavamānaṃ sarpanti
13.2.8	traiṣṭubhaḥ panthā rudrā devatāvṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasti rudrān aśīyeti sarpaṇe vikāraḥ
13.2.9	uttareṇa havirdhānaṃ gatvā dakṣiṇena mārjālīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītya pūrvayā dvārā sadaḥ praviśyāgreṇa hotāram adhvaryur yajamānaś cāvatiṣṭhete / dakṣiṇenottareṇa vā praśāstur dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītyodgātāro mādhyaṃdinena pavamānena stuvate
13.3.1	jyotiṣe hiṅkuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai stuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastān mādhyaṃdināt pavamānād yajamāno japati / caturhotāraṃ pañcahotāraṃ vā vyācaṣṭe / jyoktyai hiṅkuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai stuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti ca / sūyamāne ca caturhotāraṃ pañcahotāraṃ cā japati / madhyamāyāṃ ca stotrīyāyāṃ dvitīyam anvāroham / stute 'dhvaryuḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnīd agnīn vihara barhi stṛṇīhi puroḍāśāṁ alaṃkuru pratiprasthātar dadhigharmeṇānūdehīti
13.3.2	āgnīdhre pratiprasthātā dadhigharmaṃ gṛhṇāti
13.3.3	audumbaryāṃ srucy upastīrya yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī iti dadhi gṛhītvābhighārya vāk ca tvā manaś ca śrīṇītāṃ prāṇaś ca tvāpānaś ca śrīṇītāṃ cakṣuś ca tvā śrotraṃ ca śrīṇītāṃ dakṣaś ca tvā balaṃ ca śrīṇītām ojaś ca tvā sahaś ca śrīṇītām āyuś ca tvā jarā ca śrīṇītām ātmā ca tvā tanūś ca śrīṇītāṃ śṛto 'si śṛtaṃkṛtaḥ śṛtāya tvā śṛtebhyas tvety āgnīdhrīye 'dhiśrityāha hotar vadasva yat te vādyam iti
13.3.4	yadāsya vijānāti yadi śrāto juhotana yady aśrāto mamattanety etasmin kāle śrātaṃ havir iti pratyuktvā tam ādāyāhavanīyaṃ gatvāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati
13.4.1	dadhigharmasya yajeti
13.4.2	yam indram āhur varuṇaṃ yam āhur yaṃ mitram āhur yam u satyam āhuḥ / yo devānāṃ devatamas tapojās tasmā indrāya sutam ājuhomi svāheti vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti / svāhā vaḍ indrāyety anuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā harati bhakṣam
13.4.3	taṃ bhakṣayanti ye pravargyam
13.4.4	tasyāraṇye 'nuvākyo bhakṣamantraḥ
13.4.5	nāpravargye syād ity aparam
13.4.6	mitro janān pra sa mitreti bhakṣayitvā nābhideśān abhimṛśante
13.4.7	vyākhyātā savanīyacaryā
13.4.8	etāvan nānā / mādhyaṃdinasya savanasyendrāya puroḍāśānām iti saṃpraiṣādī namati
13.4.9	hotra iḍāṃ hṛtvā havirdhānaṃ gacchan saṃpreṣyaty unnīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhīti
13.4.10	unnayanādy ā nārāśaṃsānāṃ sādanāt
13.4.11	tatra vikāraḥ
13.4.12	acchāvākacamasaṃ daśamam unnayati
13.4.13	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati
13.4.14	mādhyaṃdinasya savanasya niṣkevalyasya bhāgasya śukravato manthivato madhuścuta indrāya somān iti saṃpraiṣādiḥ
13.4.15	ṣaḍḍhotrā bhavanti

13.4.17	etā eva hotrās tṛtīyasavane bhavanti
13.5.1	sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu dakṣiṇā dadāti / bahv aparimitaṃ saptaikaviṃśatiḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ śataṃ dvādaśaśataṃ sahasraṃ sarvavedasaṃ vā
13.5.2	jyeṣṭhaṃ vā putram apabhajya sarvavedasaṃ dadāti
13.5.3	aśvataraṃ sāhasre sarvavedase ca dadāti
13.5.4	aviṃ dadāty ajāṃ gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ hastinaṃ vāso 'no ratham odanaṃ manthaṃ māṣāṃs tilān vrīhiyavān gardabham ity adhikāny aniyatāni
13.5.5	gavāṃ saṃkhyā bhavati
13.5.6	dakṣiṇena vedim avasthitāsu dakṣiṇāsūttareṇa havirdhānaṃ gatvottareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ parītya pūrvayā dvārā prāgvaṃśaṃ praviśyātra yajamānasyāmātyānāṃ saṃhvayanādy ā srugdaṇḍopaniyamanāt kṛtvā pracarṇyā dakṣiṇāni juhoti
13.5.7	hiraṇyaṃ prabadhya ghṛte 'vadhāyod u tyaṃ citram iti dvābhyāṃ gārhapatye juhoti
13.5.8	divaṃ gaccha suvaḥ pateti hiraṇyaṃ hutvodgṛhṇāti
13.5.9	ubhayaṃ dhārayamāṇo rūpeṇa vo rūpam abhyaimīti dakṣiṇā abhyaiti
13.5.10	atinīya vibhāgam eke samāmananti
13.5.11	tutho vo viśvavedā vibhajatv iti tā yajamānaś caturdhā kṛṣṇājinena vyuttrāsya caturtham adhvaryubhyo vibhajati
13.5.12	yāvad adhvaryave dadāti tasyārdhaṃ pratiprasthātre tṛtīyaṃ neṣṭre caturtham unnetre
13.5.13	etenetareṣāṃ dānam uktam
13.6.1	hiraṇyaṃ pūrṇapātram upabarhaṇaṃ sārvasūtram ity agnīdhe 'gre dadāti
13.6.2	pratihartre 'ntataḥ
13.6.3	tathā brahmaṇe dadyād yathānyāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ nānudhyāyet
13.6.4	aṅgāni dattvā tenatena yathāliṅgaṃ niṣkrīṇīte yad dāsyan syāt
13.6.5	hotar vācaṃ te dadāmi tāṃ te 'nena niṣkrīṇāmīti
13.6.6	evaṃ brahmaṇe manaḥ / adhvaryave prāṇaṃ / udgātre cakṣuḥ / hotrakebhyaḥ śrotram / camasādhvaryubhyo 'ṅgāni / prasarpakebhyo lomāni / sadasyāyātmānam
13.6.7	anyatra dakṣiṇābhyaś camasādhvaryuprasarpakasadasyebhyaḥ
13.6.8	hiraṇyapāṇir agreṇa gārhapatyaṃ nayati jaghanena sadaḥ / antarāgnīdhraṃ ca sadaś ca tā udīcīs tīryenotsṛjati
13.6.9	etat te agne rādha iti dakṣiṇātinayanaḥ
13.6.10	tathaiva samanvārabdheṣv asamanvārabdheṣu vāgne nayety āgnīdhrīye juhoti
13.6.11	vaneṣu vy antarikṣaṃ tatāneti dvitīyāṃ yady ano ratho vāso 'dhīvāso vā dīyate yadi vā dāsyan syāt / prajāpate na tvad etānīti tṛtīyāṃ yadi puruṣo hastī vā dīyate yadi vā dāsyan syāt
13.6.12	brāhmaṇam adya rādhyāsam ity ātreyāya prathamāya hiraṇyaṃ dadāti / dvitīyāya tṛtīyāya vā
13.6.13	tadabhāve ya ārṣeyaḥ saṃhitas tasmai dadyāt
13.6.14	asmaddātrā devatrā gacchateti nītā anumantrya sada etya vi suvaḥ paśyety anuvīkṣate yady atinīya vibhajet
13.6.15	antaḥ sadasyāsīnebhya ṛtvigbhyo dadyāt / havirdhāne 'dhvaryubhyaḥ
13.6.16	ṛtvigbhyo namaskaroti
13.6.17	yaṃ yajñam āgacchet taṃ prasarped iti prasarpakāṇāṃ vijñāyate
13.7.1	dakṣiṇataḥ sadasyāsīnebhyaḥ prasarpakebhyo dadāti
13.7.2	na bahirvedi
13.7.3	na yācitaḥ
13.7.4	na bhītaḥ
13.7.5	na kaṇvakaśyapebhyaḥ
13.7.6	nābrāhmaṇāya
13.7.7	brāhmaṇāyāpy aviduṣe na deyam / apy abrāhmaṇāya vidyāvide dadyāt / yāṃ sa vidyāṃ veda tāṃ tayāvarunddhe
13.7.8	yāṃ śrotriyāya jñātaye vānṛtvije prasṛptāya yāṃ sa vidyāṃ veda tāṃ tayāvarunddhe
13.7.9	yāṃ jyeṣṭhāya yayā sa devatayā jyaiṣṭhyaṃ gacchati tāṃ tayāvarunddhe
13.7.10	yām ārṣeyāya viduṣe svargaṃ tayā lokam āpnoti
13.7.11	yām anyo dīyamānāṃ na kāmayeta yaṃ dviṣyāt tasmai dadyāt sahānyena dhanena
13.7.12	yat pratinuttāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ goṣu cārayet prati vā gṛhṇīyāt salāvṛkyenaṃ bhūtvā pravlinīyāt
13.7.13	yām adānīyāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti tām asya paśavo 'nvapakrāmanti / yadi manyetādānīyāyādām iti na ma idam upadambhiṣag ity etad yajur japed gāṃ vā dadyād brāhmaṇāya
13.7.14	yadā marutvate 'nūktam atha na deyaṃ na pratigṛhyam
13.7.15	anūbandhyāvapāyāṃ hutāyāṃ dadyāt prati ca gṛhṇīyuḥ
13.7.16	nītāsu dakṣiṇāsu cātvāle kṛṣṇaviṣāṇāṃ prāsyati hariṇasya raghuṣyato 'dhi śīrṣaṇi bheṣajam / sa kṣetriyaṃ viṣāṇayā viṣūcīnam anīnaśat // anu tvā hariṇo mṛgaḥ paḍbhiś caturbhir akramīt / viṣāṇe viṣyaitaṃ granthiṃ yad asya gulphitaṃ hṛdi mano yad asya gulphitam ity etābhyām
13.7.17	yajñapatim ṛṣaya enasāhur ity āgnīdhrīye pañca vaiśvakarmaṇāni hutvā
13.8.1	marutvatīyābhyāṃ pracarataḥ
13.8.2	indrāya marutvate 'nubrūhīndrāya marutvate preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau sānuvaṣaṭkārāv ananuvaṣaṭkārau vā / anyataro vā sānuvaṣaṭkāraḥ / dvidevatyavat saṃpātau vyavanīyābhakṣitena pātreṇādhvaryus tṛtīyaṃ marutvatīyaṃ gṛhṇāti / marutvāṁ indreti grahaṇasādanau / pratiprasthātā harati bhakṣam / ubhāv adhvaryū pratibhakṣayataḥ
13.8.3	etat pātram ādāyaindrāgnavac chastrapratigaro grahanārāśaṃsāś ca
13.8.4	māhendraṃ śukrapātreṇa gṛhṇāti / mahāṁ indro ya ojaseti grahaṇasādanau
13.8.5	māhendrasya stotram upākaroti
13.8.6	stute vaiśvadevavac chastrapratigaro grahanārāśaṃsāś ca
13.8.7	māhendraṃ tv atigrāhyā anuhūyante
13.8.8	sahaivādhvaryuṇāgneyaṃ pratiprasthātādatte / aindraṃ neṣṭā / sauryam unnetā
13.8.9	agne tejasvinn ity āgneyaṃ pratiprasthātā hutvā tejovid asīty anumantrayate / indraujasvinn ity aindraṃ neṣṭā hutvaujovid asīty anumantrayate / sūrya bhrājasvinn iti sauryam unnetā hutvā suvarvid asīty anumantrayate
13.8.10	tān hutvā sadasi pratyaṅmukhā bhakṣayanti mayi medhām ity etaiḥ svaṃsvaṃ yathāliṅgam
13.8.11	tathaivokthyavigrahāḥ
13.8.12	etāvan nānā / indrāya tvendrāya tveti sarvatra grahaṇasādanau saṃnamati
13.8.13	ukthaṃ vācīty āha mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ pratigīrya śastraṃśastraṃ vā / viśve devā maruta iti saṃsthite savana āhutiṃ juhoti
13.8.14	tathaiva saṃpraiṣaḥ sarpaṇaṃ ca
13.8.15	saṃtiṣṭhate mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanam
13.9.1	ādityārambhaṇaṃ tṛtīyasavanam
13.9.2	havirdhānasyobhe dvārau saṃvṛtya vedyāṃ bahujanāyām
13.9.3	yadi vāsya bhrātṛvyaḥ prasṛptaḥ syād antarvedi sati gṛhṇīyāt
13.9.4	bhrātṛvyayajñe tu gṛhyamāṇa āditye bahirvedi tiṣṭhet
13.9.5	ādityapātreṇa ya ādityasthālyāṃ dvidevatyagrahasaṃpātās tebhyaḥ somaṃ gṛhṇāti kadācana starīr asīti
13.9.6	kadācana prayucchasīti śṛtātaṅkyaṃ dadhi
13.9.7	yajño devānām iti punaḥ somaṃ gṛhītvā vivasva ādityeti tasmin grāvāṇam upāṃśusavanam avadhāya tenainaṃ mekṣayitvā
13.9.8	yā divyā vṛṣṭis tayā tvā śrīṇāmīti śṛtātaṅkyena dadhnā payasā vā vṛṣṭikāmasya śrītvā grāvāṇam udgṛhṇāti
13.9.9	yady udgṛhītasya tājag binduḥ praskanded varṣukaḥ parjanyaḥ syāt / yadi ciram avarṣukaḥ
13.9.10	na sādayati
13.9.11	yadi kāmayeta garbhān paśavaḥ sīvyeyur ity udgṛhyādityam avekṣeta
13.9.12	darbhair hastena vāpidhāyottiṣṭhati sūryo mā devo devebhyaḥ pātv iti
13.9.13	ahaṃ parastād ity ādityaṃ yajamāno 'nvārabhata ā homāt
13.9.14	kavir yajñasya vitanoti panthām iti harati
13.9.15	ā samudrād iti darbhair ācyāvayati
13.10.1	ādityebhyo 'nubrūhi priyebhyaḥ priyadhāmabhyaḥ priyavratebhyo mahasvasarasya patibhya uror antarikṣasyādhyakṣebhya ādityebhyaḥ preṣya priyebhyaḥ priyadhāmabhyaḥ priyavratebhyo mahasvasarasya patibhya uror antarikṣasyādhyakṣebhya iti saṃpraiṣau / ādityebhyo 'nubrūhy ādityebhyaḥ preṣyeti vā
13.10.2	yās te viśvāḥ samidhaḥ santy agna iti darbhān āhavanīye prāsyānyatrekṣamāṇa ādityaṃ juhoti
13.10.3	unnambhaya pṛthivīm iti vṛṣṭikāmasya juhuyāt
13.10.4	na hutvānvīkṣeta
13.10.5	sūdavad ādityapātram āyatane sādayitvādābhyāṃśum upāṃśupāvanau yaś copāṃśupātre 'ṃśus tān ṛjīṣe 'pisṛjya prātaḥsavanavan mahābhiṣavaḥ
13.10.6	ṛjīṣaṃ tv evābhiṣuṇvanti
13.10.7	payasyāvarjaṃ savanīyāḥ
13.10.8	āgnīdhre patnyāśiraṃ mathitvāparayā dvārā havirdhānaṃ prapādayati / pūrvayā gataśriyaḥ
13.10.9	pūrvayā yajamānaḥ prapadyate
13.10.10	pūtabhṛto bila udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitraṃ vitatya tasmin yajamānaḥ purastāt pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan saha patnyāśiram avanayaty asme devāso vapuṣe cikitsateti catasṛbhiḥ
13.10.11	grahakāla āgrayaṇam eva catasṛbhyo dhārābhyaḥ
13.10.12	āgrayaṇād utsicya dvitīyāṃ dhārāṃ karoti / ādityasthālyās tṛtīyām / ādityagrahasaṃpātāc caturthīm
13.10.13	ukthyaś ced atrokthyaṃ gṛhṇāti
13.10.14	viramati dhāraikadhanānāṃ yathārtham ity etadādi mādhyaṃdinavat
13.11.1	jāgataḥ panthā ādityā devatāvṛkeṇāparipareṇa pathā svasty ādityān aśīyeti sarpaṇe vikāraḥ / āyuṣe hiṅkuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai stuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti purastād ārbhavāt pavamānād yajamāno japati / pañcahotāraṃ saptahotāraṃ vā vyācaṣṭe / āyuvai hiṅkuru tasyai prastuhi tasyai stuhi tasyai me 'varuddhyā iti ca / stūyamāne ca pañcahotāraṃ saptahotāraṃ vā japati / madhyamāyāṃ ca stotrīyāyāṃ tṛtīyam anvāroham / stute 'dhvaryuḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnīd agnīn vihara barhi stṛṇīti puroḍāśāṁ alaṃkuru pratiprasthātaḥ paśau saṃvadasveti
13.11.2	atra śalākābhijvalato dhiṣṇiyān vihṛtān na vyāghārayet / upariṣṭād vyāghāraṇam

13.12.1	pracaraṇakāle hotṛcamasam adhvaryur ādatte / camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ
13.12.2	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati / tṛtīyasya savanasyarbhumato vibhumataḥ prabhumato vājavataḥ savitṛvato bṛhaspativato viśvadevyāvatas tīvrāṁ āśīrvata indrāya somān iti saṃpraiṣādiḥ
13.12.3	atha camasāñ juhoti
13.12.4	śyenāya patvane svāheti vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti / vaṭ svayam abhigūrtāya namaḥ svāhety anuvaṣaṭkṛte
13.12.5	hutvā harati bhakṣam
13.12.6	evam uttaraiḥ pracarati
13.12.7	etāvan nānā / pūrveṇapūrveṇa mantreṇa vaṣaṭkṛtevaṣaṭkṛte juhoti / uttareṇottareṇānuvaṣaṭkṛte
13.12.8	tṛmpantāṃ hotrā iti sarvān hutvā japati
13.12.9	sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu camasinaḥ svaṃsvaṃ camasam anū nyante trīṃstrīn puroḍāśaśakalān upavapanta etat te tatāsau ye ca tvām anv ity etaiḥ pratimantram
13.12.10	namo vaḥ pitaro rasāyeti namaskārāñ japanti

13.13.1	vāmam adya savitar ity antaryāmapātreṇa sāvitram āgrayaṇād gṛhītvā na sādayati
13.13.2	devāya savitre 'nubrūhi devāya savitre preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau
13.13.3	nānuvaṣaṭkaroti
13.13.4	etenaiva saśeṣeṇa vaiśvadevaṃ pūtabhṛto gṛhṇāti

13.13.7	vaiśvadevaṃ pratigṛṇāti

13.14.1	udgātṛbhyo haranti

13.14.5	atra punaḥ śalākābhijvalato dhiṣṇiyān vihṛtān ājyenaivāṣṭagṛhītena vyāghārayati

13.14.7	upayāmagṛhīto 'si bṛhaspatisutasya ta ity upāṃśupātreṇa pātnīvatam āgrayaṇād gṛhītvā na sādayati
13.14.8	vyāghāraṇaśeṣeṇa śrītvāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyaty agnīt pātnīvatasya yajeti / agnā3i patnīvā3 iti vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti
13.14.9	nānuvaṣaṭkaroti
13.14.10	api vopāṃśv anuvaṣaṭkuryāt
13.14.11	tataḥ saṃpreṣyaty agnīn neṣṭur upastham āsīda neṣṭaḥ patnīm udānayonnetar hotuś camasam anūnnaya hotṛcamase dhruvāyāvakāśaṃ kurūdgātrā patnīṃ saṃkhyāpayāpa upapravartayeti
13.14.12	saṃpraiṣavat kurvanti
13.14.13	antarā neṣṭāraṃ dhiṣṇiyaṃ cāgnīdhro vyavasṛpya bhakṣayati
13.14.14	agnipītasyeti bhakṣamantraṃ saṃnamati
13.15.1	nopastha āsīta / yad upastha āsīta paṇḍakaḥ syāt
13.15.2	hotṛcamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnayan sarvaṃ rājānam unnīya daśābhiḥ kalaśau mṛṣṭvā nyubjati
13.15.3	yajñāyajñiyasya stotram upākaroti
13.15.4	jvalayanti dhiṣṇiyān
13.15.5	sakarṇaprāvṛtā avakarṇaprāvṛtā vā yajñāyajñiyena stuvate
13.15.6	ye prasṛptāḥ syus te sarve 'gniṣṭomam upagāyeyuḥ
13.15.7	saptahotāraṃ yajamāno vyācaṣṭe
13.15.8	viśvasya te viśvāvata iti hiṅkāram anūdgātrā patnīṃ saṃkhyāpayati / ā tisṛbhyaḥ stotriyābhyo 'gan devān iti ca
13.15.9	patny apa upapravartayati dakṣinenorunā nagnena prācīr updīcīr vorubhyām anatarataḥ

13.16.1	bhūtam asi bhūte mā dhā iti pratiprasthātā dhruvam avekṣya dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ tvā parigṛhṇāmīty añjalinā parigṛhya viśve tvā devā vaiśvānarāḥ pracyāvayantv iti hṛtvā dhruvaṃ dhruveṇeti purastāt pratyaṅṅ āsīno hotṛcamase dhruvam avanayati
13.16.2	purastād ukthyasyāvanīyaḥ / madhyato 'ntato vā
13.16.3	uta no 'hir budhnyaḥ śṛṇotv aja ekapād iti vā vaiśvadevyām ṛci śasyamānāyām
13.16.4	paridhānīyāyāṃ vā sakṛcchāstāyām
13.16.5	madhyamāyām uttamāyāṃ vā
13.16.6	ukthaṃ vācīndrāyety āha tṛtīyasavanaṃ pratigīrya / śastraṃśastraṃ vā
13.16.7	pracaraṇakāle hotṛcamasam adhvaryur ādatte / camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ / āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyaty ukthaśā yaja somānām iti / vaṣaṭkṛtānuvaṣaṭkṛte juhvati / bhakṣān haranti
13.16.8	hotṛcamasam adhvaryuḥ pratibhakṣayati subhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmīnāṃ priyo devānāṃ saṃsadanīyaḥ / taṃ tvā subhava devā abhisaṃviśan tviṣo 'si tveṣo 'si nṛmṇo 'si yahvo 'si vrato 'si svo 'si vāraṇo 'si tasya ta iṣasya tveṣasya nṛmṇasya yahvasya vratasya svasya vāraṇasya śūdrasya cāryasya ca bhukṣiṣīyeti
13.16.9	yathā tvaṃ sūryāsi viśvadarśata evam ahaṃ viśvadarśato bhūyāsam ity ādityaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
13.16.10	āyur ma indriyaṃ dhehy ado ma āgacchatv ity āhavanīyam
13.16.11	yat kāmayate tasya nāma gṛhṇāti

13.17.1	paridhiṣu prahṛteṣūnnetā hāriyojanaṃ gṛhṇāti
13.17.2	upayāmagṛhīto 'si harir asīti droṇakalaśena sarvam āgrayaṇaṃ gṛhītvā na sādayati / bahvībhir dhānābhiḥ śrītvā śīrṣann adhinidhāyopaniṣkramyendrāya harivate 'nubrūhīndrāya harivate preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau / dhānāsomebhyo 'nubrūhi dhānāsomān prasthitān preṣyeti vā

13.17.9	devakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi manuṣyakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi pitṛkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asy ātmakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asy anyakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asy enasaenaso 'vayajanam asīty āhavanīye śakalān abhyādhāyaikadhanapariśeṣeṣu hariṇīr dūrvāḥ prāsya saṃplomnāya tīvrīkṛtya yathācamasaṃ vyānīyāpareṇa cātvālam āstāve vā pratyañcaś camasinaḥ svaṃsvaṃ camasarasam avaghreṇa bhakṣayanty apsu dhautasya soma deva iti
13.18.1	samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomi svāṃ yonim apigacchata / ariṣṭā asmākaṃ vīrāḥ santu mā parāseci naḥ svam // acchāyaṃ vo marutaḥ śloka etv acchā viṣṇuṃ niṣiktapām avobhiḥ / uta prajāyai gṛṇate vayo dhur yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā na ity antarvedi śeṣān ninīya dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam ity āgnīdhre dadhidrapsān bhakṣayanti
13.18.2	ubhā kavī yuvānā satyā tā dharmaṇaspatī / satyasya dharmaṇaspate vi sakhyāni sṛjāmaha iti tānūnaptriṇaḥ sakhyāni visṛjante
13.18.3	paśuvat patnīsaṃyājāḥ

13.18.8	agninā devena pṛtanā jayāmīti yajamāno jāgatān viṣṇukramān krāmati
13.18.9	sarvebhir devebhiḥ pṛtanā jayāmy ānuṣṭubhena chandasaikaviṃśena stomena vairājena sāmnā vaṣaṭkāreṇa vajreṇa sarvajān bhrātṛvyān adharān pādayāmy avainān bādhe praty enān nude 'smin kṣaye 'smin bhūmiloke yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo viṣṇoḥ krameṇāty enān krāmāmīti caturtham eke samāmananti

13.21.1	devīr āpa ity avabhṛthaṃ yajamāno 'bhimantrya sumitrā na āpa oṣadhaya ity apaḥ pragāhya saśiraskāv anupamakṣantau snātaḥ patnī yajamānaś ca
13.21.2	anyo'nyasya pṛṣṭhe pradhāvataḥ
13.21.3	yad didīkṣe manasā yac ca vācā yad vā prāṇaiś cakṣuṣā yac ca śrotreṇa / yad retasā mithunenāpy ātmanādbhyo lokā dadhire teja indriyam / śukrā dīkṣāyai tapaso vimocanīr āpo vimoktrīr mayi teja indriyam // yad ṛcā sāmnā yajuṣā paśūnāṃ carman haviṣā didīkṣe / yac chandobhir oṣadhībhir vanaspatāv adbhyo lokā dadhire teja indriyam / śukrā dīkṣāyai tapaso vimocanīr āpo vimoktrīr mayi teja indriyam // yena brahma yena kṣatraṃ yenendrāgnī prajāpatiḥ somo varuṇo yena rājā / viśve devā ṛṣayo yena prāṇā adbhyo lokā dadhire teja indriyam / śukrā dīkṣāyai tapaso vimocanīr āpo vimoktrīr mayi teja indriyam iti trir añjalinā viṣicyonnetar vasīyo na unnayābhi / ud it te vasuvittamā giraḥ stomāsa īrate / satrājito dhanasā akṣitotayo vājayanto rathā iva / kaṇvā iva bhṛgavaḥ sūryā iva viśvam iddhītam ānaśur iti yajamānaḥ saṃpreṣyati
13.22.1	udeta prajām āyur varco dadhānā adha syām asur ubhayor gṛheṣu / gāyatrīṃ chandāṃsy anusaṃrabhantām asmān rāya uta yajñāḥ sacantām / suprītaḥ suvar apa āviveśety unnetonnayati
